   1 | # Alianza Residencial — Instrucciones de instalación de escritorio
   2 | 
   3 | ## ¿Qué se entrega en este paquete?
   4 | 
   5 | | Archivo | Acción |
   6 | |---------|--------|
   7 | | `launcher.py` | **Reemplaza** `Run.py` como punto de entrada principal |
   8 | | `main.js` | **Reemplaza** `app/static/js/main.js` |
   9 | | `app_main.py` | **Reemplaza** `app/main.py` (renombrar a `main.py`) |
  10 | | `auth_service.py` | **Reemplaza** `app/services/auth_service.py` |
  11 | | `build.bat` | Nuevo — genera el `.exe` instalable |
  12 | 
  13 | ---
  14 | 
  15 | ## Paso 1 — Copiar archivos
  16 | 
  17 | ```
  18 | launcher.py          →  C:\alianza_backend\launcher.py
  19 | main.js              →  C:\alianza_backend\app\static\js\main.js
  20 | app_main.py          →  C:\alianza_backend\app\main.py   (renombrar)
  21 | auth_service.py      →  C:\alianza_backend\app\services\auth_service.py
  22 | build.bat            →  C:\alianza_backend\build.bat
  23 | ```
  24 | 
  25 | ---
  26 | 
  27 | ## Paso 2 — Probar localmente
  28 | 
  29 | ```bash
  30 | cd C:\alianza_backend
  31 | python launcher.py
  32 | ```
  33 | 
  34 | Verás una ventana con:
  35 | - Indicador LED rojo/verde del servidor
  36 | - Log de actividad en tiempo real
  37 | - Botón **Iniciar Sistema** → arranca FastAPI + abre el navegador
  38 | - Botón **Abrir navegador** → abre `http://localhost:8000`
  39 | - Botón **Detener** → para el servidor limpiamente
  40 | 
  41 | Al iniciar, el sistema:
  42 | 1. Verifica dependencias (`pip install -r requirements.txt`)
  43 | 2. Crea las carpetas `database/`, `logs/`, `invoices/`
  44 | 3. Arranca uvicorn en el puerto 8000
  45 | 4. Espera que el servidor responda
  46 | 5. Abre el navegador automáticamente en el login
  47 | 
  48 | ---
  49 | 
  50 | ## Paso 3 — Qué cambió en el código
  51 | 
  52 | ### `main.js` (frontend)
  53 | - Añadido objeto `Auth` — guarda/lee el token JWT en localStorage
  54 | - `apiRequest()` ahora envía `Authorization: Bearer <token>` en cada petición
  55 | - Si el servidor responde 401, limpia la sesión y redirige al login
  56 | - `renderHeader()` muestra el nombre del usuario y botón de logout
  57 | - Nueva función `logout()` — limpia localStorage y va al login
  58 | 
  59 | ### `app/main.py`
  60 | - Al arrancar, llama `create_default_admin()` — crea usuario admin si no existe
  61 | - Las rutas de API están bajo `/api` (coincide con el frontend)
  62 | 
  63 | ### `app/services/auth_service.py`
  64 | - Nueva función `create_default_admin(db)` — crea admin desde variables del `.env`
  65 | 
  66 | ---
  67 | 
  68 | ## Paso 4 — Generar el .exe (opcional, para distribuir)
  69 | 
  70 | Instalar PyInstaller:
  71 | ```bash
  72 | pip install pyinstaller
  73 | ```
  74 | 
  75 | Ejecutar el build:
  76 | ```
  77 | Doble clic en build.bat
  78 | ```
  79 | 
  80 | El resultado estará en:
  81 | ```
  82 | dist\AlianzaResidencial\AlianzaResidencial.exe
  83 | ```
  84 | 
  85 | Para distribuir al cliente: comprimir toda la carpeta `dist\AlianzaResidencial\` en un ZIP.
  86 | 
  87 | > **Nota:** El `.exe` incluye Python y todas las dependencias. El cliente solo necesita
  88 | > hacer doble clic — no necesita instalar Python.
  89 | 
  90 | ---
  91 | 
  92 | ## Credenciales por defecto
  93 | 
  94 | - **Usuario:** admin  
  95 | - **Contraseña:** Admin123
  96 | 
  97 | Se pueden cambiar en el archivo `.env`:
  98 | ```
  99 | DEFAULT_ADMIN_USER=admin
 100 | DEFAULT_ADMIN_PASS=Admin123
 101 | ```
 102 | 
 103 | ---
 104 | 
 105 | ## Próximos pasos sugeridos
 106 | 
 107 | 1. Generar el `.exe` y probarlo en una PC limpia (sin Python instalado)
 108 | 2. Crear un ícono `assets/icon.ico` para personalizar el launcher
 109 | 3. Agregar un instalador con Inno Setup (crea el típico "siguiente → siguiente → instalar")
 110 | 4. Cuando estés listo para agregar más funciones, continuar con el desarrollo normal

  33 | 
  34 | def port_free(port: int) -> bool:
  35 |     with socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM) as s:
  36 |         return s.connect_ex(("localhost", port)) != 0
  37 | 
  38 | 
  39 | def wait_server(port: int, timeout=30) -> bool:
  40 |     t = time.time()
  41 |     while time.time() - t < timeout:
  42 |         if not port_free(port):
  43 |             return True
  44 |         time.sleep(0.4)
  45 |     return False
  46 | 
  47 | 
  48 | def get_python() -> str:
  49 |     for p in [Path("venv/Scripts/python.exe"), Path("venv/bin/python")]:
  50 |         if p.exists():
  51 |             return str(p)
  52 |     return sys.executable
  53 |

 178 |     # ── Logging ──────────────────────────────
 179 |     def _log(self, msg: str, level="info"):
 180 |         ts  = time.strftime("%H:%M:%S")
 181 |         sym = {"ok": "✓", "err": "✕", "warn": "⚠"}.get(level, "·")
 182 |         self.log.configure(state="normal")
 183 |         self.log.insert("end", f"[{ts}] {sym} {msg}\n", level if level != "info" else "")
 184 |         self.log.see("end")
 185 |         self.log.configure(state="disabled")
 186 | 
 187 |     # ── Estado UI ────────────────────────────
 188 |     def _set_running(self, on: bool):
 189 |         if on:
 190 |             self.led_cv.itemconfig(self.led, fill=C_SUCCESS)
 191 |             self.lbl_status.config(text="Activo", fg=C_SUCCESS)
 192 |             self.lbl_url.config(text=f"↗  {APP_URL}   (clic para abrir)")
 193 |             self.btn_start.config(state="disabled", bg="#94a3b8", text="▶   Activo")
 194 |             self.btn_open.config(state="normal")
 195 |             self.btn_stop.config(state="normal")
 196 |         else:
 197 |             self.led_cv.itemconfig(self.led, fill=C_DANGER)
 198 |             self.lbl_status.config(text="Detenido", fg=C_DANGER)
 199 |             self.lbl_url.config(text="")
 200 |             self.btn_start.config(state="normal", bg=C_DARK, text="▶   Iniciar Sistema")
 201 |             self.btn_open.config(state="disabled")
 202 |             self.btn_stop.config(state="disabled")
 203 | 
 204 |     # ── Control servidor ─────────────────────
 205 |     def _start(self):
 206 |         if not port_free(PORT):
 207 |             self._log(f"Puerto {PORT} ya en uso — conectando", "warn")
 208 |             self._set_running(True)
 209 |             self._open()
 210 |             return
 211 |         self.btn_start.config(state="disabled", text="⏳  Iniciando...", bg="#94a3b8")
 212 |         self.running = True
 213 |         threading.Thread(target=self._run_server, daemon=True).start()
 214 | 
 215 |     def _run_server(self):
 216 |         py = get_python()
 217 |         self._log(f"Python: {py}")
 218 | 
 219 |         for d in ["database", "logs", "invoices", "supplier_docs"]:
 220 |             os.makedirs(d, exist_ok=True)
 221 | 
 222 |         if Path("requirements.txt").exists():
 223 |             self._log("Verificando dependencias...")
 224 |             try:
 225 |                 subprocess.run([py, "-m", "pip", "install", "-r", "requirements.txt", "-q"],
 226 |                                capture_output=True, timeout=180)
 227 |                 self._log("Dependencias OK", "ok")
 228 |             except Exception as e:
 229 |                 self._log(f"pip: {e}", "warn")
 230 | 
 231 |         self._log(f"Iniciando servidor en :{PORT}...")
 232 |         try:
 233 |             flags = subprocess.CREATE_NO_WINDOW if sys.platform == "win32" else 0
 234 |             self.proc = subprocess.Popen(
 235 |                 [py, "-m", "uvicorn", "app.main:app",
 236 |                  "--host", "0.0.0.0", "--port", str(PORT), "--log-level", "warning"],
 237 |                 stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT,
 238 |                 text=True, creationflags=flags)
 239 |         except Exception as e:
 240 |             self._log(f"Error al iniciar: {e}", "err")
 241 |             self.root.after(0, lambda: self._set_running(False))
 242 |             return
 243 | 
 244 |         if wait_server(PORT, 30):
 245 |             self._log(f"Servidor activo — {APP_URL}", "ok")
 246 |             self.root.after(0, lambda: self._set_running(True))
 247 |             self.root.after(800, self._open)
 248 |         else:
 249 |             self._log("El servidor no respondió a tiempo", "err")
 250 |             self.root.after(0, lambda: self._set_running(False))
 251 |             self.root.after(0, lambda: self.btn_start.config(
 252 |                 state="normal", bg=C_DARK, text="▶   Iniciar Sistema"))
 253 | 
 254 |         if self.proc:
 255 |             for line in self.proc.stdout:
 256 |                 l = line.strip()
 257 |                 if l: self._log(l)
 258 | 
 259 |     def _stop(self):
 260 |         if self.proc:
 261 |             self._log("Deteniendo servidor...")
 262 |             try:
 263 |                 self.proc.terminate()
 264 |                 self.proc.wait(timeout=5)
 265 |             except Exception:
 266 |                 try: self.proc.kill()
 267 |                 except: pass
 268 |             self.proc = None
 269 |         self.running = False
 270 |         self._set_running(False)
 271 |         self._log("Servidor detenido", "ok")
 272 | 
 273 |     def _open(self):
 274 |         if not port_free(PORT):
 275 |             webbrowser.open(APP_URL)
 276 |         else:
 277 |             self._log("El servidor no está activo aún", "warn")
 278 | 
 279 |     def _close(self):
 280 |         if self.running and self.proc:
 281 |             if messagebox.askyesno("Cerrar",
 282 |                     "El servidor está activo.\n¿Deseas detenerlo y cerrar?",
 283 |                     icon="warning"):
 284 |                 self._stop()
 285 |                 self.root.destroy()
 286 |         else:
 287 |             self.root.destroy()
 288 | 
 289 |     def run(self):
 290 |         self.root.mainloop()
 291 | 
 292 | 
 293 | if __name__ == "__main__":
 294 |     os.chdir(Path(__file__).parent.resolve())
 295 |     Launcher().run()
 296 |

   1 | from sqlalchemy import create_engine
   2 | from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker, declarative_base
   3 | from app.config import settings
   4 | 
   5 | engine = create_engine(
   6 |     settings.DATABASE_URL,
   7 |     pool_pre_ping=True
   8 | )
   9 | 
  10 | SessionLocal = sessionmaker(
  11 |     autocommit=False,
  12 |     autoflush=False,
  13 |     bind=engine
  14 | )
  15 | 
  16 | Base = declarative_base()
  17 | 
  18 | 
  19 | def get_db():
  20 |     db = SessionLocal()
  21 |     try:
  22 |         yield db
  23 |     finally:
  24 |         db.close()

================================================================================
ARCHIVO: app\main.py
TIPO: PY
RUTA COMPLETA: C:\alianza_backend\app\main.py
================================================================================

   1 | """
   2 | app/main.py — Aplicación principal FastAPI
   3 | Versión Railway: maneja proxy HTTPS y crea admin por defecto
   4 | """
   5 | 
   6 | from fastapi import FastAPI, Request
   7 | from fastapi.responses import FileResponse, RedirectResponse
   8 | from fastapi.staticfiles import StaticFiles
   9 | from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
  10 | from fastapi.middleware.httpsredirect import HTTPSRedirectMiddleware
  11 | import os
  12 | 
  13 | from app.database import engine, Base, SessionLocal
  14 | from app.routers import property, unit, owner, unit_owner, finance, charges, auth
  15 | from app.routers import suppliers, agenda
  16 | from app.routers import garita
  17 | 
  18 | # ── Crear tablas ─────────────────────────────
  19 | Base.metadata.create_all(bind=engine)
  20 | 
  21 | 
  22 | # ── Crear usuario admin por defecto ──────────
  23 | def _seed_admin():
  24 |     from app.services.auth_service import create_default_admin
  25 |     db = SessionLocal()
  26 |     try:
  27 |         create_default_admin(db)
  28 |     finally:
  29 |         db.close()
  30 | 
  31 | _seed_admin()
  32 | 
  33 | 
  34 | # ── Crear carpetas necesarias ─────────────────
  35 | for folder in ["database", "logs", "invoices", "supplier_docs"]:
  36 |     os.makedirs(folder, exist_ok=True)
  37 | 
  38 | 
  39 | # ── App principal ────────────────────────────
  40 | app = FastAPI(title="Alianza Residencial", version="1.0.0")
  41 | 
  42 | # ── Middleware para proxy HTTPS (Railway) ─────
  43 | # Railway termina SSL en el proxy y reenvía como HTTP internamente.
  44 | # Este middleware lee los headers del proxy para que FastAPI
  45 | # sepa que está detrás de HTTPS y no genere URLs con http://.
  46 | from starlette.middleware.trustedhost import TrustedHostMiddleware
  47 | 
  48 | @app.middleware("http")
  49 | async def https_redirect_middleware(request: Request, call_next):
  50 |     # Si viene del proxy de Railway, marcar como HTTPS
  51 |     if request.headers.get("x-forwarded-proto") == "https":
  52 |         request.scope["scheme"] = "https"
  53 |     response = await call_next(request)
  54 |     return response
  55 | 
  56 | app.add_middleware(
  57 |     CORSMiddleware,
  58 |     allow_origins=["*"],
  59 |     allow_credentials=True,
  60 |     allow_methods=["*"],
  61 |     allow_headers=["*"],
  62 | )
  63 | 
  64 | # ── Sub-app de API bajo /api ──────────────────
  65 | api_app = FastAPI(title="Alianza API")
  66 | 
  67 | api_app.include_router(property.router)
  68 | api_app.include_router(unit.router)
  69 | api_app.include_router(owner.router)
  70 | api_app.include_router(unit_owner.router)
  71 | api_app.include_router(finance.router)
  72 | api_app.include_router(charges.router)

  74 | api_app.include_router(suppliers.router)
  75 | api_app.include_router(agenda.router)

  77 | 
  78 | app.mount("/api", api_app)
  79 | 
  80 | # ── Archivos estáticos ────────────────────────

================================================================================
ARCHIVO: app\middleware\auth_middleware.py
TIPO: PY
RUTA COMPLETA: C:\alianza_backend\app\middleware\auth_middleware.py
================================================================================

   1 | from fastapi import Request, HTTPException
   2 | from fastapi.security import HTTPBearer, HTTPAuthorizationCredentials
   3 | from jose import jwt, JWTError
   4 | from starlette.middleware.base import BaseHTTPMiddleware
   5 | from starlette.responses import RedirectResponse
   6 | import re
   7 | 
   8 | from app.config import settings
   9 | 
  10 | security = HTTPBearer(auto_error=False)
  11 | 
  12 | class AuthMiddleware(BaseHTTPMiddleware):
  13 |     async def dispatch(self, request: Request, call_next):
  14 |         # Rutas públicas (no requieren token)
  15 |         public_paths = [
  16 |             r'^/login$',
  17 |             r'^/static/.*',
  18 |             r'^/auth/token$',
  19 |             r'^/auth/login$',
  20 |             r'^/$'
  21 |         ]
  22 |         
  23 |         path = request.url.path
  24 |         
  25 |         # Verificar si es ruta pública
  26 |         for pattern in public_paths:
  27 |             if re.match(pattern, path):
  28 |                 return await call_next(request)
  29 |         
  30 |         # Verificar token
  31 |         token = request.headers.get("Authorization")
  32 |         if not token:
  33 |             # Si no hay token, redirigir al login
  34 |             return RedirectResponse(url="/login")
  35 |         
  36 |         try:
  37 |             token = token.replace("Bearer ", "")
  38 |             payload = jwt.decode(token, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithms=[settings.ALGORITHM])
  39 |             request.state.user = payload
  40 |         except JWTError:
  41 |             return RedirectResponse(url="/login")
  42 |         
  43 |         return await call_next(request)

ARCHIVO: app\reports\pdf_generator.py
TIPO: PY
RUTA COMPLETA: C:\alianza_backend\app\reports\pdf_generator.py
================================================================================

   1 | import os
   2 | from jinja2 import Environment, FileSystemLoader
   3 | 
   4 | 
   5 | def generate_invoice_pdf(data: dict, output_path: str):
   6 |     """
   7 |     Genera un PDF de factura usando Jinja2 + WeasyPrint.
   8 |     ✅ CORREGIDO: reemplaza la implementación con ReportLab que no usaba
   9 |     la plantilla HTML ni pasaba variables dinámicas correctamente.
  10 |     """
  11 | 
  12 |     # Intentar con WeasyPrint (requiere: pip install weasyprint)
  13 |     try:
  14 |         import weasyprint
  15 | 
  16 |         template_dir = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "templates")
  17 |         template_dir = os.path.abspath(template_dir)
  18 | 
  19 |         env = Environment(loader=FileSystemLoader(template_dir))
  20 |         template = env.get_template("invoice_template.html")
  21 | 
  22 |         html_content = template.render(**data)
  23 | 
  24 |         weasyprint.HTML(string=html_content).write_pdf(output_path)
  25 | 
  26 |     except ImportError:
  27 |         # Fallback: si WeasyPrint no está instalado, genera HTML y lo guarda como .html
  28 |         # Útil para desarrollo. En producción instalar: pip install weasyprint
  29 |         template_dir = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "templates")
  30 |         template_dir = os.path.abspath(template_dir)
  31 | 
  32 |         env = Environment(loader=FileSystemLoader(template_dir))
  33 |         template = env.get_template("invoice_template.html")
  34 |         html_content = template.render(**data)
  35 | 
  36 |         html_path = output_path.replace(".pdf", ".html")
  37 |         with open(html_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
  38 |             f.write(html_content)
  39 | 
  40 |         print(f"[AVISO] WeasyPrint no instalado. Factura guardada como HTML: {html_path}")
  41 |         print("Para generar PDFs reales ejecutar: pip install weasyprint")
  42 | 
  43 |     return output_path
  44 |

ARCHIVO: app\routers\agenda.py
TIPO: PY
RUTA COMPLETA: C:\alianza_backend\app\routers\agenda.py
================================================================================

   1 | from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException
   2 | from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
   3 | from pydantic import BaseModel
   4 | from typing import Optional
   5 | from datetime import date
   6 | 
   7 | from app.database import get_db
   8 | from app.models.agenda_event import AgendaEvent
   9 | 
  10 | router = APIRouter(prefix="/agenda", tags=["Agenda"])
  11 | 
  12 | # ── Schema ────────────────────────────────────
  13 | 
  14 | class EventCreate(BaseModel):
  15 |     title:       str
  16 |     description: Optional[str] = None
  17 |     event_type:  str           # CITA | EVENTO | TAREA
  18 |     event_date:  date
  19 |     event_time:  Optional[str] = None
  20 |     location:    Optional[str] = None
  21 |     status:      str = "PENDIENTE"
  22 |     priority:    str = "NORMAL"
  23 | 
  24 | # ── Endpoints ─────────────────────────────────
  25 | 
  26 | @router.get("/")
  27 | def list_events(db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
  28 |     return db.query(AgendaEvent).order_by(
  29 |         AgendaEvent.event_date, AgendaEvent.event_time
  30 |     ).all()
  31 | 
  32 | @router.get("/upcoming")
  33 | def upcoming_events(db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
  34 |     """Próximos eventos desde hoy (para el dashboard)."""
  35 |     from datetime import date as dt
  36 |     return db.query(AgendaEvent).filter(
  37 |         AgendaEvent.event_date >= dt.today(),
  38 |         AgendaEvent.status == "PENDIENTE"
  39 |     ).order_by(AgendaEvent.event_date, AgendaEvent.event_time).limit(10).all()
  40 | 
  41 | @router.post("/")
  42 | def create_event(data: EventCreate, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
  43 |     ev = AgendaEvent(**data.dict())
  44 |     db.add(ev); db.commit(); db.refresh(ev)
  45 |     return ev
  46 | 
  47 | @router.put("/{event_id}")

   1 | from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, status
   2 | from fastapi.security import OAuth2PasswordBearer, OAuth2PasswordRequestForm
   3 | from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
   4 | from datetime import timedelta
   5 | 
   6 | from app.database import get_db
   7 | from app.models.user import User
   8 | from app.services.security import verify_password
   9 | from app.services.auth_service import create_access_token, authenticate_user, get_current_user
  10 | from app.schemas.auth_schema import LoginResponse, UserResponse
  11 | from app.config import settings
  12 | 
  13 | router = APIRouter(prefix="/auth", tags=["Authentication"])
  14 | oauth2_scheme = OAuth2PasswordBearer(tokenUrl="/auth/token")
  15 | 
  16 | # ── Roles válidos del sistema ──────────────────────────────────
  17 | # ADMIN   → acceso total
  18 | # USER    → acceso estándar (registrar pagos, propietarios, etc.)
  19 | # GARITA  → solo puede ver y registrar visitas en el módulo de garita
  20 | VALID_ROLES = ("ADMIN", "USER", "GARITA")
  21 | 
  22 | 
  23 | @router.post("/token", response_model=LoginResponse)
  24 | async def login_for_access_token(
  25 |     form_data: OAuth2PasswordRequestForm = Depends(),
  26 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db)
  27 | ):
  28 |     user = authenticate_user(db, form_data.username, form_data.password)
  29 |     if not user:
  30 |         raise HTTPException(
  31 |             status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
  32 |             detail="Usuario o contraseña incorrectos",
  33 |             headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},
  34 |         )
  35 |     access_token_expires = timedelta(minutes=settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES)
  36 |     access_token = create_access_token(
  37 |         data={"sub": user.username, "role": user.role},
  38 |         expires_delta=access_token_expires
  39 |     )
  40 |     return {
  41 |         "access_token": access_token,
  42 |         "token_type": "bearer",
  43 |         "username": user.username,
  44 |         "role": user.role
  45 |     }
  46 | 
  47 | 
  48 | @router.post("/login", response_model=LoginResponse)
  49 | async def login_json(
  50 |     login_data: dict,
  51 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db)
  52 | ):
  53 |     username = login_data.get("username")
  54 |     password = login_data.get("password")
  55 |     if not username or not password:
  56 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Username y password son requeridos")
  57 |     user = authenticate_user(db, username, password)
  58 |     if not user:
  59 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=401, detail="Usuario o contraseña incorrectos")
  60 |     access_token_expires = timedelta(minutes=settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES)
  61 |     access_token = create_access_token(
  62 |         data={"sub": user.username, "role": user.role},
  63 |         expires_delta=access_token_expires
  64 |     )
  65 |     return {
  66 |         "access_token": access_token,
  67 |         "token_type": "bearer",
  68 |         "username": user.username,
  69 |         "role": user.role
  70 |     }

 102 | # ── Listar todos los usuarios — solo ADMIN ────────────────
 103 | @router.get("/users")
 104 | def list_users(
 105 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_admin),
 106 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 107 | ):
 108 |     users = db.query(User).order_by(User.username).all()
 109 |     return [
 110 |         {
 111 |             "id":        u.id,
 112 |             "username":  u.username,
 113 |             "role":      u.role,
 114 |             "is_active": u.is_active,
 115 |         }
 116 |         for u in users
 117 |     ]
 118 | 
 119 | 
 120 | # ── Crear usuario — solo ADMIN ────────────────────────────
 121 | @router.post("/users")
 122 | def create_user(
 123 |     data: UserCreate,
 124 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_admin),
 125 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 126 | ):
 127 |     from app.services.security import hash_password
 128 | 
 129 |     if data.role not in VALID_ROLES:
 130 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=f"Rol inválido. Usa: {', '.join(VALID_ROLES)}")
 131 | 
 132 |     exists = db.query(User).filter(User.username == data.username).first()
 133 |     if exists:
 134 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="El nombre de usuario ya existe")
 135 | 
 136 |     new_user = User(
 137 |         username      = data.username,
 138 |         password_hash = hash_password(data.password),
 139 |         role          = data.role,
 140 |         is_active     = True,
 141 |     )
 142 |     db.add(new_user)
 143 |     db.commit()
 144 |     db.refresh(new_user)
 145 |     return {"message": "Usuario creado", "id": new_user.id, "username": new_user.username, "role": new_user.role}
 146 | 
 147 | 
 148 | # ── Activar / Desactivar usuario — solo ADMIN ─────────────
 149 | @router.patch("/users/{user_id}/toggle")
 150 | def toggle_user(
 151 |     user_id: int,
 152 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_admin),
 153 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 154 | ):
 155 |     user = db.query(User).filter(User.id == user_id).first()
 156 |     if not user:
 157 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Usuario no encontrado")
 158 |     if user.username == current_user.username:
 159 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="No puedes desactivarte a ti mismo")
 160 |     user.is_active = not user.is_active
 161 |     db.commit()
 162 |     return {"message": f"Usuario {'activado' if user.is_active else 'desactivado'}", "is_active": user.is_active}
 163 | 
 164 | 
 165 | # ── Cambiar contraseña de un usuario — solo ADMIN ─────────
 166 | @router.patch("/users/{user_id}/password")
 167 | def change_user_password(
 168 |     user_id: int,
 169 |     data: UserPasswordChange,
 170 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_admin),
 171 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 172 | ):
 173 |     from app.services.security import hash_password
 174 |     user = db.query(User).filter(User.id == user_id).first()
 175 |     if not user:
 176 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Usuario no encontrado")
 177 |     if not data.new_password or len(data.new_password) < 6:
 178 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="La contraseña debe tener al menos 6 caracteres")
 179 |     user.password_hash = hash_password(data.new_password)
 180 |     db.commit()
 181 |     return {"message": "Contraseña actualizada correctamente"}
 182 | 
 183 | 
 184 | # ── Eliminar usuario — solo ADMIN ─────────────────────────
 185 | @router.delete("/users/{user_id}")
 186 | def delete_user(
 187 |     user_id: int,
 188 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_admin),
 189 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 190 | ):
 191 |     user = db.query(User).filter(User.id == user_id).first()
 192 |     if not user:
 193 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Usuario no encontrado")
 194 |     if user.username == current_user.username:
 195 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="No puedes eliminar tu propia cuenta")
 196 |     db.delete(user)
 197 |     db.commit()
 198 |     return {"message": "Usuario eliminado"}

   1 | """
   2 | app/routers/charges.py  v2

   7 | 
   8 | from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException
   9 | from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
  10 | 
  11 | from app.models.charge import Charge
  12 | from app.models.unit import Unit
  13 | from app.models.payment_application import PaymentApplication
  14 | from app.schemas.charge import ChargeCreate, ChargeResponse
  15 | from app.database import get_db
  16 | from app.services.auth_service import get_current_user
  17 | from app.models.user import User
  18 | 
  19 | router = APIRouter(prefix="/charges", tags=["Charges"])
  20 | 
  21 | 
  22 | def _require_admin(current_user: User):
  23 |     if current_user.role != "ADMIN":
  24 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Solo el administrador puede realizar esta acción")
  25 | 
  26 | 
  27 | @router.post("/", response_model=ChargeResponse)
  28 | def create_charge(
  29 |     charge_data: ChargeCreate,
  30 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
  31 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user),
  32 | ):
  33 |     unit = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.id == charge_data.unit_id).first()
  34 |     if not unit:
  35 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Unidad no encontrada")
  36 | 
  37 |     if charge_data.amount <= 0:
  38 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="El monto debe ser mayor a 0")
  39 | 
  40 |     if charge_data.due_date < charge_data.date_created:
  41 |         raise HTTPException(
  42 |             status_code=400,
  43 |             detail="La fecha de vencimiento no puede ser menor a la fecha de registro",
  44 |         )
  45 | 
  46 |     new_charge = Charge(
  47 |         unit_id=charge_data.unit_id,
  48 |         description=charge_data.description,
  49 |         amount=charge_data.amount,
  50 |         balance=charge_data.amount,
  51 |         status="PENDIENTE",
  52 |         date_created=charge_data.date_created,
  53 |         due_date=charge_data.due_date,
  54 |     )
  55 |     db.add(new_charge)
  56 |     db.commit()
  57 |     db.refresh(new_charge)
  58 |     return new_charge
  59 | 
  60 | 
  61 | @router.put("/{charge_id}")
  62 | def update_charge(
  63 |     charge_id: int,
  64 |     charge_data: ChargeCreate,
  65 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
  66 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user),
  67 | ):
  68 |     """Editar un cargo existente — solo ADMIN."""
  69 |     _require_admin(current_user)
  70 | 
  71 |     charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == charge_id).first()
  72 |     if not charge:
  73 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Cargo no encontrado")
  74 | 
  75 |     if charge_data.amount <= 0:
  76 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="El monto debe ser mayor a 0")
  77 | 
  78 |     if charge_data.due_date < charge_data.date_created:
  79 |         raise HTTPException(
  80 |             status_code=400,
  81 |             detail="La fecha de vencimiento no puede ser menor a la fecha de registro",
  82 |         )
  83 | 
  84 |     from decimal import Decimal
  85 |     from sqlalchemy import func
  86 |     from app.models.payment_application import PaymentApplication
  87 | 
  88 |     # Calcular ya aplicado
  89 |     applied = db.query(
  90 |         func.coalesce(func.sum(PaymentApplication.applied_amount), 0)
  91 |     ).filter(PaymentApplication.charge_id == charge_id).scalar()
  92 | 
  93 |     new_amount  = Decimal(str(charge_data.amount))
  94 |     new_balance = new_amount - Decimal(str(applied))
  95 | 
  96 |     charge.description  = charge_data.description
  97 |     charge.amount       = new_amount
  98 |     charge.balance      = max(new_balance, Decimal("0.00"))
  99 |     charge.date_created = charge_data.date_created
 100 |     charge.due_date     = charge_data.due_date
 101 | 
 102 |     # Recalcular estado
 103 |     if new_balance <= 0:
 104 |         charge.status = "PAGADO"
 105 |     elif applied > 0:
 106 |         charge.status = "PARCIAL"
 107 |     else:
 108 |         charge.status = "PENDIENTE"
 109 | 
 110 |     db.commit()
 111 |     db.refresh(charge)
 112 |     return charge
 113 | 
 114 | 
 115 | @router.delete("/{charge_id}")
 116 | def delete_charge(
 117 |     charge_id: int,
 118 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 119 |     current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user),
 120 | ):
 121 |     """Eliminar un cargo y sus aplicaciones de pago — solo ADMIN."""
 122 |     _require_admin(current_user)
 123 | 
 124 |     charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == charge_id).first()
 125 |     if not charge:
 126 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Cargo no encontrado")
 127 | 
 128 |     # Eliminar aplicaciones asociadas primero
 129 |     db.query(PaymentApplication).filter(
 130 |         PaymentApplication.charge_id == charge_id
 131 |     ).delete()
 132 |     db.delete(charge)
 133 |     db.commit()
 134 |     return {"message": "Cargo eliminado correctamente"}
 135 |

 151 | @router.get("/invoices")
 152 | def get_invoices(db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
 153 |     invoices = db.query(Invoice).order_by(Invoice.created_at.desc()).all()
 154 |     result = []
 155 |     for inv in invoices:
 156 |         payment = db.query(Payment).filter(Payment.id == inv.payment_id).first()
 157 |         owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == payment.owner_id).first() if payment else None
 158 | 
 159 |         # Obtener unidad activa del propietario para la factura
 160 |         unit_number = None
 161 |         if payment and payment.owner_id:
 162 |             uo = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 163 |                 UnitOwner.owner_id == payment.owner_id,
 164 |                 UnitOwner.is_active == True
 165 |             ).first()
 166 |             if uo:
 167 |                 u = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.id == uo.unit_id).first()
 168 |                 if u:
 169 |                     unit_number = u.unit_number
 170 | 
 171 |         result.append({
 172 |             "id": inv.id,
 173 |             "invoice_number": inv.invoice_number,
 174 |             "fiscal_invoice_number": inv.fiscal_invoice_number,
 175 |             "payment_id": inv.payment_id,
 176 |             "owner_name": owner.full_name if owner else "—",
 177 |             "unit_number": unit_number or "—",
 178 |             "amount": float(payment.amount) if payment else 0,
 179 |             "created_at": inv.created_at,
 180 |             "pdf_path": inv.pdf_path,
 181 |             # receipt_number del pago si existe
 182 |             "receipt_number": getattr(payment, 'receipt_number', None) if payment else None,
 183 |         })
 184 |     return result

 187 | @router.get("/invoices/{invoice_id}/download")
 188 | def download_invoice(invoice_id: int, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
 189 |     invoice = db.query(Invoice).filter(Invoice.id == invoice_id).first()
 190 |     if not invoice or not invoice.pdf_path:
 191 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Factura no encontrada")
 192 | 
 193 |     from fastapi.responses import FileResponse
 194 |     import os
 195 | 
 196 |     if os.path.exists(invoice.pdf_path):
 197 |         return FileResponse(
 198 |             invoice.pdf_path,
 199 |             media_type="application/pdf",
 200 |             filename=f"factura_{invoice.invoice_number}.pdf",
 201 |         )
 202 |     raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Archivo PDF no encontrado")
 203 | 
 204 | 
 205 | @router.get("/payments-history")
 206 | def payments_history(db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
 207 |     """
 208 |     Devuelve todos los pagos del sistema con detalle completo.
 209 |     Incluye receipt_number si está disponible.
 210 |     """
 211 |     from app.models.payment import Payment
 212 |     from app.models.payment_application import PaymentApplication
 213 |     from app.models.charge import Charge
 214 |     from app.models.unit import Unit
 215 |     from app.models.unit_owner import UnitOwner
 216 |     from app.models.owner import Owner
 217 | 
 218 |     payments = db.query(Payment).order_by(Payment.payment_date.desc()).all()
 219 |     result   = []
 220 | 
 221 |     for p in payments:
 222 |         owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == p.owner_id).first() if p.owner_id else None
 223 | 
 224 |         unit_number = None
 225 |         if p.owner_id:
 226 |             uo = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 227 |                 UnitOwner.owner_id == p.owner_id,
 228 |                 UnitOwner.is_active == True
 229 |             ).first()
 230 |             if uo:
 231 |                 u = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.id == uo.unit_id).first()
 232 |                 if u:
 233 |                     unit_number = u.unit_number
 234 | 
 235 |         apps = db.query(PaymentApplication).filter(
 236 |             PaymentApplication.payment_id == p.id
 237 |         ).all()
 238 | 
 239 |         concepto    = None
 240 |         observacion = None
 241 | 
 242 |         if apps:
 243 |             descs = []
 244 |             for app in apps:
 245 |                 c = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == app.charge_id).first()
 246 |                 if c:
 247 |                     descs.append(c.description)
 248 |             if descs:
 249 |                 concepto = " / ".join(set(descs))
 250 | 
 251 |         if not concepto:
 252 |             ref = p.reference or ""
 253 |             if " — " in ref:
 254 |                 partes      = ref.split(" — ", 1)
 255 |                 concepto    = partes[0].strip()
 256 |                 observacion = partes[1].strip()
 257 |             else:
 258 |                 concepto    = ref.strip() or "—"
 259 |                 observacion = None
 260 | 
 261 |         # Factura vinculada al pago (si existe)
 262 |         invoice = db.query(Invoice).filter(Invoice.payment_id == p.id).first()
 263 | 
 264 |         result.append({
 265 |             "payment_id":    p.id,
 266 |             "factura":       p.invoice_number,
 267 |             "fecha":         str(p.payment_date) if p.payment_date else None,
 268 |             "owner_id":      p.owner_id,
 269 |             "owner_name":    owner.full_name if owner else "—",
 270 |             "unit_number":   unit_number or "—",
 271 |             "concepto":      concepto or "—",
 272 |             "observacion":   observacion,
 273 |             "monto":         float(p.amount) if p.amount else 0,
 274 |             "referencia":    p.reference,
 275 |             "receipt_number": getattr(p, 'receipt_number', None),
 276 |             "tiene_cargos":  len(apps) > 0,
 277 |             "tiene_factura": invoice is not None,
 278 |             "invoice_id":    invoice.id if invoice else None,
 279 |         })
 280 | 
 281 |     return result
 282 |

 285 | 
 286 | class PaymentUpdate(BaseModel):
 287 |     payment_date:   date
 288 |     amount:         float
 289 |     invoice_number: Optional[str] = None
 290 |     reference:      Optional[str] = None
 291 |     receipt_number: Optional[str] = None
 292 |

 294 | # ── Dependencia admin ─────────────────────────────────────────
 295 | def _admin_only(current_user = Depends(get_current_user_dep)):
 296 |     if current_user.role != "ADMIN":
 297 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=403, detail="Solo el administrador puede realizar esta acción")
 298 |     return current_user
 299 | 
 300 | 
 301 | # ── Editar pago — solo ADMIN ─────────────────────────────────
 302 | @router.put("/payment/{payment_id}")
 303 | def update_payment(
 304 |     payment_id: int,
 305 |     data: PaymentUpdate,
 306 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 307 |     current_user = Depends(_admin_only),
 308 | ):
 309 |     payment = db.query(Payment).filter(Payment.id == payment_id).first()
 310 |     if not payment:
 311 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Pago no encontrado")
 312 | 
 313 |     from decimal import Decimal
 314 |     payment.payment_date   = data.payment_date
 315 |     payment.amount         = Decimal(str(data.amount))
 316 |     payment.invoice_number = data.invoice_number
 317 |     payment.reference      = data.reference
 318 |     if hasattr(payment, 'receipt_number'):
 319 |         payment.receipt_number = data.receipt_number
 320 |     db.commit()
 321 |     db.refresh(payment)
 322 |     return {"message": "Pago actualizado", "payment_id": payment.id}
 323 | 
 324 | 
 325 | # ── Eliminar pago — solo ADMIN ───────────────────────────────
 326 | # FIX: El Error 500 al borrar ocurría porque la factura vinculada (Invoice)
 327 | # tenía una FK a payment_id y no se eliminaba antes de borrar el pago.
 328 | @router.delete("/payment/{payment_id}")
 329 | def delete_payment(
 330 |     payment_id: int,
 331 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 332 |     current_user = Depends(_admin_only),
 333 | ):
 334 |     """
 335 |     Elimina un pago y revierte los saldos de los cargos afectados.
 336 |     También elimina la factura vinculada si existe.
 337 |     Solo ADMIN.
 338 |     """
 339 |     from decimal import Decimal
 340 |     from app.models.payment_application import PaymentApplication
 341 |     from app.models.charge import Charge
 342 | 
 343 |     payment = db.query(Payment).filter(Payment.id == payment_id).first()
 344 |     if not payment:
 345 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Pago no encontrado")
 346 | 
 347 |     try:
 348 |         # 1. Revertir saldos de los cargos afectados
 349 |         apps = db.query(PaymentApplication).filter(
 350 |             PaymentApplication.payment_id == payment_id
 351 |         ).all()
 352 | 
 353 |         for app in apps:
 354 |             charge = db.query(Payment.__class__).filter(
 355 |                 PaymentApplication.charge_id == app.charge_id
 356 |             ).first() if False else db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == app.charge_id).first()
 357 | 
 358 |             if charge:
 359 |                 charge.balance = Decimal(str(charge.balance)) + Decimal(str(app.applied_amount))
 360 |                 if charge.balance >= Decimal(str(charge.amount)):
 361 |                     charge.status = "PENDIENTE"
 362 |                 else:
 363 |                     charge.status = "PARCIAL"
 364 |             db.delete(app)
 365 | 
 366 |         # 2. Eliminar la factura vinculada (si existe) — esto era la causa del Error 500
 367 |         invoice = db.query(Invoice).filter(Invoice.payment_id == payment_id).first()
 368 |         if invoice:
 369 |             db.delete(invoice)
 370 | 
 371 |         # 3. Eliminar el pago
 372 |         db.delete(payment)
 373 |         db.commit()
 374 | 
 375 |     except Exception as e:
 376 |         db.rollback()
 377 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Error al eliminar pago: {str(e)}")
 378 | 
 379 |     return {"message": "Pago eliminado y saldos revertidos correctamente"}
 380 | 
 381 | 
 382 | # ── Endpoint para que admin vea todos los pagos ───────────────
 383 | @router.get("/all-payments")
 384 | def get_all_payments(
 385 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
 386 |     current_user = Depends(_admin_only),
 387 | ):
 388 |     from app.models.owner import Owner
 389 |     from app.models.unit_owner import UnitOwner
 390 |     from app.models.unit import Unit
 391 |     from app.models.payment_application import PaymentApplication
 392 |     from app.models.charge import Charge
 393 | 
 394 |     payments = db.query(Payment).order_by(Payment.payment_date.desc()).all()
 395 |     result   = []
 396 | 
 397 |     for p in payments:
 398 |         owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == p.owner_id).first()
 399 |         uo    = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 400 |             UnitOwner.owner_id == p.owner_id, UnitOwner.is_active == True
 401 |         ).first()
 402 |         unit  = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.id == uo.unit_id).first() if uo else None
 403 | 
 404 |         apps  = db.query(PaymentApplication).filter(
 405 |             PaymentApplication.payment_id == p.id
 406 |         ).all()
 407 |         cargos = []
 408 |         for a in apps:
 409 |             c = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == a.charge_id).first()
 410 |             if c:
 411 |                 cargos.append({"description": c.description, "applied": float(a.applied_amount)})
 412 | 
 413 |         invoice = db.query(Invoice).filter(Invoice.payment_id == p.id).first()
 414 | 
 415 |         result.append({
 416 |             "payment_id":    p.id,
 417 |             "fecha":         str(p.payment_date),
 418 |             "owner_name":    owner.full_name if owner else "—",
 419 |             "unit_number":   unit.unit_number if unit else "—",
 420 |             "amount":        float(p.amount),
 421 |             "invoice_number": p.invoice_number,
 422 |             "reference":     p.reference,
 423 |             "receipt_number": getattr(p, 'receipt_number', None),
 424 |             "cargos":        cargos,
 425 |             "tiene_factura": invoice is not None,
 426 |             "invoice_id":    invoice.id if invoice else None,
 427 |         })
 428 | 
 429 |     return result

  75 |     property_id: int,
  76 |     property_data: PropertyCreate,
  77 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db)
  78 | ):
  79 |     property_obj = db.query(Property).filter(Property.id == property_id).first()
  80 | 
  81 |     if not property_obj:
  82 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Propiedad no encontrada")
  83 | 
  84 |     property_obj.name = property_data.name
  85 |     property_obj.type = property_data.type
  86 |     property_obj.address = property_data.address
  87 | 
  88 |     db.commit()
  89 |     db.refresh(property_obj)
  90 | 
  91 |     return property_obj
  92 | 
  93 | 
  94 | # Registrar ocupante en unidad de propiedad
  95 | @router.post("/{property_id}/register-occupant")
  96 | def register_occupant(
  97 |     property_id: int,
  98 |     data: RegisterOccupant,
  99 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db)
 100 | ):
 101 |     try:
 102 |         property_obj = db.query(Property).filter(Property.id == property_id).first()
 103 |         if not property_obj:
 104 |             raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Propiedad no encontrada")
 105 | 
 106 |         # Buscar o crear unidad
 107 |         unit = db.query(Unit).filter(
 108 |             Unit.property_id == property_id,
 109 |             Unit.unit_number == data.unit_number
 110 |         ).first()
 111 | 
 112 |         if not unit:
 113 |             unit = Unit(
 114 |                 property_id=property_id,
 115 |                 unit_number=data.unit_number,
 116 |                 floor=data.floor
 117 |             )
 118 |             db.add(unit)
 119 |             db.flush()
 120 | 
 121 |         # Verificar ocupación activa
 122 |         active = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 123 |             UnitOwner.unit_id == unit.id,
 124 |             UnitOwner.is_active == True
 125 |         ).first()
 126 | 
 127 |         if active:
 128 |             raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="La unidad ya está ocupada")
 129 | 
 130 |         # Crear propietario
 131 |         owner = Owner(
 132 |             full_name=data.full_name,
 133 |             identification=data.identification,
 134 |             email=data.email,
 135 |             phone=data.phone
 136 |         )
 137 |         db.add(owner)
 138 |         db.flush()
 139 | 
 140 |         # Crear relación
 141 |         occupancy = UnitOwner(
 142 |             unit_id=unit.id,
 143 |             owner_id=owner.id,
 144 |             start_date=data.start_date,
 145 |             is_active=True
 146 |         )
 147 |         db.add(occupancy)
 148 | 
 149 |         db.commit()
 150 | 
 151 |         return {"message": "Ocupante registrado correctamente"}
 152 | 
 153 |     except SQLAlchemyError:
 154 |         db.rollback()
 155 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail="Error interno")
 156 |

  62 |     result = []
  63 |     for s in suppliers:
  64 |         total_paid    = db.query(func.sum(SupplierPayment.amount)).filter(
  65 |             SupplierPayment.supplier_id == s.id, SupplierPayment.status == "PAGADO"
  66 |         ).scalar() or 0
  67 |         total_pending = db.query(func.sum(SupplierPayment.amount)).filter(
  68 |             SupplierPayment.supplier_id == s.id, SupplierPayment.status == "PENDIENTE"
  69 |         ).scalar() or 0
  70 |         result.append({
  71 |             "id": s.id, "name": s.name, "category": s.category,
  72 |             "ruc": s.ruc, "contact_name": s.contact_name,
  73 |             "phone": s.phone, "email": s.email,
  74 |             "address": s.address, "notes": s.notes,
  75 |             "total_paid": float(total_paid),
  76 |             "total_pending": float(total_pending),

 196 |     if not q: raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Cotización no encontrada")
 197 |     for k, v in data.dict().items(): setattr(q, k, v)
 198 |     db.commit(); db.refresh(q); return q

 200 | @router.delete("/quotes/{quote_id}")
 201 | def delete_quote(quote_id: int, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
 202 |     q = db.query(SupplierQuote).filter(SupplierQuote.id == quote_id).first()
 203 |     if not q: raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Cotización no encontrada")
 204 |     # Eliminar PDF si existe
 205 |     if getattr(q, 'pdf_path', None) and os.path.exists(q.pdf_path):
 206 |         os.remove(q.pdf_path)
 207 |     db.delete(q); db.commit()
 208 |     return {"message": "Cotización eliminada"}
 209 | 
 210 | # ── Upload PDF de cotización ──────────────────
 211 | @router.post("/quotes/{quote_id}/upload-pdf")
 212 | async def upload_quote_pdf(
 213 |     quote_id: int,
 214 |     file: UploadFile = File(...),
 215 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db)
 216 | ):
 217 |     q = db.query(SupplierQuote).filter(SupplierQuote.id == quote_id).first()
 218 |     if not q: raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Cotización no encontrada")
 219 | 
 220 |     # Validar que sea PDF
 221 |     if not file.content_type == "application/pdf" and not file.filename.lower().endswith(".pdf"):
 222 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Solo se aceptan archivos PDF")
 223 | 
 224 |     # Eliminar PDF anterior si existe
 225 |     if getattr(q, 'pdf_path', None) and os.path.exists(q.pdf_path):
 226 |         os.remove(q.pdf_path)
 227 | 
 228 |     # Guardar nuevo PDF
 229 |     filename    = f"quote_{quote_id}_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}.pdf"
 230 |     file_path   = os.path.join(PDF_DIR, filename)
 231 | 
 232 |     with open(file_path, "wb") as f:
 233 |         shutil.copyfileobj(file.file, f)
 234 | 
 235 |     q.pdf_path = file_path
 236 |     db.commit()
 237 | 
 238 |     return {"message": "PDF subido correctamente", "pdf_path": file_path}
 239 | 
 240 | # ── Descargar PDF de cotización ───────────────
 241 | @router.get("/quotes/{quote_id}/pdf")
 242 | def download_quote_pdf(quote_id: int, db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
 243 |     q = db.query(SupplierQuote).filter(SupplierQuote.id == quote_id).first()
 244 |     if not q: raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Cotización no encontrada")
 245 | 
 246 |     pdf_path = getattr(q, 'pdf_path', None)
 247 |     if not pdf_path or not os.path.exists(pdf_path):
 248 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="PDF no encontrado")
 249 | 
 250 |     return FileResponse(
 251 |         pdf_path,
 252 |         media_type="application/pdf",
 253 |         filename=f"cotizacion_{quote_id}.pdf"
 254 |     )
 255 |

  23 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db)
  24 | ):

   1 | """
   2 | app/services/auth_service.py
   3 | JWT + creación de usuario admin por defecto al arrancar.
   4 | """
   5 | 
   6 | from datetime import datetime, timedelta
   7 | from typing import Optional
   8 | 
   9 | from fastapi import Depends, HTTPException, status
  10 | from fastapi.security import OAuth2PasswordBearer
  11 | from jose import JWTError, jwt
  12 | from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
  13 | 
  14 | from app.config import settings
  15 | from app.database import get_db
  16 | from app.models.user import User
  17 | from app.services.security import verify_password, hash_password
  18 | 
  19 | oauth2_scheme = OAuth2PasswordBearer(tokenUrl="/api/auth/token")
  20 | 
  21 | 
  22 | # ── JWT ──────────────────────────────────────
  23 | def create_access_token(data: dict, expires_delta: Optional[timedelta] = None) -> str:
  24 |     payload = data.copy()
  25 |     payload["exp"] = datetime.utcnow() + (expires_delta or timedelta(minutes=60))
  26 |     return jwt.encode(payload, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithm=settings.ALGORITHM)
  27 | 
  28 | 
  29 | def decode_token(token: str) -> Optional[dict]:
  30 |     try:
  31 |         return jwt.decode(token, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithms=[settings.ALGORITHM])
  32 |     except JWTError:
  33 |         return None
  34 | 
  35 | 
  36 | # ── Autenticar ───────────────────────────────
  37 | def authenticate_user(db: Session, username: str, password: str) -> Optional[User]:
  38 |     user = db.query(User).filter(User.username == username).first()
  39 |     if not user or not user.is_active:
  40 |         return None
  41 |     if not verify_password(password, user.password_hash):
  42 |         return None
  43 |     return user
  44 | 
  45 | 
  46 | # ── get_current_user (dependencia FastAPI) ────
  47 | def get_current_user(
  48 |     token: str = Depends(oauth2_scheme),
  49 |     db: Session = Depends(get_db),
  50 | ) -> User:
  51 |     exc = HTTPException(
  52 |         status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
  53 |         detail="Sesión inválida o expirada",
  54 |         headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},
  55 |     )
  56 |     payload = decode_token(token)
  57 |     if not payload:
  58 |         raise exc
  59 |     username = payload.get("sub")
  60 |     if not username:
  61 |         raise exc
  62 |     user = db.query(User).filter(User.username == username).first()
  63 |     if not user or not user.is_active:
  64 |         raise exc
  65 |     return user
  66 | 
  67 | 
  68 | # ── Crear admin por defecto al arrancar ───────
  69 | def create_default_admin(db: Session):
  70 |     """
  71 |     Se llama desde app/main.py al iniciar.
  72 |     Crea el usuario admin si no existe usando las variables del .env:
  73 |       DEFAULT_ADMIN_USER / DEFAULT_ADMIN_PASS
  74 |     """
  75 |     import os
  76 |     username = getattr(settings, "DEFAULT_ADMIN_USER", "admin")
  77 |     password = getattr(settings, "DEFAULT_ADMIN_PASS", "Admin123")
  78 | 
  79 |     if not db.query(User).filter(User.username == username).first():
  80 |         db.add(User(
  81 |             username=username,
  82 |             password_hash=hash_password(password),
  83 |             role="ADMIN",
  84 |             is_active=True,
  85 |         ))
  86 |         db.commit()
  87 |         print(f"[AUTH] Usuario admin creado: {username}")
  88 |

  19 | def _to_dec(val) -> Decimal:
  20 |     """Convierte cualquier valor numérico a Decimal de forma segura."""
  21 |     return Decimal(str(val)).quantize(Decimal("0.01"), rounding=ROUND_HALF_UP)
  22 | 
  23 | 
  24 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  25 | # Función 1 — Balance de un cargo específico
  26 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  27 | def get_charge_balance(db: Session, charge_id: int):
  28 |     charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == charge_id).first()
  29 | 
  30 |     if not charge:
  31 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Cargo no encontrado")
  32 | 
  33 |     total_applied_raw = (
  34 |         db.query(func.coalesce(func.sum(PaymentApplication.applied_amount), 0))
  35 |         .filter(PaymentApplication.charge_id == charge_id)
  36 |         .scalar()
  37 |     )
  38 | 
  39 |     # ✅ Todo en Decimal para evitar errores float vs Decimal (SQLite y PostgreSQL)
  40 |     amount       = _to_dec(charge.amount)
  41 |     total_applied = _to_dec(total_applied_raw)
  42 |     balance      = amount - total_applied
  43 | 
  44 |     return {
  45 |         "charge_id":      charge.id,
  46 |         "total_amount":   amount,
  47 |         "applied_amount": total_applied,
  48 |         "balance":        balance,
  49 |     }
  50 | 
  51 | 
  52 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  53 | # Función 2 — Estado textual de un cargo
  54 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  55 | def get_charge_status(db: Session, charge_id: int) -> str:
  56 |     bd = get_charge_balance(db, charge_id)
  57 | 
  58 |     if bd["applied_amount"] == Decimal("0.00"):
  59 |         return "PENDIENTE"
  60 |     elif bd["balance"] > Decimal("0.00"):
  61 |         return "PARCIAL"
  62 |     else:
  63 |         return "PAGADO"
  64 | 
  65 | 
  66 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  67 | # Función 3 — Aplicar pago a un cargo individual
  68 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  69 | def apply_payment_to_charge(db: Session, payment_id: int, charge_id: int, amount: float):
  70 |     amount_dec = _to_dec(amount)
  71 | 
  72 |     if amount_dec <= Decimal("0.00"):
  73 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="El monto debe ser mayor a 0")
  74 | 
  75 |     charge_balance   = get_charge_balance(db, charge_id)
  76 |     payment_balance  = _to_dec(get_payment_balance(db, payment_id))
  77 | 
  78 |     if amount_dec > charge_balance["balance"]:
  79 |         raise HTTPException(
  80 |             status_code=400,
  81 |             detail=f"Monto ${float(amount_dec):.2f} supera el saldo del cargo (${float(charge_balance['balance']):.2f})"
  82 |         )
  83 | 
  84 |     if amount_dec > payment_balance:
  85 |         raise HTTPException(
  86 |             status_code=400,
  87 |             detail=f"Saldo del pago insuficiente (disponible: ${float(payment_balance):.2f})"
  88 |         )
  89 | 
  90 |     application = PaymentApplication(
  91 |         payment_id=payment_id,
  92 |         charge_id=charge_id,
  93 |         applied_amount=amount_dec,
  94 |     )
  95 |     db.add(application)
  96 | 
  97 |     charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == charge_id).first()
  98 |     new_balance = _to_dec(charge.balance) - amount_dec
  99 | 
 100 |     if new_balance <= Decimal("0.00"):
 101 |         charge.balance = Decimal("0.00")
 102 |         charge.status  = "PAGADO"
 103 |     else:
 104 |         charge.balance = new_balance
 105 |         charge.status  = "PARCIAL"
 106 | 
 107 |     db.commit()
 108 |     db.refresh(application)
 109 |     return application

 113 | # Función 4 CORREGIDA — Estado de cuenta por propietario
 114 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 115 | # BUG original: el JOIN con UnitOwner sin filtro is_active=True
 116 | # devolvía duplicados o cargos de periodos anteriores.

 120 | def get_owner_account_statement(db, owner_id: int):
 121 |     from fastapi import HTTPException
 122 |     from app.models.charge import Charge
 123 |     from app.models.unit import Unit
 124 |     from app.models.unit_owner import UnitOwner
 125 |     from app.models.owner import Owner
 126 | 
 127 |     owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == owner_id).first()
 128 |     if not owner:
 129 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Propietario no encontrado")
 130 | 
 131 |     # Obtener TODAS las unidades que alguna vez tuvo este propietario
 132 |     ownerships = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 133 |         UnitOwner.owner_id == owner_id
 134 |     ).all()
 135 | 
 136 |     unit_ids = list({o.unit_id for o in ownerships})
 137 |     if not unit_ids:
 138 |         return []
 139 | 
 140 |     charges = db.query(Charge).filter(
 141 |         Charge.unit_id.in_(unit_ids)
 142 |     ).order_by(Charge.due_date).all()
 143 | 
 144 |     result = []
 145 |     for charge in charges:
 146 |         bd   = get_charge_balance(db, charge.id)
 147 |         unit = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.id == charge.unit_id).first()
 148 |         result.append({
 149 |             "charge_id":   charge.id,
 150 |             "unit_number": unit.unit_number if unit else "N/A",
 151 |             "description": charge.description,
 152 |             "due_date":    str(charge.due_date),
 153 |             "total":       float(bd["total_amount"]),
 154 |             "paid":        float(bd["applied_amount"]),
 155 |             "balance":     float(bd["balance"]),
 156 |             "status":      get_charge_status(db, charge.id),
 157 |         })
 158 | 
 159 |     return result

 164 | # Función 4b — Estado de cuenta por unidad  ← NUEVO
 165 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 166 | def get_unit_account_statement(db: Session, unit_id: int):
 167 |     unit = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.id == unit_id).first()
 168 |     if not unit:
 169 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Unidad no encontrada")
 170 | 
 171 |     active_ownership = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 172 |         UnitOwner.unit_id == unit_id,
 173 |         UnitOwner.is_active == True,
 174 |     ).first()
 175 | 
 176 |     owner = None
 177 |     if active_ownership:
 178 |         owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == active_ownership.owner_id).first()
 179 | 
 180 |     charges = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.unit_id == unit_id).all()
 181 |     statement = []
 182 | 
 183 |     for charge in charges:
 184 |         bd = get_charge_balance(db, charge.id)
 185 |         statement.append({
 186 |             "charge_id":   charge.id,
 187 |             "unit_number": unit.unit_number,
 188 |             "owner_name":  owner.full_name if owner else "Sin propietario",
 189 |             "owner_id":    owner.id if owner else None,
 190 |             "description": charge.description,
 191 |             "due_date":    str(charge.due_date),
 192 |             "total":       float(bd["total_amount"]),
 193 |             "paid":        float(bd["applied_amount"]),
 194 |             "balance":     float(bd["balance"]),
 195 |             "status":      get_charge_status(db, charge.id),
 196 |         })
 197 | 
 198 |     return {
 199 |         "unit_id":    unit.id,
 200 |         "unit_number": unit.unit_number,
 201 |         "owner_name": owner.full_name if owner else "Sin propietario",
 202 |         "owner_id":   owner.id if owner else None,
 203 |         "charges":    statement,
 204 |     }

 208 | # Función 5 — Cargo general para toda una propiedad
 209 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 210 | def create_general_charge_for_property(
 211 |     db: Session, property_id: int, description: str, amount: float, due_date: date
 212 | ):
 213 |     property_obj = db.query(Property).filter(Property.id == property_id).first()
 214 |     if not property_obj:
 215 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Propiedad no encontrada")
 216 | 
 217 |     units = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.property_id == property_id).all()
 218 |     if not units:
 219 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="La propiedad no tiene unidades")
 220 | 
 221 |     amount_dec = _to_dec(amount)
 222 |     today      = date.today()
 223 |     created    = []
 224 | 
 225 |     for unit in units:
 226 |         charge = Charge(
 227 |             unit_id=unit.id, description=description,
 228 |             amount=amount_dec, balance=amount_dec,
 229 |             status="PENDIENTE", date_created=today, due_date=due_date,
 230 |         )
 231 |         db.add(charge)
 232 |         created.append(charge)
 233 | 
 234 |     db.commit()
 235 |     return created

 238 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 239 | # Función 6 — Resumen financiero de una propiedad
 240 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 241 | def get_property_financial_summary(db: Session, property_id: int):
 242 |     property_obj = db.query(Property).filter(Property.id == property_id).first()
 243 |     if not property_obj:
 244 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Propiedad no encontrada")
 245 | 
 246 |     charges = (
 247 |         db.query(Charge)
 248 |         .join(Unit, Charge.unit_id == Unit.id)
 249 |         .filter(Unit.property_id == property_id)
 250 |         .all()
 251 |     )
 252 | 
 253 |     total_charged = Decimal("0.00")
 254 |     total_paid    = Decimal("0.00")
 255 | 
 256 |     for charge in charges:
 257 |         bd = get_charge_balance(db, charge.id)
 258 |         total_charged += bd["total_amount"]
 259 |         total_paid    += bd["applied_amount"]
 260 | 
 261 |     return {
 262 |         "property":      property_obj.name,
 263 |         "total_charged": float(total_charged),
 264 |         "total_paid":    float(total_paid),
 265 |         "total_pending": float(total_charged - total_paid),
 266 |     }

 269 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 270 | # Función 7 — Balance disponible de un pago
 271 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 272 | def get_payment_balance(db: Session, payment_id: int) -> float:
 273 |     payment = db.query(Payment).filter(Payment.id == payment_id).first()
 274 |     if not payment:
 275 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Pago no encontrado")
 276 | 
 277 |     total_applied_raw = (
 278 |         db.query(func.coalesce(func.sum(PaymentApplication.applied_amount), 0))
 279 |         .filter(PaymentApplication.payment_id == payment_id)
 280 |         .scalar()
 281 |     )
 282 | 
 283 |     return float(_to_dec(payment.amount) - _to_dec(total_applied_raw))
 284 |

 286 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 287 | # Función 8 — Crear pago + aplicar cargos (atómico)
 288 | # ✅ CORREGIDO: flush() en lugar de commit() parcial
 289 | # ✅ CORREGIDO: un solo commit al final — todo o nada
 290 | # ✅ CORREGIDO: Decimal en todas las comparaciones
 291 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 292 | # nueva función 8b — Crear pago con aplicaciones (corrección de bugs y mejoras)
 293 | def create_payment_with_applications(db, payment_data):
 294 |     """
 295 |     FIX: Ahora también guarda receipt_number si el modelo Payment lo soporta.
 296 |     """
 297 |     from decimal import Decimal
 298 |     from fastapi import HTTPException
 299 |     from app.models.payment import Payment
 300 |     from app.models.payment_application import PaymentApplication
 301 |     from app.models.charge import Charge
 302 | 
 303 |     def _to_dec(v):
 304 |         return Decimal(str(v)) if v is not None else Decimal("0.00")
 305 | 
 306 |     total_to_apply = _to_dec(sum(app.amount for app in payment_data.applications))
 307 |     payment_amount = _to_dec(payment_data.amount)
 308 | 
 309 |     if total_to_apply > payment_amount:
 310 |         raise HTTPException(
 311 |             status_code=400,
 312 |             detail=f"Las aplicaciones (${float(total_to_apply):.2f}) superan el monto del pago (${float(payment_amount):.2f})"
 313 |         )
 314 | 
 315 |     payment = Payment(
 316 |         owner_id       = payment_data.owner_id,
 317 |         payment_date   = payment_data.payment_date,
 318 |         amount         = payment_amount,
 319 |         invoice_number = getattr(payment_data, "invoice_number", None),
 320 |         reference      = getattr(payment_data, "reference", None),
 321 |     )
 322 |     # Guardar receipt_number si el modelo lo tiene
 323 |     if hasattr(payment, 'receipt_number'):
 324 |         payment.receipt_number = getattr(payment_data, 'receipt_number', None)
 325 | 
 326 |     try:
 327 |         db.add(payment)
 328 |         db.flush()
 329 | 
 330 |         for app in payment_data.applications:
 331 |             app_amount = _to_dec(app.amount)
 332 | 
 333 |             charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == app.charge_id).first()
 334 |             if not charge:
 335 |                 raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail=f"Cargo {app.charge_id} no encontrado")
 336 | 
 337 |             charge_balance = _to_dec(charge.balance)
 338 | 
 339 |             if app_amount <= Decimal("0.00"):
 340 |                 raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="El monto de cada aplicación debe ser mayor a 0")
 341 | 
 342 |             if app_amount > charge_balance:
 343 |                 raise HTTPException(
 344 |                     status_code=400,
 345 |                     detail=f"El monto ${float(app_amount):.2f} supera el saldo de '{charge.description}' (${float(charge_balance):.2f})"
 346 |                 )
 347 | 
 348 |             db.add(PaymentApplication(
 349 |                 payment_id=payment.id,
 350 |                 charge_id=app.charge_id,
 351 |                 applied_amount=app_amount,
 352 |             ))
 353 | 
 354 |             new_balance = charge_balance - app_amount
 355 |             if new_balance <= Decimal("0.00"):
 356 |                 charge.balance = Decimal("0.00")
 357 |                 charge.status  = "PAGADO"
 358 |             else:
 359 |                 charge.balance = new_balance
 360 |                 charge.status  = "PARCIAL"
 361 | 
 362 |         db.commit()
 363 |         db.refresh(payment)
 364 | 
 365 |     except HTTPException:
 366 |         db.rollback()
 367 |         raise
 368 |     except Exception as e:
 369 |         db.rollback()
 370 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"Error al registrar pago: {str(e)}")
 371 | 
 372 |     return payment
 373 |

 434 | def get_payment_detail(db: Session, payment_id: int):
 435 |     payment = db.query(Payment).filter(Payment.id == payment_id).first()
 436 |     if not payment:
 437 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Pago no encontrado")
 438 |

 453 | def _resolve_payment_context(db: Session, payment, applications):
 454 |     owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == payment.owner_id).first() if payment.owner_id else None
 455 |     unit = None
 456 |     property_obj = None
 457 | 
 458 |     if applications:
 459 |         first_charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == applications[0].charge_id).first()
 460 |         unit = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.id == first_charge.unit_id).first() if first_charge else None
 461 |         property_obj = db.query(Property).filter(Property.id == unit.property_id).first() if unit else None
 462 | 
 463 |         if not owner and unit:
 464 |             ownership = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 465 |                 UnitOwner.unit_id == unit.id,
 466 |                 UnitOwner.is_active == True
 467 |             ).first()
 468 |             owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == ownership.owner_id).first() if ownership else None
 469 | 
 470 |     if not unit and owner:
 471 |         ownership = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 472 |             UnitOwner.owner_id == owner.id,
 473 |             UnitOwner.is_active == True
 474 |         ).first()
 475 |         unit = ownership.unit if ownership else None
 476 |         property_obj = unit.property if unit else None
 477 | 
 478 |     return owner, unit, property_obj
 479 | 
 480 | # nueva función 10b — Detalle completo de un pago para factura (corrección de bugs en owner/unit/property)
 481 | def get_payment_detail_full(db, payment_id: int):
 482 |     """
 483 |     Obtiene detalle completo de un pago para factura.
 484 |     FIX: Incluye owner, unit, property y receipt_number correctamente.
 485 |     """
 486 |     from fastapi import HTTPException
 487 |     from app.models.payment import Payment
 488 |     from app.models.owner import Owner

 496 |     payment = db.query(Payment).filter(Payment.id == payment_id).first()

 515 |     if applications:
 516 |         first_charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == applications[0].charge_id).first()

 518 |         if unit:
 519 |             property_obj = db.query(Property).filter(Property.id == unit.property_id).first()
 520 | 
 521 |         # Si aun no tenemos owner, buscarlo desde la unidad
 522 |         if not owner and unit:
 523 |             ownership = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(

 525 |                 UnitOwner.is_active == True
 526 |             ).first()
 527 |             if ownership:
 528 |                 owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == ownership.owner_id).first()
 529 | 
 530 |     # ── Si todavía no tenemos unidad, buscarla desde el owner ─
 531 |     if not unit and owner:
 532 |         ownership = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 533 |             UnitOwner.owner_id == owner.id,
 534 |             UnitOwner.is_active == True
 535 |         ).first()
 536 |         if ownership:
 537 |             unit = db.query(Unit).filter(Unit.id == ownership.unit_id).first()
 538 |             if unit:
 539 |                 property_obj = db.query(Property).filter(Property.id == unit.property_id).first()

 541 |     apps_detail = []
 542 |     for app in applications:
 543 |         charge = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == app.charge_id).first()

 545 |             "charge_id": app.charge_id,
 546 |             "description": charge.description if charge else f"Cargo #{app.charge_id}",
 547 |             "applied_amount": float(app.applied_amount),
 548 |         })

 552 |         "payment_date":          str(payment.payment_date),
 553 |         "amount":                float(payment.amount),

 569 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 570 | # Función 11 — Número de factura secuencial
 571 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 572 | def generate_invoice_number(db: Session) -> str:
 573 |     last = db.query(Invoice).order_by(Invoice.id.desc()).first()
 574 |     if not last:
 575 |         return "INV-000001"
 576 |     try:
 577 |         n = int(last.invoice_number.split("-")[1])
 578 |     except (IndexError, ValueError):
 579 |         n = 0
 580 |     return f"INV-{str(n + 1).zfill(6)}"

 583 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 584 | # Función 12 — Generar factura PDF
 585 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 586 | def create_invoice_for_payment(db: Session, payment_id: int, fiscal_number: str | None = None):
 587 |     payment = db.query(Payment).filter(Payment.id == payment_id).first()
 588 |     if not payment:
 589 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Pago no encontrado")
 590 | 
 591 |     if db.query(Invoice).filter(Invoice.payment_id == payment_id).first():
 592 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="Este pago ya tiene factura")
 593 | 
 594 |     invoice_number = generate_invoice_number(db)
 595 | 
 596 |     applications = db.query(PaymentApplication).filter(
 597 |         PaymentApplication.payment_id == payment.id
 598 |     ).all()
 599 |     if not applications:
 600 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="El pago no tiene cargos aplicados")
 601 | 
 602 |     owner, unit, property_obj = _resolve_payment_context(db, payment, applications)
 603 | 
 604 |     charges_detail = []
 605 |     for app in applications:
 606 |         c = db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.id == app.charge_id).first()
 607 |         if c:
 608 |             charges_detail.append({"description": c.description, "amount": float(app.applied_amount)})
 609 | 
 610 |     data = {
 611 |         "invoice_number":       invoice_number,
 612 |         "fiscal_invoice_number": fiscal_number or "",
 613 |         "issue_date":           date.today().strftime("%d de %B, %Y"),
 614 |         "owner_name":           owner.full_name if owner else "Desconocido",
 615 |         "unit_number":          unit.unit_number if unit else "N/A",
 616 |         "building_name":        property_obj.name if property_obj else "N/A",
 617 |         "property_address":     property_obj.address if property_obj else "N/A",
 618 |         "charges":              charges_detail,
 619 |         "total_amount":         float(payment.amount),
 620 |     }
 621 | 
 622 |     os.makedirs("invoices", exist_ok=True)
 623 |     pdf_path = f"invoices/{invoice_number}.pdf"
 624 | 
 625 |     from app.reports.pdf_generator import generate_invoice_pdf
 626 |     generate_invoice_pdf(data, pdf_path)
 627 | 
 628 |     invoice = Invoice(
 629 |         invoice_number=invoice_number,
 630 |         fiscal_invoice_number=fiscal_number,
 631 |         payment_id=payment.id,
 632 |         pdf_path=pdf_path,
 633 |     )
 634 |     db.add(invoice)
 635 |     db.commit()
 636 |     db.refresh(invoice)
 637 |     return invoice

 641 | # Función 13 — Estado de cuenta detallado de un propietario
 642 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 643 | def generate_owner_statement(db: Session, owner_id: int):
 644 |     owner = db.query(Owner).filter(Owner.id == owner_id).first()
 645 |     if not owner:
 646 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Propietario no encontrado")
 647 | 
 648 |     ownership = db.query(UnitOwner).filter(
 649 |         UnitOwner.owner_id == owner_id,
 650 |         UnitOwner.is_active == True,
 651 |     ).first()
 652 |     if not ownership:
 653 |         raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="No tiene unidad activa")
 654 | 
 655 |     unit         = ownership.unit
 656 |     property_obj = unit.property
 657 | 
 658 |     statement_data = []
 659 |     for charge in db.query(Charge).filter(Charge.unit_id == unit.id).all():
 660 |         bd = get_charge_balance(db, charge.id)
 661 | 
 662 |         payments_info = []
 663 |         for app in db.query(PaymentApplication).filter(PaymentApplication.charge_id == charge.id).all():
 664 |             inv = db.query(Invoice).filter(Invoice.payment_id == app.payment_id).first()
 665 |             pmt = db.query(Payment).filter(Payment.id == app.payment_id).first()
 666 |             payments_info.append({
 667 |             "payment_id":            app.payment_id,
 668 |             "payment_date":          str(pmt.payment_date) if pmt else None,
 669 |             "applied_amount":        float(app.applied_amount),
 670 |             "fiscal_invoice_number": inv.fiscal_invoice_number if inv else None,
 671 |             "reference":             pmt.reference if pmt else None,
 672 |         })
 673 | 
 674 |         statement_data.append({
 675 |             "description": charge.description,
 676 |             "due_date":    str(charge.due_date),
 677 |             "amount":      float(bd["total_amount"]),
 678 |             "paid":        float(bd["applied_amount"]),
 679 |             "balance":     float(bd["balance"]),
 680 |             "status":      get_charge_status(db, charge.id),
 681 |             "payments":    payments_info,
 682 |         })
 683 | 
 684 |     return {
 685 |         "property_name":    property_obj.name,
 686 |         "property_address": property_obj.address,
 687 |         "owner_name":       owner.full_name,
 688 |         "unit_number":      unit.unit_number,
 689 |         "statement":        statement_data,
 690 |     }

 693 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 694 | # Función 14 — Total pendiente por propiedad
 695 | # ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 696 | def property_accounts_receivable(db: Session, property_id: int):
 697 |     charges = (
 698 |         db.query(Charge)
 699 |         .join(Unit, Charge.unit_id == Unit.id)
 700 |         .filter(Unit.property_id == property_id)
 701 |         .all()
 702 |     )
 703 |     total = Decimal("0.00")
 704 |     for charge in charges:
 705 |         bd = get_charge_balance(db, charge.id)
 706 |         total += bd["balance"]
 707 |     return {"property_id": property_id, "total_pending": float(total)}

   1 | from passlib.hash import bcrypt
   2 | 
   3 | def hash_password(password: str):
   4 |     return bcrypt.hash(password[:72])
   5 | 
   6 | def verify_password(password: str, hashed: str):
   7 |     return bcrypt.verify(password[:72], hashed)
