 268 | // Manteniendo la lógica funcional original intacta
 269 | const fmoney = v => parseFloat(v||0).toLocaleString('es-PA', {
 270 |   minimumFractionDigits:2, maximumFractionDigits:2
 271 | });
 272 | const fdate = s => {
 273 |   if (!s) return '—';
 274 |   try {
 275 |     const [y,m,d] = String(s).split('T')[0].split('-');
 276 |     const months = ['Ene','Feb','Mar','Abr','May','Jun','Jul','Ago','Sep','Oct','Nov','Dic'];
 277 |     return `${parseInt(d)} ${months[parseInt(m)-1]} ${y}`;
 278 |   } catch { return s; }
 279 | };
 280 | 
 281 | (async () => {
 282 |   const params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
 283 |   const pid    = params.get('payment_id');
 284 |   if (!pid) { document.getElementById('loading').textContent = 'Error: No se encontró el ID de pago.'; return; }
 285 | 
 286 |   try {
 287 |     const token   = localStorage.getItem('access_token');
 288 |     const headers = token ? { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } : {};
 289 | 
 290 |     const [pay, detail] = await Promise.all([
 291 |       fetch(`/api/finance/payment/${pid}`,             { headers }).then(r => r.json()),
 292 |       fetch(`/api/finance/payment-detail-full/${pid}`, { headers }).then(r => r.ok ? r.json() : null),
 293 |     ]);
 294 | 
 295 |     const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString('es-PA', {
 296 |       year:'numeric', month:'long', day:'numeric'
 297 |     });
 298 | 
 299 |     // Actualizar nombre del PH si viene del API
 300 |     if(detail?.property_name) {
 301 |         document.getElementById('display-property-name').textContent = detail.property_name.toUpperCase();
 302 |     }
 303 | 
 304 |     // Referencias
 305 |     let refHtml = '';
 306 |     if (detail?.invoice_number)       refHtml += `N° Sistema: ${detail.invoice_number} | `;
 307 |     if (detail?.fiscal_invoice_number) refHtml += `N° Fiscal: ${detail.fiscal_invoice_number}`;
 308 |     document.getElementById('inv-ref-num').innerHTML = refHtml || `ID Pago: #${pid}`;
 309 | 
 310 |     // Propietario
 311 |     document.getElementById('inv-owner').innerHTML =
 312 |       `${detail?.owner_name || '—'}
 313 |        <span class="sub-value">Unidad: ${detail?.unit_number || '—'}</span>`;
 314 | 
 315 |     // Datos del pago
 316 |     document.getElementById('inv-pay-info').innerHTML =
 317 |       `Fecha: ${fdate(detail?.payment_date || pay?.payment_date)}
 318 |        ${detail?.reference ? `<span class="sub-value">Ref: ${detail.reference}</span>` : ''}`;
 319 | 
 320 |     // Tabla de cargos
 321 |     const tbody = document.getElementById('inv-tbody');
 322 |     const apps  = pay?.applications || [];
 323 | 
 324 |     if (!apps.length) {
 325 |       tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="3" style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:#999;">Sin detalles de aplicación disponibles.</td></tr>`;
 326 |     } else {
 327 |       apps.forEach((a, i) => {
 328 |         tbody.innerHTML += `
 329 |           <tr>
 330 |             <td class="td-num">${i+1}</td>
 331 |             <td>${a.description || `Aplicación de cargo #${a.charge_id}`}</td>
 332 |             <td class="td-price">$${fmoney(a.applied_amount)}</td>
 333 |           </tr>`;
 334 |       });
 335 |     }
 336 | 
 337 |     document.getElementById('inv-total').textContent = `$${fmoney(pay?.amount || 0)}`;
 338 |     document.getElementById('inv-date').textContent  = today;
 339 | 
 340 |     document.getElementById('loading').style.display  = 'none';
 341 |     document.getElementById('inv-page').style.display = 'block';
 342 | 
 343 |   } catch(e) {
 344 |     document.getElementById('loading').textContent = `Error crítico: ${e.message}`;
 345 |   }
 346 | })();
 347 | </script>
 348 | </body>
 349 | </html>

 360 | // ── Verificar acceso admin ───────────────────────────────

 371 | // ── Descripción dinámica del rol ─────────────────────────
 372 | function updateRoleDescription() {
 373 |   const role = document.getElementById('new-role').value;
 374 |   const desc = document.getElementById('role-desc');
 375 |   const texts = {
 376 |     'USER':   '<strong>Rol Usuario:</strong> puede registrar pagos, crear cargos, propietarios y propiedades, pero <strong>no puede eliminar ni editar</strong> pagos o cargos existentes.',
 377 |     'ADMIN':  '<strong>Rol Administrador:</strong> acceso total, incluyendo eliminar y editar pagos, cargos y usuarios.',
 378 |     'GARITA': '<strong>Rol Garita:</strong> acceso <strong>exclusivo al módulo de Control de Garita</strong>. Solo puede registrar visitas, ver historial y gestionar pre-registros. No tiene acceso a finanzas, propietarios ni administración.',
 379 |   };
 380 |   desc.innerHTML = texts[role] || '';
 381 | }

 383 | // ── Estado global ────────────────────────────────────────
 384 | let allPayments = [];
 385 | let allCharges  = [];
 386 | let allOwners   = [];
 387 | let allUnits    = [];
 388 | let editingPwdUserId = null;

 390 | // ── Tabs ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
 391 | function switchTab(tab) {
 392 |   document.querySelectorAll('.adm-tab').forEach((b, i) => {
 393 |     const ids = ['usuarios','pagos','cargos'];
 394 |     b.classList.toggle('active', ids[i] === tab);
 395 |   });
 396 |   document.querySelectorAll('.adm-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
 397 |   document.getElementById(`panel-${tab}`).classList.add('active');
 398 | 
 399 |   if (tab === 'pagos')  loadPayments();
 400 |   if (tab === 'cargos') loadCharges();
 401 | }
 402 | 
 403 | // ── Init ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
 404 | async function initAdmin() {
 405 |   const [owners, units] = await Promise.all([
 406 |     apiRequest('/owners'),
 407 |     apiRequest('/units'),
 408 |   ]);
 409 |   allOwners = owners || [];
 410 |   allUnits  = units  || [];
 411 | 
 412 |   // Llenar filtros de pagos
 413 |   const pfOwner = document.getElementById('pf-owner');
 414 |   const cfOwner = document.getElementById('cf-owner');
 415 |   allOwners.forEach(o => {
 416 |     pfOwner.innerHTML += `<option value="${o.id}">${o.full_name}</option>`;
 417 |     cfOwner.innerHTML += `<option value="${o.id}">${o.full_name}</option>`;
 418 |   });
 419 | 
 420 |   // Llenar filtros de unidad
 421 |   const pfUnit = document.getElementById('pf-unit');
 422 |   const cfUnit = document.getElementById('cf-unit');
 423 |   allUnits.forEach(u => {
 424 |     pfUnit.innerHTML += `<option value="${u.unit_number}">Apt. ${u.unit_number}</option>`;
 425 |     cfUnit.innerHTML += `<option value="${u.unit_number}">Apt. ${u.unit_number}</option>`;
 426 |   });
 427 | 
 428 |   loadUsers();
 429 | }
 430 | 
 431 | // ══ USUARIOS ════════════════════════════════════════════
 432 | 
 433 | async function loadUsers() {
 434 |   const users = await apiRequest('/auth/users') || [];
 435 |   document.getElementById('users-count').textContent = users.length;
 436 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('users-tbody');
 437 |   if (!users.length) {
 438 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="4" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin usuarios</td></tr>`;
 439 |     return;
 440 |   }
 441 |   tbody.innerHTML = users.map(u => `
 442 |     <tr>
 443 |       <td><strong>${u.username}</strong></td>
 444 |       <td><span class="role-badge role-${u.role}">${u.role}</span></td>
 445 |       <td>
 446 |         <span class="${u.is_active ? 'active-dot' : 'inactive-dot'}"></span>
 447 |         ${u.is_active ? 'Activo' : 'Inactivo'}
 448 |       </td>
 449 |       <td>
 450 |         <div class="action-btns">
 451 |           <button class="btn-edit" onclick="openPwdModal(${u.id}, '${u.username}')">
 452 |             <i class="fas fa-key"></i> Clave
 453 |           </button>
 454 |           <button class="btn-edit" onclick="toggleUser(${u.id})" title="${u.is_active ? 'Desactivar' : 'Activar'}">
 455 |             <i class="fas fa-${u.is_active ? 'ban' : 'check'}"></i>
 456 |           </button>
 457 |           <button class="btn-del" onclick="deleteUser(${u.id}, '${u.username}')">
 458 |             <i class="fas fa-trash"></i>
 459 |           </button>
 460 |         </div>
 461 |       </td>
 462 |     </tr>`).join('');
 463 | }
 464 | 
 465 | async function createUser() {
 466 |   const username = document.getElementById('new-username').value.trim();
 467 |   const password = document.getElementById('new-password').value;
 468 |   const role     = document.getElementById('new-role').value;
 469 |   if (!username || !password) { showToast('Completa todos los campos', 'error'); return; }
 470 |   if (password.length < 6) { showToast('La contraseña debe tener al menos 6 caracteres', 'error'); return; }
 471 |   const r = await apiRequest('/auth/users', 'POST', { username, password, role });
 472 |   if (r) {
 473 |     showToast(`Usuario "${username}" creado con rol ${role}`, 'success');
 474 |     document.getElementById('new-username').value = '';
 475 |     document.getElementById('new-password').value = '';
 476 |     loadUsers();
 477 |   }
 478 | }
 479 | 
 480 | async function toggleUser(id) {
 481 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/auth/users/${id}/toggle`, 'PATCH');
 482 |   if (r) { showToast('Estado actualizado'); loadUsers(); }
 483 | }
 484 | 
 485 | async function deleteUser(id, username) {
 486 |   if (!confirm(`¿Eliminar el usuario "${username}"? Esta acción no se puede deshacer.`)) return;
 487 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/auth/users/${id}`, 'DELETE');
 488 |   if (r) { showToast(`Usuario "${username}" eliminado`); loadUsers(); }
 489 | }
 490 | 
 491 | function openPwdModal(id, username) {
 492 |   editingPwdUserId = id;
 493 |   document.getElementById('pwd-modal-user').textContent = username;
 494 |   document.getElementById('modal-new-pwd').value = '';
 495 |   document.getElementById('pwd-modal').classList.add('open');
 496 | }
 497 | function closePwdModal() { document.getElementById('pwd-modal').classList.remove('open'); }
 498 | 
 499 | async function confirmPwdChange() {
 500 |   const pwd = document.getElementById('modal-new-pwd').value;
 501 |   if (!pwd || pwd.length < 6) { showToast('Mínimo 6 caracteres', 'error'); return; }
 502 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/auth/users/${editingPwdUserId}/password`, 'PATCH', { new_password: pwd });
 503 |   if (r) { showToast('Contraseña actualizada', 'success'); closePwdModal(); }
 504 | }
 505 | 
 506 | // ══ PAGOS ════════════════════════════════════════════════
 507 | 
 508 | async function loadPayments() {
 509 |   const data = await apiRequest('/finance/all-payments') || [];
 510 |   allPayments = data;
 511 |   document.getElementById('payments-count').textContent = data.length;
 512 |   filterPayments();
 513 | }
 514 | 
 515 | function filterPayments() {
 516 |   const ownerId = document.getElementById('pf-owner').value;
 517 |   const unitNum = document.getElementById('pf-unit').value;
 518 |   const search  = document.getElementById('pf-search').value.toLowerCase();
 519 | 
 520 |   const filtered = allPayments.filter(p => {
 521 |     if (ownerId && String(p.owner_id || '') !== ownerId) return false;
 522 |     if (unitNum && p.unit_number !== unitNum) return false;
 523 |     if (search) {
 524 |       const hay = `${p.invoice_number || ''} ${p.reference || ''} ${p.owner_name || ''} ${p.receipt_number || ''}`.toLowerCase();
 525 |       if (!hay.includes(search)) return false;
 526 |     }
 527 |     return true;
 528 |   });
 529 | 
 530 |   renderPayments(filtered);
 531 | }
 532 | 
 533 | function renderPayments(list) {
 534 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('payments-tbody');
 535 |   if (!list.length) {
 536 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin resultados</td></tr>`;
 537 |     return;
 538 |   }
 539 |   tbody.innerHTML = list.map(p => `
 540 |     <tr>
 541 |       <td class="td-mono">${p.payment_id}</td>
 542 |       <td>${formatDate(p.fecha)}</td>
 543 |       <td>${p.owner_name}</td>
 544 |       <td>${p.unit_number}</td>
 545 |       <td style="max-width:180px;font-size:.8rem;color:var(--text-secondary);">
 546 |         ${(p.cargos || []).map(c => c.description).join(', ') || '—'}
 547 |       </td>
 548 |       <td class="td-right"><strong>$${formatMoney(p.amount)}</strong></td>
 549 |       <td style="font-size:.8rem;">
 550 |         ${p.invoice_number ? `<span class="badge badge-primary">${p.invoice_number}</span>` : '<span style="color:var(--text-muted);">—</span>'}
 551 |         ${p.tiene_factura ? `<br><a href="/static/factura.html?payment_id=${p.payment_id}" target="_blank" style="font-size:.72rem;color:var(--accent);">ver factura</a>` : ''}
 552 |       </td>
 553 |       <td>
 554 |         <div class="action-btns">
 555 |           <button class="btn-edit" onclick="openEditPayment(${p.payment_id}, '${p.fecha}', ${p.amount}, '${p.invoice_number||''}', '${p.reference||''}', '${p.receipt_number||''}')">
 556 |             <i class="fas fa-edit"></i>
 557 |           </button>
 558 |           <button class="btn-del" onclick="deletePayment(${p.payment_id})">
 559 |             <i class="fas fa-trash"></i>
 560 |           </button>
 561 |         </div>
 562 |       </td>
 563 |     </tr>`).join('');
 564 | }
 565 | 
 566 | function clearPaymentFilters() {
 567 |   ['pf-owner','pf-unit','pf-search'].forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value = '');
 568 |   filterPayments();
 569 | }
 570 | 
 571 | function openEditPayment(id, fecha, amount, invoice, ref, receipt) {
 572 |   document.getElementById('edit-pay-id').value      = id;
 573 |   document.getElementById('edit-pay-date').value    = fecha;
 574 |   document.getElementById('edit-pay-amount').value  = amount;
 575 |   document.getElementById('edit-pay-invoice').value = invoice;
 576 |   document.getElementById('edit-pay-ref').value     = ref;
 577 |   document.getElementById('edit-pay-receipt').value = receipt;
 578 |   document.getElementById('edit-payment-modal').classList.add('open');
 579 | }
 580 | function closeEditPayment() { document.getElementById('edit-payment-modal').classList.remove('open'); }
 581 | 
 582 | async function confirmEditPayment() {
 583 |   const id      = document.getElementById('edit-pay-id').value;
 584 |   const fecha   = document.getElementById('edit-pay-date').value;
 585 |   const amount  = parseFloat(document.getElementById('edit-pay-amount').value);
 586 |   const invoice = document.getElementById('edit-pay-invoice').value.trim() || null;
 587 |   const ref     = document.getElementById('edit-pay-ref').value.trim() || null;
 588 |   const receipt = document.getElementById('edit-pay-receipt').value.trim() || null;
 589 |   if (!fecha || !amount) { showToast('Fecha y monto son obligatorios', 'error'); return; }
 590 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/finance/payment/${id}`, 'PUT', {
 591 |     payment_date: fecha, amount, invoice_number: invoice, reference: ref, receipt_number: receipt
 592 |   });
 593 |   if (r) { showToast('Pago actualizado', 'success'); closeEditPayment(); loadPayments(); }
 594 | }
 595 | 
 596 | async function deletePayment(id) {
 597 |   if (!confirm(`¿Eliminar el pago #${id}?\n\nEsto revertirá los saldos de los cargos vinculados y eliminará la factura asociada si existe.`)) return;
 598 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/finance/payment/${id}`, 'DELETE');
 599 |   if (r) { showToast('Pago eliminado y saldos revertidos', 'success'); loadPayments(); }
 600 | }
 601 | 
 602 | // ══ CARGOS ═══════════════════════════════════════════════
 603 | 
 604 | async function loadCharges() {
 605 |   const data = await apiRequest('/finance/charges') || [];
 606 |   allCharges = data;
 607 |   document.getElementById('charges-count').textContent = data.length;
 608 |   filterCharges();
 609 | }
 610 | 
 611 | function filterCharges() {
 612 |   const status  = document.getElementById('cf-status').value;
 613 |   const ownerId = document.getElementById('cf-owner').value;
 614 |   const unitNum = document.getElementById('cf-unit').value;
 615 |   const desc    = document.getElementById('cf-desc').value.toLowerCase();
 616 | 
 617 |   const filtered = allCharges.filter(c => {
 618 |     if (status  && c.status !== status) return false;
 619 |     if (ownerId && String(c.owner_id || '') !== ownerId) return false;
 620 |     if (unitNum && c.unit_number !== unitNum) return false;
 621 |     if (desc    && !c.description.toLowerCase().includes(desc)) return false;
 622 |     return true;
 623 |   });
 624 | 
 625 |   renderCharges(filtered);
 626 | }
 627 | 
 628 | function renderCharges(list) {
 629 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('charges-tbody');
 630 |   if (!list.length) {
 631 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin resultados</td></tr>`;
 632 |     return;
 633 |   }
 634 |   tbody.innerHTML = list.map(c => `
 635 |     <tr>
 636 |       <td>${c.owner_name || '—'}</td>
 637 |       <td>${c.unit_number || '—'}</td>
 638 |       <td>${c.description}</td>
 639 |       <td>${formatDate(c.due_date)}</td>
 640 |       <td class="td-right">$${formatMoney(c.amount)}</td>
 641 |       <td class="td-right">$${formatMoney(c.balance)}</td>
 642 |       <td><span class="badge badge-${c.status}">${c.status}</span></td>
 643 |       <td>
 644 |         <div class="action-btns">
 645 |           <button class="btn-edit" onclick="openEditCharge(${c.id}, ${c.unit_id}, \`${c.description.replace(/`/g,"'")}\`, ${c.amount}, '${c.date_created}', '${c.due_date}')">
 646 |             <i class="fas fa-edit"></i>
 647 |           </button>
 648 |           <button class="btn-del" onclick="deleteCharge(${c.id}, \`${c.description.replace(/`/g,"'")}\`)">
 649 |             <i class="fas fa-trash"></i>
 650 |           </button>
 651 |         </div>
 652 |       </td>
 653 |     </tr>`).join('');
 654 | }
 655 | 
 656 | function clearChargeFilters() {
 657 |   ['cf-status','cf-owner','cf-unit','cf-desc'].forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value = '');
 658 |   filterCharges();
 659 | }
 660 | 
 661 | function openEditCharge(id, unitId, desc, amount, dateCreated, dueDate) {
 662 |   document.getElementById('edit-chg-id').value           = id;
 663 |   document.getElementById('edit-chg-unit-id').value      = unitId;
 664 |   document.getElementById('edit-chg-desc').value         = desc;
 665 |   document.getElementById('edit-chg-amount').value       = amount;
 666 |   document.getElementById('edit-chg-date-created').value = dateCreated;
 667 |   document.getElementById('edit-chg-due-date').value     = dueDate;
 668 |   document.getElementById('edit-charge-modal').classList.add('open');
 669 | }
 670 | function closeEditCharge() { document.getElementById('edit-charge-modal').classList.remove('open'); }
 671 | 
 672 | async function confirmEditCharge() {
 673 |   const id          = document.getElementById('edit-chg-id').value;
 674 |   const unitId      = document.getElementById('edit-chg-unit-id').value;
 675 |   const desc        = document.getElementById('edit-chg-desc').value.trim();
 676 |   const amount      = parseFloat(document.getElementById('edit-chg-amount').value);
 677 |   const dateCreated = document.getElementById('edit-chg-date-created').value;
 678 |   const dueDate     = document.getElementById('edit-chg-due-date').value;
 679 |   if (!desc || !amount || !dateCreated || !dueDate) { showToast('Completa todos los campos', 'error'); return; }
 680 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/charges/${id}`, 'PUT', {
 681 |     unit_id: parseInt(unitId), description: desc, amount, date_created: dateCreated, due_date: dueDate
 682 |   });
 683 |   if (r) { showToast('Cargo actualizado'); closeEditCharge(); loadCharges(); }
 684 | }
 685 | 
 686 | async function deleteCharge(id, desc) {
 687 |   if (!confirm(`¿Eliminar el cargo "${desc}"?\n\nEsto eliminará también los registros de pago vinculados a este cargo.`)) return;
 688 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/charges/${id}`, 'DELETE');
 689 |   if (r) { showToast('Cargo eliminado', 'success'); loadCharges(); loadPayments(); }
 690 | }
 691 | 
 692 | // Cerrar modales al click fuera
 693 | ['pwd-modal','edit-payment-modal','edit-charge-modal'].forEach(id => {
 694 |   document.getElementById(id).addEventListener('click', function(e) {
 695 |     if (e.target === this) this.classList.remove('open');
 696 |   });
 697 | });
 698 | </script>
 699 | </body>
 700 | </html>

 156 |       <div class="cal-grid" id="cal-grid"></div>
 157 |     </div>
 158 |   </div>
 159 | 
 160 |   <!-- ══ TAB: LISTA ══ -->
 161 |   <div class="ag-panel" id="panel-lista">
 162 |     <div class="card" style="margin-bottom:0;">
 163 |       <div class="card-header">
 164 |         <h3><i class="fas fa-list-ul"></i> Todos los eventos</h3>
 165 |         <span class="badge badge-primary" id="ev-count">0</span>
 166 |       </div>
 167 |       <div class="card-body">
 168 |         <div class="filter-chips">
 169 |           <span class="filter-chip on" data-filter="ALL"    onclick="setFilter('ALL',this)">Todos</span>
 170 |           <span class="filter-chip"    data-filter="CITA"   onclick="setFilter('CITA',this)">🗓 Citas</span>
 171 |           <span class="filter-chip"    data-filter="EVENTO" onclick="setFilter('EVENTO',this)">🏛 Eventos</span>
 172 |           <span class="filter-chip"    data-filter="TAREA"  onclick="setFilter('TAREA',this)">✅ Tareas</span>
 173 |           <span class="filter-chip"    data-filter="PENDIENTE" onclick="setFilter('PENDIENTE',this)">Pendientes</span>
 174 |         </div>
 175 |         <div id="ev-list">
 176 |           <div style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Cargando...</div>
 177 |         </div>

 183 |   <div class="ag-panel" id="panel-nuevo">
 184 |     <div style="max-width:560px;">
 185 |       <div class="card">
 186 |         <div class="card-header">
 187 |           <h3><i class="fas fa-plus-circle"></i> <span id="ev-form-title">Nuevo Evento</span></h3>
 188 |           <button class="btn btn-muted btn-sm" id="ev-btn-cancel" onclick="cancelEvEdit()" style="display:none;">
 189 |             <i class="fas fa-times"></i> Cancelar
 190 |           </button>

 192 |         <div class="card-body">
 193 |           <input type="hidden" id="ev-id">

 209 |             <div>

 212 |             </div>

 214 |               <label class="field-label">Hora</label>

 216 |             </div>
 217 |           </div>

 219 |           <label class="field-label">Lugar / Ubicación</label>
 220 |           <input type="text" id="ev-location" placeholder="Ej: Salón comunal, Piso 1">
 221 | 
 222 |           <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:12px;">
 223 |             <div>
 224 |               <label class="field-label">Prioridad</label>
 225 |               <select id="ev-priority">
 226 |                 <option value="NORMAL">Normal</option>
 227 |                 <option value="ALTA">Alta</option>
 228 |                 <option value="BAJA">Baja</option>
 229 |               </select>

 232 |               <label class="field-label">Estado</label>
 233 |               <select id="ev-status">
 234 |                 <option value="PENDIENTE">Pendiente</option>
 235 |                 <option value="COMPLETADO">Completado</option>
 236 |                 <option value="CANCELADO">Cancelado</option>
 237 |               </select>
 238 |             </div>

 242 |             <i class="fas fa-save"></i> <span id="ev-btn-label">Guardar Evento</span>

 249 | </div><!-- /app -->

 251 | <div id="notification"></div>
 252 | <script src="js/main.js"></script>
 253 | <script>
 254 | renderHeader('agenda');
 255 | 
 256 | let allEvents  = [];
 257 | let evEditingId = null;
 258 | let calYear, calMonth;
 259 | let activeFilter = 'ALL';
 260 | 
 261 | const TYPE_ICONS = { CITA:'fa-handshake', EVENTO:'fa-landmark', TAREA:'fa-check-square' };
 262 | 
 263 | // ── Init ─────────────────────────────────────
 264 | async function init() {
 265 |   const now = new Date();
 266 |   calYear  = now.getFullYear();
 267 |   calMonth = now.getMonth();
 268 |   document.getElementById('ev-date').value = todayISO();
 269 |   await loadEvents();
 270 | }
 271 | 
 272 | // ── Tabs ──────────────────────────────────────
 273 | function switchTab(tab) {
 274 |   document.querySelectorAll('.ag-tab').forEach((b,i) => {
 275 |     b.classList.toggle('active', ['calendario','lista','nuevo'][i] === tab);
 276 |   });
 277 |   document.querySelectorAll('.ag-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
 278 |   document.getElementById('panel-' + tab).classList.add('active');
 279 | }
 280 | 
 281 | // ── Cargar eventos ────────────────────────────
 282 | async function loadEvents() {
 283 |   allEvents = await apiRequest('/agenda') || [];
 284 |   renderCalendar();
 285 |   renderList();
 286 | }
 287 | 
 288 | // ── Filtro lista ──────────────────────────────
 289 | function setFilter(f, el) {
 290 |   activeFilter = f;
 291 |   document.querySelectorAll('.filter-chip').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('on'));
 292 |   el.classList.add('on');
 293 |   renderList();
 294 | }
 295 | 
 296 | function renderList() {
 297 |   let list = allEvents;
 298 |   if (activeFilter !== 'ALL') {
 299 |     if (['CITA','EVENTO','TAREA'].includes(activeFilter))
 300 |       list = list.filter(e => e.event_type === activeFilter);
 301 |     else
 302 |       list = list.filter(e => e.status === activeFilter);
 303 |   }
 304 | 
 305 |   document.getElementById('ev-count').textContent = list.length;
 306 |   const container = document.getElementById('ev-list');
 307 | 
 308 |   if (!list.length) {
 309 |     container.innerHTML = `<div style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 310 |       <i class="fas fa-calendar-times" style="font-size:2rem;opacity:.3;display:block;margin-bottom:.5rem;"></i>
 311 |       Sin eventos que mostrar</div>`;
 312 |     return;
 313 |   }
 314 | 
 315 |   // Agrupar por fecha
 316 |   const grouped = {};
 317 |   list.forEach(e => {
 318 |     const key = e.event_date;
 319 |     if (!grouped[key]) grouped[key] = [];
 320 |     grouped[key].push(e);
 321 |   });
 322 | 
 323 |   container.innerHTML = Object.keys(grouped).sort().map(dateKey => {
 324 |     const d = new Date(dateKey + 'T00:00:00');
 325 |     const label = d.toLocaleDateString('es-PA', { weekday:'long', year:'numeric', month:'long', day:'numeric' });
 326 |     return `
 327 |       <div style="font-size:.72rem;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.06em;
 328 |         color:var(--text-muted);padding:6px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);margin:12px 0 8px;">
 329 |         ${label}
 330 |       </div>
 331 |       ${grouped[dateKey].map(e => `
 332 |         <div class="event-card priority-${e.priority}">
 333 |           <div class="event-type-icon icon-${e.event_type}">
 334 |             <i class="fas ${TYPE_ICONS[e.event_type]}"></i>
 335 |           </div>
 336 |           <div class="event-info">
 337 |             <strong>${e.title}</strong>
 338 |             <div class="event-meta">
 339 |               ${e.event_time ? `<i class="fas fa-clock" style="opacity:.5;"></i> ${e.event_time} &nbsp;` : ''}
 340 |               ${e.location ? `<i class="fas fa-map-marker-alt" style="opacity:.5;"></i> ${e.location} &nbsp;` : ''}
 341 |               ${e.description ? `<span style="opacity:.7;">${e.description}</span>` : ''}
 342 |             </div>
 343 |           </div>
 344 |           <div class="event-actions">
 345 |             <span class="status-chip chip-${e.status}">${e.status}</span>
 346 |             ${e.status === 'PENDIENTE' ? `
 347 |               <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" title="Marcar completado"
 348 |                 onclick="markDone(${e.id})" style="color:var(--success);">
 349 |                 <i class="fas fa-check"></i>
 350 |               </button>` : ''}
 351 |             <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="editEvent(${e.id})" title="Editar">
 352 |               <i class="fas fa-pencil-alt"></i>
 353 |             </button>
 354 |             <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="deleteEvent(${e.id})" title="Eliminar">
 355 |               <i class="fas fa-trash" style="color:var(--danger);"></i>
 356 |             </button>
 357 |           </div>
 358 |         </div>`).join('')}`;
 359 |   }).join('');
 360 | }
 361 | 
 362 | // ── Calendario ────────────────────────────────
 363 | function prevMonth() { if (--calMonth < 0) { calMonth = 11; calYear--; } renderCalendar(); }
 364 | function nextMonth() { if (++calMonth > 11) { calMonth = 0;  calYear++; } renderCalendar(); }
 365 | 
 366 | function renderCalendar() {
 367 |   const months = ['Enero','Febrero','Marzo','Abril','Mayo','Junio',
 368 |                   'Julio','Agosto','Septiembre','Octubre','Noviembre','Diciembre'];
 369 |   document.getElementById('cal-title').textContent = `${months[calMonth]} ${calYear}`;
 370 | 
 371 |   const firstDay = new Date(calYear, calMonth, 1).getDay();
 372 |   const daysInMonth = new Date(calYear, calMonth + 1, 0).getDate();
 373 |   const daysInPrev  = new Date(calYear, calMonth, 0).getDate();
 374 |   const today = todayISO();
 375 | 
 376 |   // Indexar eventos del mes
 377 |   const evMap = {};
 378 |   allEvents.forEach(e => {
 379 |     const [y, m] = e.event_date.split('-').map(Number);
 380 |     if (y === calYear && m - 1 === calMonth) {
 381 |       const d = parseInt(e.event_date.split('-')[2]);
 382 |       if (!evMap[d]) evMap[d] = [];
 383 |       evMap[d].push(e);
 384 |     }
 385 |   });
 386 | 
 387 |   let html = '';
 388 |   let day = 1;
 389 | 
 390 |   // Días del mes anterior
 391 |   for (let i = 0; i < firstDay; i++) {
 392 |     html += `<div class="cal-day other-month">
 393 |       <div class="day-num">${daysInPrev - firstDay + i + 1}</div></div>`;
 394 |   }
 395 |   // Días del mes actual
 396 |   for (let d = 1; d <= daysInMonth; d++) {
 397 |     const dateStr = `${calYear}-${String(calMonth+1).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(d).padStart(2,'0')}`;
 398 |     const isToday = dateStr === today;
 399 |     const evs = evMap[d] || [];
 400 |     html += `<div class="cal-day${isToday ? ' today' : ''}" onclick="openDayModal('${dateStr}')">
 401 |       <div class="day-num">${isToday ? `<span style="background:var(--accent);color:#fff;width:22px;height:22px;border-radius:50%;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;">${d}</span>` : d}</div>
 402 |       <div class="day-events">
 403 |         ${evs.slice(0, 3).map(e => `
 404 |           <div class="day-event-dot dot-${e.event_type} ${e.status!=='PENDIENTE'?'dot-done':''}"
 405 |             onclick="event.stopPropagation();editEvent(${e.id})">
 406 |             ${e.title}
 407 |           </div>`).join('')}
 408 |         ${evs.length > 3 ? `<div style="font-size:.65rem;color:var(--text-muted);padding:0 2px;">+${evs.length-3} más</div>` : ''}
 409 |       </div>
 410 |     </div>`;
 411 |   }
 412 |   // Días del mes siguiente
 413 |   const remaining = 42 - firstDay - daysInMonth;
 414 |   for (let i = 1; i <= remaining; i++) {
 415 |     html += `<div class="cal-day other-month"><div class="day-num">${i}</div></div>`;
 416 |   }
 417 | 
 418 |   document.getElementById('cal-grid').innerHTML = html;
 419 | }
 420 | 
 421 | function openDayModal(dateStr) {
 422 |   document.getElementById('ev-date').value = dateStr;
 423 |   switchTab('nuevo');
 424 | }
 425 | 
 426 | // ── Guardar evento ────────────────────────────
 427 | async function saveEvent() {
 428 |   const title = document.getElementById('ev-title').value.trim();
 429 |   const dt    = document.getElementById('ev-date').value;
 430 |   if (!title || !dt) { showToast('Título y fecha son obligatorios', 'error'); return; }
 431 | 
 432 |   const time = document.getElementById('ev-time').value;
 433 |   const data = {
 434 |     title,
 435 |     description: document.getElementById('ev-desc').value.trim()     || null,
 436 |     event_type:  document.getElementById('ev-type').value,
 437 |     event_date:  dt,
 438 |     event_time:  time || null,
 439 |     location:    document.getElementById('ev-location').value.trim() || null,
 440 |     priority:    document.getElementById('ev-priority').value,
 441 |     status:      document.getElementById('ev-status').value,
 442 |   };
 443 | 
 444 |   let r;
 445 |   if (evEditingId) {
 446 |     r = await apiRequest(`/agenda/${evEditingId}`, 'PUT', data);
 447 |     if (r) showToast('Evento actualizado');
 448 |   } else {
 449 |     r = await apiRequest('/agenda/', 'POST', data);
 450 |     if (r) showToast('Evento guardado');
 451 |   }
 452 |   if (r) { cancelEvEdit(); loadEvents(); switchTab('calendario'); }
 453 | }
 454 | 
 455 | function editEvent(id) {
 456 |   const e = allEvents.find(x => x.id === id);
 457 |   if (!e) return;
 458 |   evEditingId = id;
 459 |   document.getElementById('ev-id').value            = id;
 460 |   document.getElementById('ev-type').value          = e.event_type;
 461 |   document.getElementById('ev-title').value         = e.title;
 462 |   document.getElementById('ev-desc').value          = e.description || '';
 463 |   document.getElementById('ev-date').value          = e.event_date;
 464 |   document.getElementById('ev-time').value          = e.event_time || '';
 465 |   document.getElementById('ev-location').value      = e.location || '';
 466 |   document.getElementById('ev-priority').value      = e.priority;
 467 |   document.getElementById('ev-status').value        = e.status;
 468 |   document.getElementById('ev-form-title').textContent = 'Editar Evento';
 469 |   document.getElementById('ev-btn-label').textContent  = 'Actualizar';
 470 |   document.getElementById('ev-btn-cancel').style.display = '';
 471 |   switchTab('nuevo');
 472 | }
 473 | 
 474 | function cancelEvEdit() {
 475 |   evEditingId = null;
 476 |   ['ev-id','ev-title','ev-desc','ev-time','ev-location'].forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value = '');
 477 |   document.getElementById('ev-type').value     = 'CITA';
 478 |   document.getElementById('ev-priority').value = 'NORMAL';
 479 |   document.getElementById('ev-status').value   = 'PENDIENTE';
 480 |   document.getElementById('ev-date').value     = todayISO();
 481 |   document.getElementById('ev-form-title').textContent = 'Nuevo Evento';
 482 |   document.getElementById('ev-btn-label').textContent  = 'Guardar Evento';
 483 |   document.getElementById('ev-btn-cancel').style.display = 'none';
 484 | }
 485 | 
 486 | async function markDone(id) {
 487 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/agenda/${id}/status?status=COMPLETADO`, 'PATCH');
 488 |   if (r) { showToast('Marcado como completado', 'success'); loadEvents(); }
 489 | }
 490 | 
 491 | async function deleteEvent(id) {
 492 |   if (!confirm('¿Eliminar este evento?')) return;
 493 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/agenda/${id}`, 'DELETE');
 494 |   if (r) { showToast('Evento eliminado'); loadEvents(); }
 495 | }
 496 | 
 497 | init();
 498 | </script>
 499 | </body>
 500 | </html>
 501 |

 315 | <script>
 316 | const fmoney = v => parseFloat(v||0).toLocaleString('es-PA',{minimumFractionDigits:2});
 317 | const fdate = s => s ? new Date(s).toLocaleDateString('es-PA') : '—';
 318 | 
 319 | (async () => {
 320 | 
 321 | const params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
 322 | const ownerId = params.get('owner_id');
 323 | 
 324 | const data = await fetch(`/api/finance/owner-statement-detailed/${ownerId}`).then(r=>r.json());
 325 | 
 326 | document.getElementById('stmt-date').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('es-PA');
 327 | 
 328 | document.getElementById('s-owner').textContent = data.owner_name;
 329 | document.getElementById('s-unit').textContent = data.unit_number;
 330 | document.getElementById('s-prop').textContent = data.property_name;
 331 | document.getElementById('stmt-prop-addr').textContent = data.property_address;
 332 | 
 333 | let t=0,p=0,b=0;
 334 | 
 335 | data.statement.forEach(c=>{
 336 |   t+=c.amount;
 337 |   p+=c.paid;
 338 |   b+=c.balance;
 339 | 
 340 |   const fechaPago = c.payments?.length ? fdate(c.payments[0].payment_date) : '—';
 341 | 
 342 |   document.getElementById('stmt-tbody').innerHTML+=`
 343 |     <tr>
 344 |       <td class="b">${c.description}</td>
 345 |       <td class="muted">${fechaPago}</td>
 346 |       <td class="r">$${fmoney(c.amount)}</td>
 347 |       <td class="r">$${fmoney(c.paid)}</td>
 348 |       <td class="r b">$${fmoney(c.balance)}</td>
 349 |     </tr>
 350 |   `;
 351 | });
 352 | 
 353 | document.getElementById('sum-total').textContent="$"+fmoney(t);
 354 | document.getElementById('sum-paid').textContent="$"+fmoney(p);
 355 | document.getElementById('sum-pend').textContent="$"+fmoney(b);
 356 | 
 357 | document.getElementById('loading').style.display='none';
 358 | document.getElementById('stmt-page').style.display='block';
 359 | 
 360 | })();
 361 | </script>

 225 | <script>
 226 | const fmoney = v => parseFloat(v||0).toLocaleString('es-PA', {
 227 |   minimumFractionDigits:2, maximumFractionDigits:2
 228 | });
 229 | const fdate = s => {
 230 |   if (!s) return '—';
 231 |   try {
 232 |     const [y,m,d] = String(s).split('T')[0].split('-');
 233 |     const months = ['ene','feb','mar','abr','may','jun','jul','ago','sep','oct','nov','dic'];
 234 |     return `${parseInt(d)} ${months[parseInt(m)-1]} ${y}`;
 235 |   } catch { return s; }
 236 | };
 237 | 
 238 | (async () => {
 239 |   const params = new URLSearchParams(location.search);
 240 |   const pid    = params.get('payment_id');
 241 |   if (!pid) { document.getElementById('loading').textContent = 'No se especificó un pago.'; return; }
 242 | 
 243 |   try {
 244 |     const token   = localStorage.getItem('access_token');
 245 |     const headers = token ? { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } : {};
 246 | 
 247 |     const [pay, detail] = await Promise.all([
 248 |       fetch(`/api/finance/payment/${pid}`,             { headers }).then(r => r.json()),
 249 |       fetch(`/api/finance/payment-detail-full/${pid}`, { headers }).then(r => r.ok ? r.json() : null),
 250 |     ]);
 251 | 
 252 |     // Logo
 253 |     const logoEl = document.getElementById('inv-logo');
 254 |     const img    = new Image();
 255 |     img.onload   = () => { logoEl.innerHTML = `<img src="/static/logo.png" alt="Logo">`; };
 256 |     img.src      = '/static/logo.png';
 257 | 
 258 |     const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString('es-PA', {
 259 |       year:'numeric', month:'long', day:'numeric'
 260 |     });
 261 | 
 262 |     // Referencia
 263 |     let refHtml = '';
 264 |     if (detail?.invoice_number)       refHtml += `N° Sistema: ${detail.invoice_number}<br>`;
 265 |     if (detail?.fiscal_invoice_number) refHtml += `N° Fiscal: ${detail.fiscal_invoice_number}`;
 266 |     document.getElementById('inv-ref-num').innerHTML = refHtml || `Pago #${pid}`;
 267 | 
 268 |     // Propietario
 269 |     document.getElementById('inv-owner').innerHTML =
 270 |       `${detail?.owner_name || '—'}
 271 |        <small>Unidad: ${detail?.unit_number || '—'}</small>
 272 |        <small>Propiedad: ${detail?.property_name || '—'}</small>`;
 273 | 
 274 |     // Datos del pago
 275 |     document.getElementById('inv-pay-info').innerHTML =
 276 |       `Fecha: ${fdate(detail?.payment_date || pay?.payment_date)}
 277 |        ${detail?.reference ? `<small>Referencia: ${detail.reference}</small>` : ''}`;
 278 | 
 279 |     // Tabla de cargos
 280 |     const tbody = document.getElementById('inv-tbody');
 281 |     const apps  = pay?.applications || [];
 282 | 
 283 |     if (!apps.length) {
 284 |       tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="3" style="text-align:center;padding:16px;color:#bbb;">Sin detalle disponible</td></tr>`;
 285 |     } else {
 286 |       apps.forEach((a, i) => {
 287 |         tbody.innerHTML += `
 288 |           <tr>
 289 |             <td class="muted">${i+1}</td>
 290 |             <td>${a.description || `Cargo #${a.charge_id}`}</td>
 291 |             <td class="r">$${fmoney(a.applied_amount)}</td>
 292 |           </tr>`;
 293 |       });
 294 |     }
 295 | 
 296 |     document.getElementById('inv-total').textContent = `$${fmoney(pay?.amount || 0)}`;
 297 |     document.getElementById('inv-date').textContent  = today;
 298 | 
 299 |     document.getElementById('loading').style.display  = 'none';
 300 |     document.getElementById('inv-page').style.display = 'block';
 301 | 
 302 |   } catch(e) {
 303 |     document.getElementById('loading').textContent = `Error: ${e.message}`;
 304 |   }
 305 | })();
 306 | </script>
 307 | </body>
 308 | </html>
 309 |

 445 | <div id="notification"></div>
 446 | <script src="js/main.js"></script>
 447 | <script>
 448 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 449 | // ESTADO GLOBAL
 450 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 451 | let mode          = 'owner';
 452 | let activeOwnerId = null;
 453 | let lastPaymentId = null;
 454 | let allChargesCache = [];
 455 | let allPropsCache   = [];
 456 | let allUnitsCache   = [];
 457 | 
 458 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 459 | // INIT
 460 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 461 | async function init() {
 462 |   
 463 | 
 464 |   const [props, owners, units] = await Promise.all([
 465 |     apiRequest('/properties'),
 466 |     apiRequest('/owners'),
 467 |     apiRequest('/units'),
 468 |   ]);
 469 | 
 470 |   allPropsCache = props  || [];
 471 |   allUnitsCache = units  || [];
 472 | 
 473 |   // Owner select (pago)
 474 |   const ownerSel = document.getElementById('owner-select');
 475 |   (owners || []).forEach(o =>
 476 |     ownerSel.innerHTML += `<option value="${o.id}">${o.full_name}</option>`);
 477 |   ownerSel.addEventListener('change', () => {
 478 |     const id = parseInt(ownerSel.value);
 479 |     if (!id) { resetPayForm(); return; }
 480 |     activeOwnerId = id;
 481 |     document.getElementById('post-pay-panel').style.display = 'none';
 482 |     loadOwnerCharges(id);
 483 |   });
 484 | 
 485 |   // Prop select (pago por unidad)
 486 |   const propPaySel = document.getElementById('prop-pay-select');
 487 |   allPropsCache.forEach(p =>
 488 |     propPaySel.innerHTML += `<option value="${p.id}">${p.name}</option>`);
 489 | 
 490 |   // Prop select (cargo)
 491 |   const chargePropSel = document.getElementById('charge-prop-select');
 492 |   allPropsCache.forEach(p =>
 493 |     chargePropSel.innerHTML += `<option value="${p.id}">${p.name}</option>`);
 494 | 
 495 |   // Estado de cuenta select
 496 |   const stmtSel = document.getElementById('stmt-select');
 497 |   (owners || []).forEach(o =>
 498 |     stmtSel.innerHTML += `<option value="${o.id}">${o.full_name}</option>`);
 499 | 
 500 |   // Fechas por defecto
 501 |   document.getElementById('charge-date').value = todayISO();
 502 | 
 503 |   // Cargar historial
 504 |   await loadChargesTable();
 505 | }
 506 | 
 507 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 508 | // TABS
 509 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 510 | function switchTab(tab) {
 511 |   document.querySelectorAll('.fin-tab').forEach((b, i) => {
 512 |     const ids = ['pagos','cargos','historial','estados'];
 513 |     b.classList.toggle('active', ids[i] === tab);
 514 |   });
 515 |   document.querySelectorAll('.fin-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
 516 |   document.getElementById(`panel-${tab}`).classList.add('active');
 517 | 
 518 |   if (tab === 'historial') loadChargesTable();
 519 | }
 520 | 
 521 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 522 | // TOGGLE MODO PAGO
 523 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 524 | function switchMode(m) {
 525 |   mode = m;
 526 |   activeOwnerId = null;
 527 |   document.getElementById('btn-owner').classList.toggle('active', m === 'owner');
 528 |   document.getElementById('btn-unit').classList.toggle('active',  m === 'unit');
 529 |   document.getElementById('panel-owner').style.display = m === 'owner' ? '' : 'none';
 530 |   document.getElementById('panel-unit').style.display  = m === 'unit'  ? '' : 'none';
 531 |   document.getElementById('owner-select').value = '';
 532 |   document.getElementById('prop-pay-select').value = '';
 533 |   resetPayForm();
 534 | }
 535 | 
 536 | function resetPayForm() {
 537 |   activeOwnerId = null;
 538 |   lastPaymentId = null;
 539 |   document.getElementById('owner-info-box').style.display = 'none';
 540 |   document.getElementById('post-pay-panel').style.display = 'none';
 541 |   document.getElementById('charges-panel').innerHTML = `
 542 |     <div class="charges-empty">
 543 |       <i class="fas fa-hand-point-up"></i>
 544 |       Selecciona un propietario o apartamento
 545 |     </div>`;
 546 |   document.getElementById('payment-form-wrapper').innerHTML = `
 547 |     <div class="charges-empty" style="padding:2.5rem 1rem;">
 548 |       <i class="fas fa-arrow-left"></i>
 549 |       Selecciona los cargos a pagar primero
 550 |     </div>`;
 551 | }
 552 | 
 553 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 554 | // CARGAR UNIDADES POR PROPIEDAD (modo unidad)
 555 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 556 | function loadUnitsByProp() {
 557 |   const propId = parseInt(document.getElementById('prop-pay-select').value);
 558 |   const sel = document.getElementById('unit-pay-select');
 559 |   sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Seleccione unidad</option>';
 560 |   const filtered = propId ? allUnitsCache.filter(u => u.property_id === propId) : allUnitsCache;
 561 |   filtered.forEach(u => sel.innerHTML += `<option value="${u.id}">Apt. ${u.unit_number}</option>`);
 562 |   resetPayForm();
 563 | }
 564 | 
 565 | async function loadUnitCharges() {
 566 |   const unitId = parseInt(document.getElementById('unit-pay-select').value);
 567 |   if (!unitId) { resetPayForm(); return; }
 568 | 
 569 |   const data = await apiRequest(`/finance/unit-statement/${unitId}`);
 570 |   if (!data) return;
 571 | 
 572 |   activeOwnerId = data.owner_id;
 573 |   document.getElementById('post-pay-panel').style.display = 'none';
 574 | 
 575 |   const infoBox = document.getElementById('owner-info-box');
 576 |   if (data.owner_id) {
 577 |     infoBox.style.display = 'block';
 578 |     document.getElementById('owner-info-text').textContent =
 579 |       `Propietario activo: ${data.owner_name}`;
 580 |   } else {
 581 |     infoBox.style.display = 'block';
 582 |     document.getElementById('owner-info-text').textContent =
 583 |       '⚠ Esta unidad no tiene propietario activo asignado.';
 584 |   }
 585 | 
 586 |   renderCharges(data.charges || []);
 587 | }
 588 | 
 589 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 590 | // CARGOS DEL PROPIETARIO
 591 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 592 | async function loadOwnerCharges(ownerId) {
 593 |   const charges = await apiRequest(`/finance/owner-statement/${ownerId}`);
 594 |   renderCharges(charges || []);
 595 | }
 596 | 
 597 | function renderCharges(charges) {
 598 |   const panel = document.getElementById('charges-panel');
 599 |   const formW = document.getElementById('payment-form-wrapper');
 600 | 
 601 |   const pendientes = charges.filter(c => c.status !== 'PAGADO');
 602 | 
 603 |   if (!pendientes.length) {
 604 |     panel.innerHTML = `
 605 |       <div class="charges-empty">
 606 |         <i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color:var(--success)"></i>
 607 |         Sin cargos pendientes
 608 |       </div>`;
 609 |     formW.innerHTML = `
 610 |       <div class="charges-empty" style="padding:2.5rem 1rem;">
 611 |         <i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color:var(--success)"></i>
 612 |         Este propietario no tiene deuda pendiente
 613 |       </div>`;
 614 |     return;
 615 |   }
 616 | 
 617 |   // Renderizar lista de cargos
 618 |   let html = `<p style="font-weight:600;font-size:.85rem;margin-bottom:10px;color:var(--text-secondary);">
 619 |     Selecciona los cargos a incluir en el pago:</p>`;
 620 | 
 621 |   pendientes.forEach(c => {
 622 |     html += `
 623 |     <div class="charge-row">
 624 |       <input type="checkbox" id="chk-${c.charge_id}" value="${c.charge_id}" onchange="recalcTotal()">
 625 |       <label for="chk-${c.charge_id}">
 626 |         <span class="cdesc">${c.description}</span>
 627 |         <span class="cmeta">Vence: ${formatDate(c.due_date)} &nbsp;·&nbsp;
 628 |           Total: $${formatMoney(c.total || c.amount)} &nbsp;·&nbsp;
 629 |           <strong>Saldo: $${formatMoney(c.balance)}</strong></span>
 630 |       </label>
 631 |       <span class="badge badge-${c.status}">${c.status}</span>
 632 |       <input type="number"
 633 |              data-charge="${c.charge_id}"
 634 |              data-max="${parseFloat(c.balance).toFixed(4)}"
 635 |              value="${parseFloat(c.balance).toFixed(2)}"
 636 |              step="0.01" min="0.01" max="${parseFloat(c.balance).toFixed(2)}"
 637 |              style="width:110px;margin-bottom:0;text-align:right;"
 638 |              oninput="recalcTotal()">
 639 |     </div>`;
 640 |   });
 641 | 
 642 |   panel.innerHTML = html;
 643 | 
 644 |   // Renderizar formulario de pago
 645 |   formW.innerHTML = `
 646 |     <label class="field-label">Total calculado</label>
 647 |     <div class="total-preview">
 648 |       <span>Monto a registrar</span>
 649 |       <strong id="total-display">$0.00</strong>
 650 |     </div>
 651 | 
 652 |     <label class="field-label">Fecha de pago</label>
 653 |     <input type="date" id="pay-date" value="${todayISO()}">
 654 | 
 655 |     <label class="field-label">N° Factura física (opcional)</label>
 656 |     <input type="text" id="pay-invoice" placeholder="Ej: 00542">
 657 | 
 658 |     <label class="field-label">Referencia / N° Transferencia (opcional)</label>
 659 |     <input type="text" id="pay-ref" placeholder="Ej: T-0098345">
 660 | 
 661 |     <div id="pay-feedback"></div>
 662 | 
 663 |     <button onclick="registerPayment()" style="width:100%;justify-content:center;margin-top:6px;">
 664 |       <i class="fas fa-save"></i> Registrar Pago
 665 |     </button>`;
 666 | 
 667 |   recalcTotal();
 668 | }
 669 | 
 670 | function recalcTotal() {
 671 |   let total = 0;
 672 |   document.querySelectorAll('#charges-panel input[type=checkbox]:checked').forEach(cb => {
 673 |     const inp = document.querySelector(`input[data-charge='${cb.value}']`);
 674 |     if (inp) total += parseFloat(inp.value) || 0;
 675 |   });
 676 |   const el = document.getElementById('total-display');
 677 |   if (el) el.textContent = `$${formatMoney(total)}`;
 678 | }
 679 | 
 680 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 681 | // REGISTRAR PAGO
 682 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 683 | async function registerPayment() {
 684 |   const fb = document.getElementById('pay-feedback');
 685 |   if (fb) fb.innerHTML = '';
 686 | 
 687 |   if (!activeOwnerId) {
 688 |     showToast('No hay propietario seleccionado', 'error'); return;
 689 |   }
 690 | 
 691 |   const applications = [];
 692 |   let error = null;
 693 | 
 694 |   document.querySelectorAll('#charges-panel input[type=checkbox]:checked').forEach(cb => {
 695 |     if (error) return;
 696 |     const chargeId = parseInt(cb.value);
 697 |     const inp      = document.querySelector(`input[data-charge='${chargeId}']`);
 698 |     const max      = parseFloat(inp.dataset.max);
 699 |     const amount   = parseFloat(inp.value);
 700 | 
 701 |     if (!amount || amount <= 0) { error = 'El monto debe ser mayor a $0.00'; return; }
 702 |     if (amount > max + 0.005)   { error = `$${amount.toFixed(2)} supera el saldo ($${max.toFixed(2)})`; return; }
 703 |     applications.push({ charge_id: chargeId, amount: parseFloat(amount.toFixed(2)) });
 704 |   });
 705 | 
 706 |   if (error) {
 707 |     if (fb) fb.innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-error">${error}</div>`; return;
 708 |   }
 709 |   if (!applications.length) {
 710 |     if (fb) fb.innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-warning">Selecciona al menos un cargo</div>`; return;
 711 |   }
 712 | 
 713 |   const payDate = document.getElementById('pay-date')?.value;
 714 |   if (!payDate) {
 715 |     if (fb) fb.innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-error">Ingresa la fecha del pago</div>`; return;
 716 |   }
 717 | 
 718 |   const total = applications.reduce((s, a) => s + a.amount, 0);
 719 | 
 720 |   const result = await apiRequest('/finance/payment-complete', 'POST', {
 721 |     owner_id:       activeOwnerId,
 722 |     payment_date:   payDate,
 723 |     amount:         parseFloat(total.toFixed(2)),
 724 |     invoice_number: document.getElementById('pay-invoice')?.value || null,
 725 |     reference:      document.getElementById('pay-ref')?.value     || null,
 726 |     applications,
 727 |   });
 728 | 
 729 |   if (result) {
 730 |     lastPaymentId = result.payment_id;
 731 |     document.getElementById('post-pay-panel').style.display = 'block';
 732 |     document.getElementById('pay-feedback').innerHTML =
 733 |       `<div class="alert alert-success">✓ Pago #${lastPaymentId} registrado correctamente</div>`;
 734 | 
 735 |     await loadChargesTable();
 736 | 
 737 |     // Refrescar cargos
 738 |     if (mode === 'owner') {
 739 |       loadOwnerCharges(activeOwnerId);
 740 |     } else {
 741 |       const uid = parseInt(document.getElementById('unit-pay-select').value);
 742 |       if (uid) loadUnitCharges(uid);
 743 |     }
 744 |   }
 745 | }
 746 | 
 747 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 748 | // FACTURA
 749 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 750 | function openInvoiceModal() {
 751 |   document.getElementById('modal-fiscal').value = '';
 752 |   document.getElementById('invoice-modal').classList.add('open');
 753 | }
 754 | 
 755 | function closeInvoiceModal() {
 756 |   document.getElementById('invoice-modal').classList.remove('open');
 757 | }
 758 | 
 759 | async function confirmInvoice() {
 760 |   closeInvoiceModal();
 761 |   if (!lastPaymentId) return;
 762 |   const fiscal = document.getElementById('modal-fiscal').value.trim();
 763 |   if (fiscal) {
 764 |     await apiRequest(`/finance/generate-invoice/payment/${lastPaymentId}?fiscal_number=${encodeURIComponent(fiscal)}`, 'POST');
 765 |   }
 766 |   window.open(`/static/factura.html?payment_id=${lastPaymentId}`, '_blank');
 767 | }
 768 | 
 769 | function openStatementFromPay() {
 770 |   if (!activeOwnerId) return;
 771 |   window.open(`/static/estado_cuenta.html?owner_id=${activeOwnerId}&t=${Date.now()}`, '_blank');
 772 | }
 773 | 
 774 | function openStatementSelected() {
 775 |   const id = document.getElementById('stmt-select').value;
 776 |   if (!id) { showToast('Selecciona un propietario', 'warning'); return; }
 777 |   window.open(`/static/estado_cuenta.html?owner_id=${id}&t=${Date.now()}`, '_blank');
 778 | }

 780 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 781 | // CREAR CARGO
 782 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 783 | function loadChargeUnits() {
 784 |   const propId = parseInt(document.getElementById('charge-prop-select').value);
 785 |   const sel = document.getElementById('charge-unit-select');
 786 |   sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Todas las unidades</option>';
 787 | 
 788 |   const units = propId ? allUnitsCache.filter(u => u.property_id === propId) : allUnitsCache;
 789 |   units.forEach(u => sel.innerHTML += `<option value="${u.id}">Apt. ${u.unit_number}</option>`);
 790 | 
 791 |   // Preview unidades afectadas
 792 |   const preview = document.getElementById('affected-units');
 793 |   if (!propId) {
 794 |     preview.innerHTML = `<div class="charges-empty"><i class="fas fa-building"></i>Selecciona una propiedad</div>`;
 795 |     return;
 796 |   }
 797 | 
 798 |   if (!units.length) {
 799 |     preview.innerHTML = `<div class="charges-empty"><i class="fas fa-info-circle"></i>Sin unidades en esta propiedad</div>`;
 800 |     return;
 801 |   }
 802 | 
 803 |   preview.innerHTML = `
 804 |     <p style="font-size:.8rem;color:var(--text-secondary);margin-bottom:10px;">
 805 |       Si no seleccionas unidad específica, el cargo se creará para estas ${units.length} unidades:
 806 |     </p>
 807 |     <div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:6px;">
 808 |       ${units.map(u => `<span class="badge badge-primary">Apt. ${u.unit_number}</span>`).join('')}
 809 |     </div>`;
 810 | }
 811 | 
 812 | async function createCharge() {
 813 |   const propId  = parseInt(document.getElementById('charge-prop-select').value);
 814 |   const unitId  = parseInt(document.getElementById('charge-unit-select').value) || null;
 815 |   const desc    = document.getElementById('charge-desc').value.trim();
 816 |   const amount  = parseFloat(document.getElementById('charge-amount').value);
 817 |   const created = document.getElementById('charge-date').value;
 818 |   const due     = document.getElementById('charge-due').value;
 819 | 
 820 |   if (!propId) { showToast('Selecciona una propiedad', 'error'); return; }
 821 |   if (!desc)   { showToast('Ingresa la descripción', 'error'); return; }
 822 |   if (!amount || amount <= 0) { showToast('Ingresa un monto válido', 'error'); return; }
 823 |   if (!due)    { showToast('Ingresa la fecha de vencimiento', 'error'); return; }
 824 | 
 825 |   let result;
 826 | 
 827 |   if (unitId) {
 828 |     // Cargo para una sola unidad
 829 |     result = await apiRequest('/charges/', 'POST', {
 830 |       unit_id: unitId, description: desc, amount,
 831 |       date_created: created || todayISO(), due_date: due,
 832 |     });
 833 |   } else {
 834 |     // Cargo general para toda la propiedad
 835 |     result = await apiRequest(`/finance/general-charge/${propId}`, 'POST', {
 836 |       description: desc, amount, due_date: due,
 837 |     });
 838 |   }
 839 | 
 840 |   if (result) {
 841 |     showToast(unitId
 842 |       ? 'Cargo creado correctamente'
 843 |       : `Cargos creados para todas las unidades`);
 844 |     document.getElementById('charge-desc').value   = '';
 845 |     document.getElementById('charge-amount').value = '';
 846 |     document.getElementById('charge-due').value    = '';
 847 |     document.getElementById('amount-preview').textContent = '0.00';
 848 |     await loadChargesTable();
 849 |   }
 850 | }
 851 | 
 852 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 853 | // TABLA HISTORIAL
 854 | // ══════════════════════════════════════════════
 855 | async function loadChargesTable() {
 856 |   allChargesCache = await apiRequest('/finance/charges');
 857 | 
 858 |   if (!Array.isArray(allChargesCache)) {
 859 |     console.error("ERROR API /finance/charges:", allChargesCache);
 860 |     allChargesCache = [];
 861 |   }
 862 | 
 863 |   const owners = [...new Set(allChargesCache.map(c => c.owner_name).filter(Boolean))].sort();
 864 |   const units  = [...new Set(allChargesCache.map(c => c.unit_number).filter(Boolean))].sort();
 865 | 
 866 |   const ownerSel = document.getElementById('filter-owner');
 867 |   const unitSel  = document.getElementById('filter-unit');
 868 | 
 869 |   if (ownerSel) {
 870 |     const prev = ownerSel.value;
 871 |     ownerSel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Todos</option>';
 872 |     owners.forEach(o => ownerSel.innerHTML += `<option value="${o}">${o}</option>`);
 873 |     ownerSel.value = prev;
 874 |   }
 875 |   if (unitSel) {
 876 |     const prev = unitSel.value;
 877 |     unitSel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Todos</option>';
 878 |     units.forEach(u => unitSel.innerHTML += `<option value="${u}">Apt. ${u}</option>`);
 879 |     unitSel.value = prev;
 880 |   }
 881 | 
 882 |   filterChargesTable();
 883 | }
 884 | 
 885 | function clearChargeFilters() {
 886 |   ['filter-status','filter-owner','filter-unit'].forEach(id => {
 887 |     const el = document.getElementById(id);
 888 |     if (el) el.value = '';
 889 |   });
 890 |   const descEl = document.getElementById('filter-desc');
 891 |   if (descEl) descEl.value = '';
 892 |   filterChargesTable();
 893 | }
 894 | 
 895 | function filterChargesTable() {
 896 |   const status = document.getElementById('filter-status')?.value  || '';
 897 |   const owner  = document.getElementById('filter-owner')?.value   || '';
 898 |   const unit   = document.getElementById('filter-unit')?.value    || '';
 899 |   const desc   = (document.getElementById('filter-desc')?.value   || '').toLowerCase().trim();
 900 | 
 901 |   const list = allChargesCache.filter(c => {
 902 |     if (status && c.status      !== status)                      return false;
 903 |     if (owner  && c.owner_name  !== owner)                       return false;
 904 |     if (unit   && c.unit_number !== unit)                        return false;
 905 |     if (desc   && !c.description?.toLowerCase().includes(desc))  return false;
 906 |     return true;
 907 |   });
 908 | 
 909 |   const badge = document.getElementById('charges-count-badge');
 910 |   if (badge) badge.textContent = list.length;
 911 | 
 912 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('charges-table-body');
 913 | 
 914 |   if (!list.length) {
 915 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="9" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 916 |       Sin cargos con los filtros aplicados</td></tr>`;
 917 |     return;
 918 |   }
 919 | 
 920 |   tbody.innerHTML = list.map(c => {
 921 |     const paid = parseFloat(c.amount || 0) - parseFloat(c.balance || 0);
 922 | 
 923 |     // Botón de factura para cargos PAGADOS
 924 |     // c.payment_id viene del endpoint /finance/charges
 925 |     let accionBtn = '—';
 926 |     if (c.status === 'PAGADO' && c.payment_id) {
 927 |       accionBtn = `
 928 |         <button onclick="verFacturaDesdeHistorial(${c.payment_id})"
 929 |           style="background:var(--accent-soft);color:var(--accent);border:1px solid var(--border);
 930 |                  padding:4px 10px;font-size:.75rem;border-radius:5px;cursor:pointer;
 931 |                  font-family:inherit;font-weight:600;display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;
 932 |                  margin:0;width:auto;">
 933 |           <i class="fas fa-receipt"></i> Ver Factura
 934 |         </button>`;
 935 |     } else if (c.status === 'PARCIAL' && c.payment_id) {
 936 |       accionBtn = `
 937 |         <button onclick="verFacturaDesdeHistorial(${c.payment_id})"
 938 |           style="background:#fef3c7;color:#92400e;border:1px solid #fde68a;
 939 |                  padding:4px 10px;font-size:.75rem;border-radius:5px;cursor:pointer;
 940 |                  font-family:inherit;font-weight:600;display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;
 941 |                  margin:0;width:auto;">
 942 |           <i class="fas fa-receipt"></i> Ver Recibo
 943 |         </button>`;
 944 |     }
 945 | 
 946 |     return `<tr>
 947 |       <td>${c.owner_name || '<em style="color:var(--text-muted)">Sin asignar</em>'}</td>
 948 |       <td>${c.unit_number ? `Apt. ${c.unit_number}` : '—'}</td>
 949 |       <td><strong>${c.description}</strong></td>
 950 |       <td style="font-size:.82rem;color:var(--text-secondary);">${formatDate(c.due_date)}</td>
 951 |       <td class="td-right">$${formatMoney(c.amount)}</td>
 952 |       <td class="td-right" style="color:var(--success);">$${formatMoney(paid)}</td>
 953 |       <td class="td-right td-bold">$${formatMoney(c.balance)}</td>
 954 |       <td><span class="badge badge-${c.status}">${c.status}</span></td>
 955 |       <td>${accionBtn}</td>
 956 |     </tr>`;
 957 |   }).join('');
 958 | }
 959 | // Nueva función para ver factura desde el historial
 960 | function verFacturaDesdeHistorial(paymentId) {
 961 |   window.open(`/static/factura.html?payment_id=${paymentId}`, '_blank');
 962 | }
 963 | 
 964 | renderSidebar('finances');
 965 | init();
 966 | </script>
 967 | </body>
 968 | </html>

 286 |           <span class="badge badge-primary" id="pre-count">0</span>
 287 |         </div>
 288 |         <div id="pre-lista" style="padding:12px;">
 289 |           <div style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 290 |             <i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin" style="font-size:1.5rem;display:block;margin-bottom:.5rem;opacity:.4;"></i>

 305 | // ── Estado ────────────────────────────────────────────
 306 | let allUnits        = [];
 307 | let allVisitas      = [];
 308 | let allPreregistros = [];
 309 | let filteredVisitas = [];
 310 | 
 311 | // ── Init ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 312 | async function init() {
 313 |   allUnits = await apiRequest('/units') || [];
 314 | 
 315 |   // Llenar selects de apartamentos
 316 |   ['visit-apto','pre-apto','hf-apto'].forEach(id => {
 317 |     const sel = document.getElementById(id);
 318 |     if (!sel) return;
 319 |     const isFilter = id === 'hf-apto';
 320 |     if (isFilter) sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Todos</option>';
 321 |     else          sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Seleccione apartamento</option>';
 322 |     [...allUnits].sort((a,b) => a.unit_number.localeCompare(b.unit_number))
 323 |       .forEach(u => sel.innerHTML += `<option value="${u.id}" data-num="${u.unit_number}">Apt. ${u.unit_number}</option>`);
 324 |   });
 325 | 
 326 |   // Fecha de hoy por defecto
 327 |   document.getElementById('pre-fecha').value = todayISO();
 328 |   document.getElementById('hf-desde').value  = todayISO();
 329 | 
 330 |   await Promise.all([cargarVisitas(), cargarPreregistros()]);
 331 | }
 332 | 
 333 | // ══ VISITAS ══════════════════════════════════════════
 334 | 
 335 | async function cargarVisitas() {
 336 |   allVisitas = await apiRequest('/garita/visitas') || [];
 337 |   filtrarHistorial();
 338 | }
 339 | 
 340 | function filtrarHistorial() {
 341 |   const apto   = document.getElementById('hf-apto').value;
 342 |   const tipo   = document.getElementById('hf-tipo').value;
 343 |   const desde  = document.getElementById('hf-desde').value;
 344 |   const hasta  = document.getElementById('hf-hasta').value;
 345 |   const search = document.getElementById('hf-search').value.toLowerCase().trim();
 346 | 
 347 |   filteredVisitas = allVisitas.filter(v => {
 348 |     if (apto  && String(v.unit_id) !== String(apto)) return false;
 349 |     if (tipo  && v.tipo_visita     !== tipo)          return false;
 350 |     if (desde && v.fecha_ingreso   < desde)           return false;
 351 |     if (hasta && v.fecha_ingreso   > hasta + 'T23:59') return false;
 352 |     if (search) {
 353 |       const txt = [v.nombre_visitante, v.cedula, v.motivo, v.unit_number, v.placa||''].join(' ').toLowerCase();
 354 |       if (!txt.includes(search)) return false;
 355 |     }
 356 |     return true;
 357 |   });
 358 | 
 359 |   renderHistorial();
 360 | }
 361 | 
 362 | function limpiarFiltrosHistorial() {
 363 |   document.getElementById('hf-apto').value   = '';
 364 |   document.getElementById('hf-tipo').value   = '';
 365 |   document.getElementById('hf-desde').value  = todayISO();
 366 |   document.getElementById('hf-hasta').value  = '';
 367 |   document.getElementById('hf-search').value = '';
 368 |   filtrarHistorial();
 369 | }
 370 | 
 371 | function renderHistorial() {
 372 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('hist-tbody');
 373 |   if (!filteredVisitas.length) {
 374 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="9" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 375 |       Sin registros con los filtros aplicados</td></tr>`;
 376 |     return;
 377 |   }
 378 |   tbody.innerHTML = filteredVisitas.map(v => {
 379 |     const fecha    = v.fecha_ingreso ? new Date(v.fecha_ingreso).toLocaleString('es-PA') : '—';
 380 |     const statusCls= `status-${v.estado}`;
 381 |     const salida   = v.estado === 'INGRESO'
 382 |       ? `<button onclick="registrarSalida(${v.id})"
 383 |            style="background:#fee2e2;color:#991b1b;border:1px solid #fca5a5;
 384 |                   padding:3px 10px;font-size:.72rem;border-radius:5px;cursor:pointer;
 385 |                   font-family:inherit;font-weight:600;width:auto;margin:0;">
 386 |            <i class="fas fa-sign-out-alt"></i> Salida
 387 |          </button>` : '—';
 388 |     return `<tr>
 389 |       <td style="font-size:.78rem;white-space:nowrap;">${fecha}</td>
 390 |       <td><strong>${v.nombre_visitante}</strong></td>
 391 |       <td style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--text-muted);">${v.cedula||'—'}</td>
 392 |       <td>Apt. ${v.unit_number||'—'}</td>
 393 |       <td style="font-size:.82rem;">${v.motivo}</td>
 394 |       <td><span class="badge" style="font-size:.7rem;">${v.tipo_visita}</span></td>
 395 |       <td style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--text-muted);">${v.placa||'—'}</td>
 396 |       <td><span class="badge ${statusCls}" style="font-size:.7rem;">${v.estado}</span></td>
 397 |       <td>${salida}</td>
 398 |     </tr>`;
 399 |   }).join('');
 400 | }
 401 | 
 402 | async function registrarIngreso() {
 403 |   const nombre = document.getElementById('visit-nombre').value.trim();
 404 |   const aptoSel= document.getElementById('visit-apto');
 405 |   const unitId = aptoSel.value;
 406 |   const motivo = document.getElementById('visit-motivo').value.trim();
 407 | 
 408 |   if (!nombre) { showToast('Ingresa el nombre del visitante', 'error'); return; }
 409 |   if (!unitId) { showToast('Selecciona el apartamento', 'error'); return; }
 410 |   if (!motivo) { showToast('Ingresa el motivo de la visita', 'error'); return; }
 411 | 
 412 |   const preId  = document.getElementById('visit-preregistro-id').value || null;
 413 |   const unitNum= aptoSel.options[aptoSel.selectedIndex]?.getAttribute('data-num') || '';
 414 | 
 415 |   const data = {
 416 |     nombre_visitante: nombre,
 417 |     cedula:           document.getElementById('visit-cedula').value.trim() || null,
 418 |     unit_id:          parseInt(unitId),
 419 |     unit_number:      unitNum,
 420 |     motivo:           motivo,
 421 |     tipo_visita:      document.getElementById('visit-tipo').value,
 422 |     placa:            document.getElementById('visit-placa').value.trim() || null,
 423 |     observaciones:    document.getElementById('visit-obs').value.trim()   || null,
 424 |     preregistro_id:   preId ? parseInt(preId) : null,
 425 |     fecha_ingreso:    new Date().toISOString(),
 426 |     estado:           'INGRESO',
 427 |   };
 428 | 
 429 |   const r = await apiRequest('/garita/visitas', 'POST', data);
 430 |   if (r) {
 431 |     showToast(`✓ Ingreso registrado para Apt. ${unitNum}`, 'success');
 432 |     limpiarFormulario();
 433 |     cargarVisitas();
 434 |     // Marcar pre-registro como usado si aplica
 435 |     if (preId) {
 436 |       await apiRequest(`/garita/preregistros/${preId}/usar`, 'PATCH', {});
 437 |       cargarPreregistros();
 438 |     }
 439 |   }
 440 | }
 441 | 
 442 | async function registrarSalida(visitaId) {
 443 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/garita/visitas/${visitaId}/salida`, 'PATCH', {
 444 |     fecha_salida: new Date().toISOString(),
 445 |     estado: 'SALIDA',
 446 |   });
 447 |   if (r) { showToast('Salida registrada', 'success'); cargarVisitas(); }
 448 | }
 449 | 
 450 | function limpiarFormulario() {
 451 |   ['visit-nombre','visit-cedula','visit-motivo','visit-placa','visit-obs'].forEach(id => {
 452 |     document.getElementById(id).value = '';
 453 |   });
 454 |   document.getElementById('visit-apto').value = '';
 455 |   document.getElementById('visit-tipo').value = 'Personal';
 456 |   document.getElementById('visit-preregistro-id').value = '';
 457 |   document.getElementById('codigo-buscar').value = '';
 458 |   document.getElementById('codigo-resultado').innerHTML = '';
 459 | }
 460 | 
 461 | // ── Buscar por código ─────────────────────────────────
 462 | async function buscarPorCodigo() {
 463 |   const codigo = document.getElementById('codigo-buscar').value.trim().toUpperCase();
 464 |   if (!codigo) { showToast('Ingresa un código', 'warning'); return; }
 465 | 
 466 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/garita/preregistros/codigo/${codigo}`);
 467 |   const el = document.getElementById('codigo-resultado');
 468 | 
 469 |   if (!r || r.error) {
 470 |     el.innerHTML = `<div style="padding:10px;background:#fee2e2;border-radius:6px;font-size:.83rem;color:#991b1b;">
 471 |       <i class="fas fa-times-circle"></i> Código no encontrado o ya utilizado
 472 |     </div>`;
 473 |     return;
 474 |   }
 475 | 
 476 |   el.innerHTML = `<div style="padding:12px;background:#d1fae5;border-radius:6px;font-size:.83rem;color:#065f46;border:1px solid #a7f3d0;">
 477 |     <i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> <strong>Código válido</strong><br>
 478 |     Apartamento: <strong>Apt. ${r.unit_number}</strong><br>
 479 |     ${r.nombre_visitante ? `Visitante esperado: <strong>${r.nombre_visitante}</strong><br>` : ''}
 480 |     ${r.motivo ? `Motivo: ${r.motivo}` : ''}
 481 |   </div>`;
 482 | 
 483 |   // Prellenar formulario
 484 |   document.getElementById('visit-preregistro-id').value = r.id;
 485 |   if (r.nombre_visitante) document.getElementById('visit-nombre').value = r.nombre_visitante;
 486 |   if (r.motivo)           document.getElementById('visit-motivo').value = r.motivo;
 487 |   // Seleccionar el apartamento
 488 |   const sel = document.getElementById('visit-apto');
 489 |   for (const opt of sel.options) {
 490 |     if (opt.value === String(r.unit_id)) { sel.value = opt.value; break; }
 491 |   }
 492 | }
 493 | 
 494 | // ══ PRE-REGISTROS ═════════════════════════════════════
 495 | 
 496 | async function cargarPreregistros() {
 497 |   allPreregistros = await apiRequest('/garita/preregistros?activos=true') || [];
 498 |   document.getElementById('pre-count').textContent = allPreregistros.length;
 499 |   renderPreregistros();
 500 | }
 501 | 
 502 | function renderPreregistros() {
 503 |   const el = document.getElementById('pre-lista');
 504 |   if (!allPreregistros.length) {
 505 |     el.innerHTML = `<div style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 506 |       Sin pre-registros activos</div>`;
 507 |     return;
 508 |   }
 509 |   el.innerHTML = allPreregistros.map(p => `
 510 |     <div style="border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:var(--radius-md);padding:12px 14px;margin-bottom:8px;background:var(--card-bg);">
 511 |       <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;">
 512 |         <div>
 513 |           <div style="font-size:.85rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--text-primary);margin-bottom:4px;">
 514 |             Apt. ${p.unit_number}
 515 |             ${p.nombre_visitante ? `· <span style="font-weight:400;color:var(--text-secondary);">${p.nombre_visitante}</span>` : ''}
 516 |           </div>
 517 |           <span class="pre-code-badge">
 518 |             <i class="fas fa-key" style="font-size:.7rem;"></i>
 519 |             ${p.codigo}
 520 |           </span>
 521 |           ${p.fecha_esperada ? `<span style="font-size:.75rem;color:var(--text-muted);margin-left:8px;">${formatDate(p.fecha_esperada)}</span>` : ''}
 522 |           ${p.motivo ? `<div style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--text-muted);margin-top:4px;">${p.motivo}</div>` : ''}
 523 |         </div>
 524 |         <button onclick="cancelarPreregistro(${p.id})"
 525 |           style="background:#fee2e2;color:#991b1b;border:1px solid #fca5a5;
 526 |                  padding:3px 8px;font-size:.72rem;border-radius:5px;cursor:pointer;
 527 |                  font-family:inherit;font-weight:600;width:auto;margin:0;flex-shrink:0;">
 528 |           <i class="fas fa-times"></i>
 529 |         </button>
 530 |       </div>
 531 |     </div>`).join('');
 532 | }
 533 | 
 534 | async function crearPreregistro() {
 535 |   const unitId = document.getElementById('pre-apto').value;
 536 |   if (!unitId) { showToast('Selecciona el apartamento', 'error'); return; }
 537 | 
 538 |   const sel     = document.getElementById('pre-apto');
 539 |   const unitNum = sel.options[sel.selectedIndex]?.getAttribute('data-num') || '';
 540 | 
 541 |   // Generar código aleatorio VIS-XXXX
 542 |   const codigo = 'VIS-' + Math.floor(1000 + Math.random() * 9000);
 543 | 
 544 |   const data = {
 545 |     unit_id:          parseInt(unitId),
 546 |     unit_number:      unitNum,
 547 |     codigo:           codigo,
 548 |     nombre_visitante: document.getElementById('pre-nombre').value.trim() || null,
 549 |     fecha_esperada:   document.getElementById('pre-fecha').value   || null,
 550 |     motivo:           document.getElementById('pre-motivo').value.trim() || null,
 551 |     notas:            document.getElementById('pre-notas').value.trim()  || null,
 552 |     activo:           true,
 553 |   };
 554 | 
 555 |   const r = await apiRequest('/garita/preregistros', 'POST', data);
 556 |   if (r) {
 557 |     showToast(`Código ${codigo} generado para Apt. ${unitNum}`, 'success');
 558 |     ['pre-nombre','pre-motivo','pre-notas'].forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value = '');
 559 |     document.getElementById('pre-apto').value   = '';
 560 |     document.getElementById('pre-fecha').value  = todayISO();
 561 |     cargarPreregistros();
 562 |   }
 563 | }
 564 | 
 565 | async function cancelarPreregistro(id) {
 566 |   if (!confirm('¿Cancelar este pre-registro?')) return;
 567 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/garita/preregistros/${id}`, 'DELETE');
 568 |   if (r) { showToast('Pre-registro cancelado'); cargarPreregistros(); }
 569 | }
 570 | 
 571 | // ── Exportar historial ────────────────────────────────
 572 | function exportarHistorial() {
 573 |   if (!filteredVisitas.length) { showToast('Sin datos para exportar', 'warning'); return; }
 574 |   const headers = ['Fecha Ingreso','Fecha Salida','Visitante','Cédula','Apartamento','Motivo','Tipo','Placa','Estado','Observaciones'];
 575 |   const rows    = filteredVisitas.map(v => [
 576 |     v.fecha_ingreso ? new Date(v.fecha_ingreso).toLocaleString('es-PA') : '',
 577 |     v.fecha_salida  ? new Date(v.fecha_salida).toLocaleString('es-PA')  : '',
 578 |     v.nombre_visitante, v.cedula||'', `Apt. ${v.unit_number||''}`,
 579 |     v.motivo, v.tipo_visita, v.placa||'', v.estado, v.observaciones||''
 580 |   ]);
 581 |   const ws = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet([headers, ...rows]);
 582 |   ws['!cols'] = [{wch:18},{wch:18},{wch:22},{wch:12},{wch:10},{wch:25},{wch:12},{wch:10},{wch:10},{wch:25}];
 583 |   const wb = XLSX.utils.book_new();
 584 |   XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb, ws, 'Visitas');
 585 |   XLSX.writeFile(wb, `visitas_${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.xlsx`);
 586 |   showToast('Exportado', 'success');
 587 | }
 588 | 
 589 | // ── Tabs ──────────────────────────────────────────────
 590 | function switchTab(tab) {
 591 |   document.querySelectorAll('.garita-tab').forEach((b,i) => {
 592 |     b.classList.toggle('active', ['registrar','historial','preregistro'][i] === tab);
 593 |   });
 594 |   document.querySelectorAll('.garita-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
 595 |   document.getElementById('panel-' + tab).classList.add('active');
 596 | }
 597 | 
 598 | init();
 599 | </script>
 600 | </body>
 601 | </html>
