 310 | 
 311 | let allPagos  = [];
 312 | let filtrados = [];
 313 | 
 314 | /* ── Tag de concepto ─────────────────────────────────── */
 315 | function razonTag(t) {
 316 |   if (!t || t === '—') return `<span class="razon-tag tag-otros">—</span>`;
 317 |   const l = t.toLowerCase();
 318 |   let c = 'tag-otros';
 319 |   if (l.includes('mantenimiento'))                         c = 'tag-mant';
 320 |   else if (l.includes('gas'))                              c = 'tag-gas';
 321 |   else if (l.includes('ascensor') || l.includes('cuota')) c = 'tag-asc';
 322 |   else if (l.includes('admin'))                            c = 'tag-admin';
 323 |   return `<span class="razon-tag ${c}">${t}</span>`;
 324 | }
 325 | 
 326 | /* ── Init ─────────────────────────────────────────────── */
 327 | async function init() {
 328 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('hist-tbody');
 329 |   const pagos = await apiRequest('/finance/payments-history');
 330 | 
 331 |   if (!pagos) {
 332 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="7" style="text-align:center;padding:3rem;color:var(--danger);">Error al cargar el historial.</td></tr>`;
 333 |     return;
 334 |   }
 335 |   if (!pagos.length) {
 336 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="7" style="text-align:center;padding:3rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 337 |       <i class="fas fa-inbox" style="font-size:2rem;opacity:.3;display:block;margin-bottom:.5rem;"></i>
 338 |       No hay pagos registrados.<br><small>Usa el importador de historial para cargar registros.</small>
 339 |     </td></tr>`;
 340 |     return;
 341 |   }
 342 | 
 343 |   allPagos = pagos.map(p => ({
 344 |     payment_id:  p.payment_id,
 345 |     factura:     p.factura     || '—',
 346 |     fecha:       p.fecha       || '',
 347 |     apto:        p.unit_number || '—',
 348 |     owner_name:  p.owner_name  || '—',
 349 |     concepto:    p.concepto    || '—',
 350 |     observacion: p.observacion || '',
 351 |     monto:       parseFloat(p.monto || 0),
 352 |   })).sort((a, b) => b.fecha.localeCompare(a.fecha));
 353 | 
 354 |   llenarFiltros();
 355 |   aplicar();
 356 |   llenarSelectoresReporte();
 357 | }
 358 | 
 359 | /* ── Selects ──────────────────────────────────────────── */
 360 | function llenarFiltros() {
 361 |   const owners    = [...new Set(allPagos.map(p => p.owner_name))].sort();
 362 |   const aptos     = [...new Set(allPagos.map(p => p.apto))].sort();
 363 |   const conceptos = [...new Set(allPagos.map(p => p.concepto))].sort();
 364 |   document.getElementById('f-owner').innerHTML   += owners.map(o    => `<option>${o}</option>`).join('');
 365 |   document.getElementById('f-apto').innerHTML    += aptos.map(a     => `<option>${a}</option>`).join('');
 366 |   document.getElementById('f-concepto').innerHTML+= conceptos.map(c => `<option>${c}</option>`).join('');
 367 | }
 368 | 
 369 | function llenarSelectoresReporte() {
 370 |   const aptos     = [...new Set(allPagos.map(p => p.apto))].sort();
 371 |   const conceptos = [...new Set(allPagos.map(p => p.concepto))].sort();
 372 |   document.getElementById('rep-apto').innerHTML    += aptos.map(a     => `<option>${a}</option>`).join('');
 373 |   document.getElementById('rep-concepto').innerHTML+= conceptos.map(c => `<option>${c}</option>`).join('');
 374 | }
 375 | 
 376 | /* ── Filtros tabla ───────────────────────────────────── */
 377 | function aplicar() {
 378 |   const owner    = document.getElementById('f-owner').value;
 379 |   const apto     = document.getElementById('f-apto').value;
 380 |   const concepto = document.getElementById('f-concepto').value;
 381 |   const desde    = document.getElementById('f-desde').value;
 382 |   const hasta    = document.getElementById('f-hasta').value;
 383 |   const search   = document.getElementById('f-search').value.toLowerCase().trim();
 384 | 
 385 |   filtrados = allPagos.filter(p => {
 386 |     if (owner    && p.owner_name !== owner)    return false;
 387 |     if (apto     && p.apto       !== apto)     return false;
 388 |     if (concepto && p.concepto   !== concepto) return false;
 389 |     if (desde    && p.fecha < desde)           return false;
 390 |     if (hasta    && p.fecha > hasta)           return false;
 391 |     if (search) {
 392 |       const txt = [p.factura, String(p.monto), p.concepto, p.owner_name, p.apto].join(' ').toLowerCase();
 393 |       if (!txt.includes(search)) return false;
 394 |     }
 395 |     return true;
 396 |   });
 397 |   renderTabla();
 398 |   renderResumen();
 399 | }
 400 | 
 401 | function limpiarFiltros() {
 402 |   ['f-owner','f-apto','f-concepto','f-desde','f-hasta','f-search'].forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value = '');
 403 |   aplicar();
 404 | }
 405 | 
 406 | /* ── Tabla ───────────────────────────────────────────── */
 407 | function renderTabla() {
 408 |   document.getElementById('total-count').textContent = filtrados.length;
 409 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('hist-tbody');
 410 |   if (!filtrados.length) {
 411 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="7" style="text-align:center;padding:3rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin resultados</td></tr>`;
 412 |     document.getElementById('page-info').textContent = '';
 413 |     return;
 414 |   }
 415 |   const visible = filtrados.slice(0, 500);
 416 |   tbody.innerHTML = visible.map(p => `
 417 |     <tr>
 418 |       <td class="td-mono" style="font-size:.78rem;color:var(--text-muted);">${p.factura}</td>
 419 |       <td style="white-space:nowrap;">${formatDate(p.fecha)}</td>
 420 |       <td><strong>Apt. ${p.apto}</strong></td>
 421 |       <td style="font-size:.83rem;">${p.owner_name}</td>
 422 |       <td>${razonTag(p.concepto)}</td>
 423 |       <td class="td-right"><strong>$${formatMoney(p.monto)}</strong></td>
 424 |       <td>
 425 |         ${p.payment_id ? `
 426 |           <button onclick="verFacturaDesdeHistorial(${p.payment_id})"
 427 |             style="background:var(--accent-soft);color:var(--accent);border:1px solid var(--border);
 428 |                    padding:4px 10px;font-size:.75rem;border-radius:5px;cursor:pointer;
 429 |                    font-family:inherit;font-weight:600;display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;
 430 |                    margin:0;width:auto;">
 431 |             <i class="fas fa-receipt"></i> Ver Factura
 432 |           </button>
 433 |         ` : `<span style="color:var(--text-muted);">�</span>`}
 434 |       </td>
 435 |     </tr>`).join('');
 436 |   document.getElementById('page-info').textContent =
 437 |     filtrados.length > 500
 438 |       ? `Mostrando 500 de ${filtrados.length} — exporta Excel para ver todos`
 439 |       : `${filtrados.length} registro${filtrados.length !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`;
 440 | }
 441 | 
 442 | function verFacturaDesdeHistorial(paymentId) {
 443 |   window.open(`/static/factura.html?payment_id=${paymentId}`, '_blank');
 444 | }
 445 | /* ── Resumen chips ───────────────────────────────────── */
 446 | function renderResumen() {
 447 |   const chips = document.getElementById('summary-chips');
 448 |   if (!filtrados.length) { chips.innerHTML = ''; return; }
 449 |   const total = filtrados.reduce((s, p) => s + p.monto, 0);
 450 |   const porC  = {};
 451 |   filtrados.forEach(p => { porC[p.concepto] = (porC[p.concepto] || 0) + p.monto; });
 452 |   let html = `
 453 |     <div class="s-chip"><strong>${filtrados.length}</strong><span>Registros</span></div>
 454 |     <div class="s-chip"><strong>$${formatMoney(total)}</strong><span>Total</span></div>`;
 455 |   Object.entries(porC).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]).slice(0,5).forEach(([k,v]) => {
 456 |     html += `<div class="s-chip"><strong>$${formatMoney(v)}</strong><span>${k}</span></div>`;
 457 |   });
 458 |   chips.innerHTML = html;
 459 | }
 460 | 
 461 | /* ── Excel general ───────────────────────────────────── */
 462 | function exportarExcel() {
 463 |   if (!filtrados.length) { showToast('Sin datos para exportar','warning'); return; }
 464 |   const headers = ['# Factura','Fecha','Apartamento','Propietario','Concepto','Monto'];
 465 |   const rows    = filtrados.map(p => [p.factura, p.fecha, p.apto, p.owner_name, p.concepto, p.monto]);
 466 |   const ws = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet([headers, ...rows]);
 467 |   ws['!cols'] = [{wch:12},{wch:12},{wch:12},{wch:28},{wch:22},{wch:12}];
 468 |   const wb = XLSX.utils.book_new();
 469 |   XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb, ws, 'Historial');
 470 |   XLSX.writeFile(wb, `historial_${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.xlsx`);
 471 |   showToast('Archivo descargado','success');
 472 | }
 473 | 
 474 | /* ══ REPORTE PDF ═══════════════════════════════════════ */
 475 | function abrirReporte() {
 476 |   document.getElementById('reporte-modal').classList.add('open');
 477 | }
 478 | function cerrarReporte() {
 479 |   document.getElementById('reporte-modal').classList.remove('open');
 480 | }
 481 | document.getElementById('reporte-modal').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
 482 |   if (e.target === this) cerrarReporte();
 483 | });
 484 | 
 485 | function getPagosFiltradosReporte() {
 486 |   const apto     = document.getElementById('rep-apto').value;
 487 |   const desde    = document.getElementById('rep-desde').value;
 488 |   const hasta    = document.getElementById('rep-hasta').value;
 489 |   const concepto = document.getElementById('rep-concepto').value;
 490 |   if (!apto) return null;
 491 |   let p = allPagos.filter(x => x.apto === apto);
 492 |   if (desde)    p = p.filter(x => x.fecha >= desde);
 493 |   if (hasta)    p = p.filter(x => x.fecha <= hasta);
 494 |   if (concepto) p = p.filter(x => x.concepto === concepto);
 495 |   return { apto, desde, hasta, concepto, pagos: p };
 496 | }
 497 | 
 498 | function fdate(s) {
 499 |   if (!s) return '—';
 500 |   try {
 501 |     const [y,m,d] = s.split('T')[0].split('-');
 502 |     const months = ['ene','feb','mar','abr','may','jun','jul','ago','sep','oct','nov','dic'];
 503 |     return `${parseInt(d)} ${months[parseInt(m)-1]} ${y}`;
 504 |   } catch { return s; }
 505 | }
 506 | 
 507 | function generarReporte() {
 508 |   const content = document.getElementById('reporte-content');
 509 |   const res = getPagosFiltradosReporte();
 510 | 
 511 |   if (!res) {
 512 |     content.innerHTML = `<div style="text-align:center;padding:3rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 513 |       <i class="fas fa-home" style="font-size:2rem;opacity:.3;display:block;margin-bottom:.5rem;"></i>
 514 |       Selecciona un apartamento para generar el reporte</div>`;
 515 |     return;
 516 |   }
 517 | 
 518 |   const { apto, desde, hasta, concepto, pagos } = res;
 519 | 
 520 |   if (!pagos.length) {
 521 |     content.innerHTML = `<div style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin pagos con los filtros seleccionados</div>`;
 522 |     return;
 523 |   }
 524 | 
 525 |   const owner  = pagos[0]?.owner_name || '—';
 526 |   const total  = pagos.reduce((s, p) => s + p.monto, 0);
 527 |   const hoy    = new Date().toLocaleDateString('es-PA', { year:'numeric', month:'long', day:'numeric' });
 528 |   const periodo= desde && hasta ? `${fdate(desde)} al ${fdate(hasta)}`
 529 |                : desde ? `Desde ${fdate(desde)}`
 530 |                : hasta ? `Hasta ${fdate(hasta)}` : 'Histórico completo';
 531 | 
 532 |   // Resumen por concepto
 533 |   const porC = {};
 534 |   pagos.forEach(p => { porC[p.concepto] = (porC[p.concepto] || 0) + p.monto; });
 535 | 
 536 |   // Intentar logo
 537 |   const logoHtml = `<div class="brand-logo" id="pdf-logo-box">AR</div>`;
 538 | 
 539 |   content.innerHTML = `
 540 |     <div id="pdf-doc" class="pdf-doc">
 541 | 
 542 |       <!-- Cabecera igual al estado de cuenta -->
 543 |       <div class="doc-head">
 544 |         <div class="brand">
 545 |           ${logoHtml}
 546 |           <div class="brand-name">
 547 |             <h1>ALIANZA RESIDENCIAL</h1>
 548 |             <p>Administración de Propiedades</p>
 549 |           </div>
 550 |         </div>
 551 |         <div class="doc-title">
 552 |           <h2>Reporte de Pagos</h2>
 553 |           <p>Generado el ${hoy}</p>
 554 |         </div>
 555 |       </div>
 556 | 
 557 |       <!-- Info del apartamento -->
 558 |       <div class="info-grid">
 559 |         <div class="info-cell">
 560 |           <div class="ic-lbl">Apartamento</div>
 561 |           <div class="ic-val">Apt. ${apto}</div>
 562 |         </div>
 563 |         <div class="info-cell">
 564 |           <div class="ic-lbl">Propietario</div>
 565 |           <div class="ic-val">${owner}</div>
 566 |         </div>
 567 |         <div class="info-cell">
 568 |           <div class="ic-lbl">Período</div>
 569 |           <div class="ic-val" style="font-size:.82rem;">${periodo}</div>
 570 |         </div>
 571 |       </div>
 572 | 
 573 |       <!-- Resumen por concepto -->
 574 |       <div class="section-title">Resumen por concepto</div>
 575 |       <div class="sum-row">
 576 |         ${Object.entries(porC).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]).map(([k,v]) => `
 577 |           <div class="sum-chip">
 578 |             <strong>$${formatMoney(v)}</strong>
 579 |             <span>${k}</span>
 580 |           </div>`).join('')}
 581 |       </div>
 582 | 
 583 |       <!-- Tabla de pagos -->
 584 |       <div class="section-title">Detalle de pagos</div>
 585 |       <table>
 586 |         <thead>
 587 |           <tr>
 588 |             <th># Factura</th>
 589 |             <th>Fecha</th>
 590 |             <th>Concepto</th>
 591 |             <th class="r">Monto</th>
 592 |           </tr>
 593 |         </thead>
 594 |         <tbody>
 595 |           ${pagos.map(p => `
 596 |             <tr>
 597 |               <td class="muted">${p.factura}</td>
 598 |               <td>${fdate(p.fecha)}</td>
 599 |               <td>${p.concepto}</td>
 600 |               <td class="r">$${formatMoney(p.monto)}</td>
 601 |             </tr>`).join('')}
 602 |         </tbody>
 603 |       </table>
 604 | 
 605 |       <!-- Totales -->
 606 |       <div class="total-line">
 607 |         <div>
 608 |           <div class="tl">Registros</div>
 609 |           <div class="tv">${pagos.length}</div>
 610 |         </div>
 611 |         <div>
 612 |           <div class="tl">Total pagado</div>
 613 |           <div class="tv">$${formatMoney(total)}</div>
 614 |         </div>
 615 |       </div>
 616 | 
 617 |       <!-- Aviso legal -->
 618 |       <div class="legal-notice">
 619 |         <p>
 620 |           <strong>DOCUMENTO NO FISCAL —</strong>
 621 |           Este reporte es un documento informativo generado por el sistema de administración
 622 |           de Alianza Residencial y <strong>no constituye una factura fiscal ni comprobante de
 623 |           pago con validez tributaria</strong> ante la Dirección General de Ingresos (DGI) u
 624 |           otra autoridad competente. Para efectos fiscales y legales, solicite el recibo o
 625 |           factura oficial emitido al momento del pago.
 626 |         </p>
 627 |       </div>
 628 | 
 629 |       <!-- Footer -->
 630 |       <div class="doc-footer">
 631 |         <div class="doc-footer-left">
 632 |           Alianza Residencial &bull; Sistema de Administración de Propiedades<br>
 633 |           Generado el ${hoy}
 634 |         </div>
 635 |         <div class="firma-line">Firma Administración</div>
 636 |       </div>
 637 | 
 638 |     </div>`;
 639 | 
 640 |   // Cargar logo si existe
 641 |   const logoImg = new Image();
 642 |   logoImg.onload = () => {
 643 |     const box = document.getElementById('pdf-logo-box');
 644 |     if (box) box.innerHTML = `<img src="/static/logo.png" alt="Logo">`;
 645 |   };
 646 |   logoImg.src = '/static/logo.png';
 647 | }
 648 | 
 649 | /* ── Imprimir / Exportar PDF ─────────────────────────── */
 650 | function imprimirPDF() {
 651 |   const apto = document.getElementById('rep-apto').value;
 652 |   if (!apto) { showToast('Selecciona un apartamento primero','warning'); return; }
 653 |   const doc = document.getElementById('pdf-doc');
 654 |   if (!doc)  { showToast('Genera el reporte primero','warning'); return; }
 655 |   window.print();
 656 | }
 657 | 
 658 | /* ── Excel del reporte ───────────────────────────────── */
 659 | function exportarReporteExcel() {
 660 |   const res = getPagosFiltradosReporte();
 661 |   if (!res) { showToast('Selecciona un apartamento primero','warning'); return; }
 662 |   const { apto, pagos } = res;
 663 |   if (!pagos.length) { showToast('Sin datos para exportar','warning'); return; }
 664 | 
 665 |   const total   = pagos.reduce((s,p) => s+p.monto, 0);
 666 |   const headers = ['# Factura','Fecha','Apartamento','Propietario','Concepto','Monto'];
 667 |   const rows    = pagos.map(p => [p.factura, p.fecha, p.apto, p.owner_name, p.concepto, p.monto]);
 668 |   rows.push([], ['','','','','TOTAL', total]);
 669 | 
 670 |   const ws = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet([headers, ...rows]);
 671 |   ws['!cols'] = [{wch:12},{wch:12},{wch:12},{wch:28},{wch:22},{wch:12}];
 672 |   const wb = XLSX.utils.book_new();
 673 |   XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb, ws, `Apt ${apto}`);
 674 |   XLSX.writeFile(wb, `reporte_apt${apto}_${new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]}.xlsx`);
 675 |   showToast('Reporte descargado','success');
 676 | }
 677 | 
 678 | init();
 679 | </script>
 680 | </body>
 681 | </html>

 225 | let parsedOwners  = [];
 226 | let parsedCharges = [];
 227 | let allProps      = [];

 230 | async function init() {
 231 |   [allProps, allUnits] = await Promise.all([
 232 |     apiRequest('/properties') || [],
 233 |     apiRequest('/units')      || []
 234 |   ]);
 235 |   allProps = allProps || [];
 236 |   allUnits = allUnits || [];
 237 | 
 238 |   ['imp-prop-select','imp-charge-prop'].forEach(id => {
 239 |     const sel = document.getElementById(id);
 240 |     allProps.forEach(p => sel.innerHTML += `<option value="${p.id}">${p.name}</option>`);
 241 |   });
 242 | }
 243 | 
 244 | function switchTab(tab) {
 245 |   document.querySelectorAll('.imp-tab').forEach((b,i) => {
 246 |     b.classList.toggle('active', ['propietarios','cargos','exportar'][i] === tab);
 247 |   });
 248 |   document.querySelectorAll('.imp-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
 249 |   document.getElementById('panel-' + tab).classList.add('active');
 250 | }
 251 | 
 252 | // ── Helpers para leer valores de Excel de forma robusta ──
 253 | function readStr(val) {
 254 |   if (val === null || val === undefined) return '';
 255 |   return String(val).trim();
 256 | }
 257 | 
 258 | /**
 259 |  * Lee un número de una celda de Excel.
 260 |  * SheetJS a veces entrega el número directamente como float,
 261 |  * otras como string con coma o punto decimal.
 262 |  * También puede entregar 0 si la celda tiene formato de texto.
 263 |  */
 264 | function readNum(val) {
 265 |   if (val === null || val === undefined || val === '') return null;
 266 |   // Si ya es número, úsalo directamente
 267 |   if (typeof val === 'number') return val;
 268 |   // Si es string, limpiar y parsear
 269 |   const cleaned = String(val).replace(/,/g, '.').replace(/[^0-9.\-]/g, '').trim();
 270 |   const parsed = parseFloat(cleaned);
 271 |   return isNaN(parsed) ? null : parsed;
 272 | }
 273 | 
 274 | /**
 275 |  * Lee una fecha de Excel.
 276 |  * Puede venir como: objeto Date, string "YYYY-MM-DD", número serial de Excel.
 277 |  */
 278 | function readDate(val) {
 279 |   if (!val) return todayISO();
 280 |   if (val instanceof Date) return val.toISOString().split('T')[0];
 281 |   if (typeof val === 'number') {
 282 |     // Número serial de Excel → convertir con SheetJS
 283 |     const d = XLSX.SSF.parse_date_code(val);
 284 |     if (d) return `${d.y}-${String(d.m).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(d.d).padStart(2,'0')}`;
 285 |   }
 286 |   // String: puede ser "2026-03-01" o "01/03/2026"
 287 |   const s = String(val).trim();
 288 |   if (/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}/.test(s)) return s.split('T')[0];
 289 |   if (/^\d{2}\/\d{2}\/\d{4}/.test(s)) {
 290 |     const [d, m, y] = s.split('/');
 291 |     return `${y}-${m}-${d}`;
 292 |   }
 293 |   return s.split('T')[0];
 294 | }
 295 | 
 296 | // ── Manejo de archivos ────────────────────────
 297 | function handleDrop(e, type) {
 298 |   e.preventDefault();
 299 |   document.getElementById('drop-' + (type==='owners'?'owners':'charges')).classList.remove('drag-over');
 300 |   if (e.dataTransfer.files[0]) parseExcel(e.dataTransfer.files[0], type);
 301 | }
 302 | function handleFile(input, type) {
 303 |   if (input.files[0]) parseExcel(input.files[0], type);
 304 | }
 305 | 
 306 | function parseExcel(file, type) {
 307 |   const reader = new FileReader();
 308 |   reader.onload = e => {
 309 |     try {
 310 |       // raw:false → SheetJS convierte todo a string, evita problemas con fechas y números
 311 |       // cellDates:true → convierte fechas de Excel a objetos Date
 312 |       const wb   = XLSX.read(e.target.result, { type:'binary', cellDates:true, raw:false });
 313 |       const ws   = wb.Sheets[wb.SheetNames[0]];
 314 |       // defval:'' → celdas vacías retornan '' en vez de undefined
 315 |       const data = XLSX.utils.sheet_to_json(ws, { defval:'' });
 316 | 
 317 |       if (!data.length) { showToast('El archivo está vacío o no tiene datos', 'error'); return; }
 318 | 
 319 |       if (type === 'owners')  { parsedOwners = data;  previewData(data, 'owners'); }
 320 |       if (type === 'charges') { parsedCharges = data; previewData(data, 'charges'); }
 321 |     } catch(err) {
 322 |       showToast('Error al leer el archivo: ' + err.message, 'error');
 323 |       console.error(err);
 324 |     }
 325 |   };
 326 |   reader.readAsBinaryString(file);
 327 | }
 328 | 
 329 | function previewData(data, type) {
 330 |   const cols      = Object.keys(data[0]);
 331 |   const previewEl = document.getElementById('preview-' + type);
 332 |   const actionsEl = document.getElementById('import-' + type + '-actions');
 333 |   const countEl   = document.getElementById(type + '-count');
 334 | 
 335 |   previewEl.innerHTML = `
 336 |     <div style="margin-bottom:10px;">
 337 |       <span style="font-size:.82rem;color:var(--text-secondary);">
 338 |         Vista previa: <strong>${data.length} registros</strong> encontrados
 339 |       </span>
 340 |     </div>
 341 |     <div class="preview-table table-wrapper">
 342 |       <table>
 343 |         <thead><tr>${cols.map(c=>`<th>${c}</th>`).join('')}</tr></thead>
 344 |         <tbody>
 345 |           ${data.slice(0,8).map(row=>`
 346 |             <tr>${cols.map(c=>`<td style="font-size:.78rem;">${row[c]||'—'}</td>`).join('')}</tr>`).join('')}
 347 |           ${data.length>8?`<tr><td colspan="${cols.length}" style="text-align:center;color:var(--text-muted);font-size:.78rem;padding:8px;">... y ${data.length-8} registros más</td></tr>`:''}
 348 |         </tbody>
 349 |       </table>
 350 |     </div>`;
 351 | 
 352 |   if (countEl)   countEl.textContent = data.length;
 353 |   if (actionsEl) actionsEl.style.display = '';
 354 | }
 355 | 
 356 | function clearImport(type) {
 357 |   if (type === 'owners')  parsedOwners  = [];
 358 |   if (type === 'charges') parsedCharges = [];
 359 |   document.getElementById('preview-' + type).innerHTML = '';
 360 |   document.getElementById('import-' + type + '-actions').style.display = 'none';
 361 |   document.getElementById('import-' + type + '-result').innerHTML = '';
 362 |   document.getElementById('file-' + type).value = '';
 363 | }

 365 | // ── Ejecutar importación ──────────────────────
 366 | async function executeImport(type) {
 367 |   if (type === 'owners')  await importOwners();
 368 |   if (type === 'charges') await importCharges();
 369 | }

 371 | // ── Importar propietarios ─────────────────────
 372 | async function importOwners() {
 373 |   if (!parsedOwners.length) return;
 374 |   const propId   = document.getElementById('imp-prop-select').value;
 375 |   const resultEl = document.getElementById('import-owners-result');
 376 |   let ok = 0, err = 0, errs = [];
 377 | 
 378 |   resultEl.innerHTML = `<div style="text-align:center;padding:1rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 379 |     <i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Importando...</div>`;
 380 | 
 381 |   // Refrescar owners y units desde la BD
 382 |   const [owners, units] = await Promise.all([
 383 |     apiRequest('/owners'), apiRequest('/units')
 384 |   ]);
 385 |   const localOwners = owners || [];
 386 |   const localUnits  = units  || [];
 387 | 
 388 |   for (const row of parsedOwners) {
 389 |     try {
 390 |       const name     = readStr(row['nombre_propietario'] || row['nombre']);
 391 |       const cedula   = readStr(row['cedula'] || row['identificacion']);
 392 |       const email    = readStr(row['email'])    || null;
 393 |       const phone    = readStr(row['telefono']) || null;
 394 |       const aptNum   = readStr(row['numero_apartamento'] || row['apartamento']);
 395 |       const propName = readStr(row['nombre_propiedad']   || row['propiedad']);
 396 |       const piso     = readStr(row['piso']) || null;
 397 | 
 398 |       if (!name) { errs.push('Fila sin nombre de propietario'); err++; continue; }
 399 | 
 400 |       // 1. Crear o encontrar propietario
 401 |       let owner = (cedula ? localOwners.find(o => o.identification === cedula) : null)
 402 |                || localOwners.find(o => o.full_name.toLowerCase() === name.toLowerCase());
 403 | 
 404 |       if (!owner) {
 405 |         owner = await apiRequest('/owners/', 'POST', {
 406 |           full_name: name, identification: cedula || null, email, phone
 407 |         });
 408 |         if (!owner) { err++; errs.push(`Error creando propietario: ${name}`); continue; }
 409 |         localOwners.push(owner);
 410 |       }
 411 | 
 412 |       // 2. Resolver propiedad
 413 |       const targetPropId = propId
 414 |         || allProps.find(p => p.name.toLowerCase() === propName.toLowerCase())?.id
 415 |         || allProps.find(p => p.name.toLowerCase().includes(propName.toLowerCase()))?.id;
 416 | 
 417 |       if (!targetPropId && aptNum) {
 418 |         err++; errs.push(`Propiedad no encontrada para ${name} (${propName})`); continue;
 419 |       }
 420 | 
 421 |       // 3. Crear o encontrar unidad
 422 |       if (aptNum && targetPropId) {
 423 |         let unit = localUnits.find(u =>
 424 |           u.unit_number === aptNum && u.property_id === parseInt(targetPropId)
 425 |         );
 426 |         if (!unit) {
 427 |           unit = await apiRequest('/units/', 'POST', {
 428 |             property_id: parseInt(targetPropId), unit_number: aptNum, floor: piso
 429 |           });
 430 |           if (!unit) { err++; errs.push(`Error creando unidad ${aptNum}`); continue; }
 431 |           localUnits.push(unit);
 432 |           allUnits.push(unit);
 433 |         }
 434 | 
 435 |         // 4. Asignar propietario a unidad
 436 |         await apiRequest('/unit-owners/', 'POST', {
 437 |           unit_id: unit.id, owner_id: owner.id, start_date: todayISO()
 438 |         }).catch(() => null);
 439 |       }
 440 | 
 441 |       ok++;
 442 |     } catch(e) {
 443 |       err++; errs.push(`Error: ${e.message}`);
 444 |     }
 445 |   }
 446 | 
 447 |   showResult('owners', ok, err, errs);
 448 |   if (ok > 0) showToast(`${ok} propietarios importados`, 'success');
 449 | }
 450 | 
 451 | // ── Importar cargos ───────────────────────────
 452 | async function importCharges() {
 453 |   if (!parsedCharges.length) return;
 454 | 
 455 |   const resultEl = document.getElementById('import-charges-result');
 456 |   let ok = 0, err = 0, errs = [];
 457 | 
 458 |   resultEl.innerHTML = `<div style="text-align:center;padding:1rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 459 |     <i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Importando ${parsedCharges.length} cargos...</div>`;
 460 | 
 461 |   // Refrescar unidades
 462 |   const units = await apiRequest('/units') || [];
 463 | 
 464 |   for (const row of parsedCharges) {
 465 |     try {
 466 |       const aptNum   = readStr(row['numero_apartamento'] || row['apartamento']);
 467 |       const desc     = readStr(row['descripcion']        || row['description']);
 468 |       const amount   = readNum(row['monto']              || row['amount']     || row['Monto']);
 469 |       const propName = readStr(row['nombre_propiedad']   || row['propiedad']  || '');
 470 | 
 471 |       const dateCreated = readDate(row['fecha_creacion'] || row['fecha']);
 472 |       const dueDate     = readDate(row['fecha_vencimiento'] || row['vencimiento'] || row['fecha_creacion'] || row['fecha']);
 473 | 
 474 |       // Validaciones
 475 |       if (!aptNum) { errs.push(`Fila sin número de apartamento`); err++; continue; }
 476 |       if (!desc)   { errs.push(`Apt ${aptNum}: sin descripción`);  err++; continue; }
 477 |       if (amount === null || amount <= 0) {
 478 |         errs.push(`Apt ${aptNum} (${desc}): monto inválido → "${row['monto'] ?? row['amount']}"`);
 479 |         err++; continue;
 480 |       }
 481 | 
 482 |       // Resolver propiedad
 483 |       let targetPropId = readStr(document.getElementById('imp-charge-prop').value);
 484 | 
 485 |       if (!targetPropId && propName) {
 486 |         const found = allProps.find(p =>
 487 |           p.name.toLowerCase() === propName.toLowerCase() ||
 488 |           p.name.toLowerCase().includes(propName.toLowerCase())
 489 |         );
 490 |         if (found) targetPropId = String(found.id);
 491 |       }
 492 | 
 493 |       if (!targetPropId) {
 494 |         errs.push(`Apt ${aptNum}: no se encontró propiedad "${propName}"`);
 495 |         err++; continue;
 496 |       }
 497 | 
 498 |       // Encontrar unidad
 499 |       const unit = units.find(u =>
 500 |         u.unit_number === aptNum && u.property_id === parseInt(targetPropId)
 501 |       );
 502 | 
 503 |       if (!unit) {
 504 |         errs.push(`Unidad "${aptNum}" no encontrada en la propiedad seleccionada`);
 505 |         err++; continue;
 506 |       }
 507 | 
 508 |       // Crear cargo
 509 |       const r = await apiRequest('/charges/', 'POST', {
 510 |         unit_id:      unit.id,
 511 |         description:  desc,
 512 |         amount:       amount,
 513 |         date_created: dateCreated,
 514 |         due_date:     dueDate,
 515 |       });
 516 | 
 517 |       if (!r) { err++; errs.push(`Error del servidor creando cargo para apt ${aptNum}`); }
 518 |       else ok++;
 519 | 
 520 |     } catch(e) {
 521 |       err++; errs.push(`Error inesperado: ${e.message}`);
 522 |     }
 523 |   }
 524 | 
 525 |   showResult('charges', ok, err, errs);
 526 |   if (ok > 0) showToast(`${ok} cargos creados correctamente`, 'success');
 527 | }
 528 | 
 529 | // ── Mostrar resultado ─────────────────────────
 530 | function showResult(type, ok, err, errs) {
 531 |   const resultEl = document.getElementById('import-' + type + '-result');
 532 |   resultEl.innerHTML = `
 533 |     <div style="margin-top:12px;padding:14px;border-radius:var(--radius-md);
 534 |       background:${ok>0?'var(--success-bg)':'var(--danger-bg)'};
 535 |       border:1px solid ${ok>0?'var(--success-brd)':'var(--danger-brd)'};">
 536 |       <div class="result-ok"><i class="fas fa-check-circle"></i> <strong>${ok}</strong> registros importados correctamente</div>
 537 |       ${err>0?`<div class="result-err" style="margin-top:4px;"><i class="fas fa-exclamation-circle"></i> <strong>${err}</strong> errores</div>`:''}
 538 |       ${errs.slice(0,8).map(e=>`<div style="font-size:.76rem;color:var(--danger);margin-top:3px;">· ${e}</div>`).join('')}
 539 |       ${errs.length>8?`<div style="font-size:.74rem;color:var(--text-muted);margin-top:4px;">... y ${errs.length-8} errores más</div>`:''}
 540 |     </div>`;
 541 | }
 542 | 
 543 | // ── Descargar plantillas ──────────────────────
 544 | function downloadTemplate(type) {
 545 |   let headers, example, filename;
 546 |   if (type === 'propietarios') {
 547 |     headers = ['nombre_propietario','cedula','email','telefono','nombre_propiedad','numero_apartamento','piso'];
 548 |     example = ['Juan Pérez','8-123-456','juan@email.com','+507 6000-0000','Torre Alianza I','101','1'];
 549 |     filename = 'plantilla_propietarios.xlsx';
 550 |   } else {
 551 |     headers = ['numero_apartamento','descripcion','monto','fecha_creacion','fecha_vencimiento','nombre_propiedad'];
 552 |     example = ['1-A','GAS Marzo 2026',56.54,'2026-03-01','2026-03-31','PARK VIEW'];
 553 |     filename = 'plantilla_cargos.xlsx';
 554 |   }
 555 |   const ws = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet([headers, example]);
 556 |   const wb = XLSX.utils.book_new();
 557 |   XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb, ws, 'Datos');
 558 |   XLSX.writeFile(wb, filename);
 559 | }
 560 | 
 561 | // ── Exportar datos ────────────────────────────
 562 | async function exportData(type) {
 563 |   showToast('Generando archivo...', 'success');
 564 |   let rows = [], headers = [], filename = '';
 565 | 
 566 |   if (type === 'propietarios') {
 567 |     const [owners, unitOwners, units, props] = await Promise.all([
 568 |       apiRequest('/owners'), apiRequest('/unit-owners/all'),
 569 |       apiRequest('/units'),  apiRequest('/properties')
 570 |     ]);
 571 |     headers  = ['ID','Nombre','Cédula','Email','Teléfono','Unidad','Propiedad'];
 572 |     rows     = (owners||[]).map(o => {
 573 |       const uo = (unitOwners||[]).find(x => x.owner_id===o.id && x.is_active);
 574 |       const u  = uo ? (units||[]).find(x=>x.id===uo.unit_id) : null;
 575 |       const p  = u  ? (props||[]).find(x=>x.id===u.property_id) : null;
 576 |       return [o.id, o.full_name, o.identification||'', o.email||'', o.phone||'',
 577 |               u?`Apt. ${u.unit_number}`:'', p?p.name:''];
 578 |     });
 579 |     filename = 'propietarios_alianza.xlsx';
 580 |   } else if (type === 'cargos') {
 581 |     const charges = await apiRequest('/finance/charges') || [];
 582 |     headers  = ['ID','Propietario','Unidad','Descripción','Vencimiento','Total','Saldo','Estado'];
 583 |     rows     = charges.map(c=>[c.id,c.owner_name||'',c.unit_number||'',
 584 |       c.description,c.due_date,c.amount,c.balance,c.status]);
 585 |     filename = 'cargos_alianza.xlsx';
 586 |   } else if (type === 'proveedores') {
 587 |     const suppliers = await apiRequest('/suppliers') || [];
 588 |     headers  = ['ID','Nombre','Categoría','RUC','Teléfono','Email','Total Pagado','Pendiente'];
 589 |     rows     = suppliers.map(s=>[s.id,s.name,s.category,s.ruc||'',
 590 |       s.phone||'',s.email||'',s.total_paid,s.total_pending]);
 591 |     filename = 'proveedores_alianza.xlsx';
 592 |   }
 593 | 
 594 |   const ws = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet([headers, ...rows]);
 595 |   const wb = XLSX.utils.book_new();
 596 |   XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb, ws, 'Datos');
 597 |   XLSX.writeFile(wb, filename);
 598 |   showToast('Archivo descargado', 'success');
 599 | }
 600 | 
 601 | init();
 602 | </script>
 603 | </body>
 604 | </html>

 100 | renderSidebar('index');

 102 | async function loadDashboard() {
 103 |   const [props, units, owners, charges, agendaEvents] = await Promise.all([
 104 |     apiRequest('/properties'),
 105 |     apiRequest('/units'),
 106 |     apiRequest('/owners'),
 107 |     apiRequest('/finance/charges'),
 108 |     apiRequest('/agenda/upcoming'),
 109 |   ]);
 110 | 
 111 |   document.getElementById('stat-props').textContent  = props?.length  ?? '—';
 112 |   document.getElementById('stat-units').textContent  = units?.length  ?? '—';
 113 |   document.getElementById('stat-owners').textContent = owners?.length ?? '—';
 114 | 
 115 |   // Stats financieras
 116 |   if (charges) {
 117 |     const pending = charges.filter(c => c.status !== 'PAGADO').reduce((s,c) => s + parseFloat(c.balance||0), 0);
 118 |     document.getElementById('stat-pending').textContent = `$${formatMoney(pending)}`;
 119 | 
 120 |     const list = document.getElementById('activity-list');
 121 |     const pendingCharges = charges.filter(c => c.status !== 'PAGADO').slice(0, 6);
 122 |     if (!pendingCharges.length) {
 123 |       list.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state"><i class="fas fa-check-circle" style="color:var(--success)"></i><p>¡Sin cargos pendientes!</p></div>`;
 124 |     } else {
 125 |       list.innerHTML = pendingCharges.map(c => `
 126 |         <div class="activity-item">
 127 |           <span class="activity-dot" style="background:${c.status==='PARCIAL'?'var(--warning)':'var(--danger)'}"></span>
 128 |           <div class="activity-content">
 129 |             <div class="activity-title"><strong>${c.owner_name||'Sin propietario'}</strong>${c.unit_number?` · Apt. ${c.unit_number}`:''}</div>
 130 |             <div class="activity-time">${c.description}</div>
 131 |           </div>
 132 |           <span class="badge badge-${c.status}">${c.status}</span>
 133 |           <div class="activity-value">$${formatMoney(c.balance)}</div>
 134 |         </div>`).join('');
 135 |     }
 136 |   }
 137 | 
 138 |   // Agenda de la semana
 139 |   const agList = document.getElementById('agenda-list');
 140 |   if (!agendaEvents?.length) {
 141 |     agList.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state" style="padding:1.5rem;"><i class="fas fa-calendar-check" style="font-size:1.8rem;"></i><p>Sin eventos próximos esta semana</p></div>`;
 142 |   } else {
 143 |     const typeIcon = { CITA:'fa-handshake', EVENTO:'fa-landmark', TAREA:'fa-check-square' };
 144 |     agList.innerHTML = agendaEvents.map(e => `
 145 |       <div class="agenda-item">
 146 |         <div class="agenda-type-dot dot-${e.event_type}"></div>
 147 |         <div class="agenda-info">
 148 |           <strong>${e.title}</strong>
 149 |           <span>${e.event_type}${e.event_time?' · '+e.event_time:''}${e.location?' · '+e.location:''}</span>
 150 |         </div>
 151 |         <div class="agenda-date">${formatDate(e.event_date)}</div>
 152 |       </div>`).join('');
 153 |   }
 154 | }

 156 |     <script>
 157 |         // ── Claves de localStorage (deben coincidir con Auth en main.js) ──
 158 |         const TOKEN_KEY = 'alianza_token';
 159 |         const USER_KEY  = 'alianza_user';
 160 |         const ROLE_KEY  = 'alianza_role';
 161 | 
 162 |         // ── Redirección según rol ──────────────────────────────────────────
 163 |         function redirectByRole(role) {
 164 |             if (role === 'GARITA') {
 165 |                 window.location.href = '/static/garita.html';
 166 |             } else {
 167 |                 window.location.href = '/static/index.html';
 168 |             }
 169 |         }
 170 | 
 171 |         // ── Si ya hay sesión activa, redirigir directo ────────────────────
 172 |         const existingToken = localStorage.getItem(TOKEN_KEY);
 173 |         const existingRole  = localStorage.getItem(ROLE_KEY);
 174 |         if (existingToken && existingRole) {
 175 |             redirectByRole(existingRole);
 176 |         }
 177 | 
 178 |         // ── Formulario de login ───────────────────────────────────────────
 179 |         document.getElementById('loginForm').addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
 180 |             e.preventDefault();
 181 | 
 182 |             const username  = document.getElementById('username').value.trim();
 183 |             const password  = document.getElementById('password').value;
 184 |             const alertEl   = document.getElementById('alertMessage');
 185 |             const alertText = document.getElementById('alertText');
 186 |             const loginBtn  = document.getElementById('loginBtn');
 187 | 
 188 |             if (!username || !password) {
 189 |                 alertText.innerText = 'Usuario y contraseña son requeridos';
 190 |                 alertEl.className   = 'alert alert-error';
 191 |                 alertEl.style.display = 'flex';
 192 |                 return;
 193 |             }
 194 | 
 195 |             loginBtn.disabled = true;
 196 |             loginBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Iniciando sesión...';
 197 |             alertEl.style.display = 'none';
 198 | 
 199 |             try {
 200 |                 const response = await fetch('/api/auth/login', {
 201 |                     method: 'POST',
 202 |                     headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
 203 |                     body: JSON.stringify({ username, password })
 204 |                 });
 205 | 
 206 |                 const data = await response.json();
 207 | 
 208 |                 if (!response.ok) {
 209 |                     throw new Error(data.detail || 'Usuario o contraseña incorrectos');
 210 |                 }
 211 | 
 212 |                 // ── Guardar con las mismas claves que usa Auth en main.js ──
 213 |                 localStorage.setItem(TOKEN_KEY, data.access_token);
 214 |                 localStorage.setItem(USER_KEY,  data.username);
 215 |                 localStorage.setItem(ROLE_KEY,  data.role || 'USER');
 216 | 
 217 |                 // ── Mostrar mensaje de éxito ───────────────────────────────
 218 |                 alertEl.className = 'alert alert-success';
 219 |                 const roleLabel = data.role === 'GARITA' ? 'Seguridad Garita'
 220 |                                 : data.role === 'ADMIN'  ? 'Administrador'
 221 |                                 : 'Usuario';
 222 |                 alertText.innerText = `¡Bienvenido, ${data.username}! (${roleLabel}) Redirigiendo...`;
 223 |                 alertEl.style.display = 'flex';
 224 | 
 225 |                 // ── Redirigir según el rol ─────────────────────────────────
 226 |                 setTimeout(() => {
 227 |                     redirectByRole(data.role);
 228 |                 }, 900);
 229 | 
 230 |             } catch (error) {
 231 |                 alertEl.className = 'alert alert-error';
 232 |                 alertText.innerText = error.message;
 233 |                 alertEl.style.display = 'flex';
 234 |                 loginBtn.disabled = false;
 235 |                 loginBtn.innerHTML = '<span>Iniciar Sesión</span> <i class="fas fa-arrow-right"></i>';
 236 |             }
 237 |         });
 238 |     </script>
 239 | </body>
 240 | </html>

 105 | async function loadTable() {
 106 |   const [owners, unitOwners, units] = await Promise.all([
 107 |     apiRequest('/owners'),
 108 |     apiRequest('/unit-owners/all').catch(() => null),
 109 |     apiRequest('/units'),
 110 |   ]);
 111 | 
 112 |   allOwnersCache = owners || [];
 113 |   document.getElementById('owner-count').textContent = allOwnersCache.length;
 114 | 
 115 |   // Fill stmt select
 116 |   const stmtSel = document.getElementById('stmt-owner');
 117 |   stmtSel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Seleccione propietario</option>';
 118 |   allOwnersCache.forEach(o => stmtSel.innerHTML += `<option value="${o.id}">${o.full_name}</option>`);
 119 | 
 120 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('owners-table');
 121 | 
 122 |   if (!allOwnersCache.length) {
 123 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin propietarios registrados</td></tr>`;
 124 |     return;
 125 |   }
 126 | 
 127 |   // Build unit per owner from unit-owners
 128 |   const unitMap = {};
 129 |   if (unitOwners && Array.isArray(unitOwners)) {
 130 |     unitOwners.filter(uo => uo.is_active).forEach(uo => {
 131 |       const u = (units || []).find(x => x.id === uo.unit_id);
 132 |       if (u) unitMap[uo.owner_id] = `Apt. ${u.unit_number}`;
 133 |     });
 134 |   }
 135 | 
 136 |   tbody.innerHTML = allOwnersCache.map(o => `
 137 |     <tr>
 138 |       <td class="td-mono">${o.id}</td>
 139 |       <td><strong>${o.full_name}</strong></td>
 140 |       <td style="color:var(--text-secondary);font-size:.82rem;">${o.identification || '—'}</td>
 141 |       <td style="font-size:.82rem;">
 142 |         ${o.email ? `<div><i class="fas fa-envelope" style="opacity:.5;margin-right:4px;"></i>${o.email}</div>` : ''}
 143 |         ${o.phone ? `<div><i class="fas fa-phone" style="opacity:.5;margin-right:4px;"></i>${o.phone}</div>` : ''}
 144 |         ${!o.email && !o.phone ? '—' : ''}
 145 |       </td>
 146 |       <td>
 147 |         ${unitMap[o.id]
 148 |           ? `<span class="badge badge-success">${unitMap[o.id]}</span>`
 149 |           : `<em style="color:var(--text-muted);font-size:.82rem;">Sin unidad</em>`}
 150 |       </td>
 151 |       <td>
 152 |         <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="editOwner(${o.id})">
 153 |           <i class="fas fa-pencil-alt"></i>
 154 |         </button>
 155 |       </td>
 156 |     </tr>`).join('');
 157 | }
 158 | 
 159 | async function saveOwner() {
 160 |   const name = document.getElementById('full_name').value.trim();
 161 |   if (!name) { showToast('El nombre es obligatorio', 'error'); return; }
 162 | 
 163 |   const data = {
 164 |     full_name:      name,
 165 |     identification: document.getElementById('identification').value.trim() || null,
 166 |     email:          document.getElementById('email').value.trim() || null,
 167 |     phone:          document.getElementById('phone').value.trim() || null,
 168 |   };
 169 | 
 170 |   let result;
 171 |   if (editingId) {
 172 |     result = await apiRequest(`/owners/${editingId}`, 'PUT', data);
 173 |     if (result) showToast('Propietario actualizado');
 174 |   } else {
 175 |     result = await apiRequest('/owners/', 'POST', data);
 176 |     if (result) showToast('Propietario creado correctamente');
 177 |   }
 178 | 
 179 |   if (result) { cancelEdit(); loadTable(); }
 180 | }
 181 | 
 182 | function editOwner(id) {
 183 |   const o = allOwnersCache.find(x => x.id === id);
 184 |   if (!o) return;
 185 | 
 186 |   editingId = id;
 187 |   document.getElementById('owner-id').value        = id;
 188 |   document.getElementById('full_name').value        = o.full_name;
 189 |   document.getElementById('identification').value   = o.identification || '';
 190 |   document.getElementById('email').value            = o.email || '';
 191 |   document.getElementById('phone').value            = o.phone || '';
 192 |   document.getElementById('form-title').textContent = 'Editar Propietario';
 193 |   document.getElementById('btn-label').textContent  = 'Actualizar';
 194 |   document.getElementById('btn-cancel').style.display = '';
 195 |   window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
 196 | }
 197 | 
 198 | function cancelEdit() {
 199 |   editingId = null;
 200 |   ['owner-id','full_name','identification','email','phone'].forEach(id => {
 201 |     document.getElementById(id).value = '';
 202 |   });
 203 |   document.getElementById('form-title').textContent = 'Nuevo Propietario';
 204 |   document.getElementById('btn-label').textContent  = 'Guardar Propietario';
 205 |   document.getElementById('btn-cancel').style.display = 'none';
 206 | }
 207 | 
 208 | function openStatement() {
 209 |   const ownerId = document.getElementById('stmt-owner').value;
 210 |   if (!ownerId) { showToast('Selecciona un propietario', 'warning'); return; }
 211 |   window.open(`/static/estado_cuenta.html?owner_id=${ownerId}`, '_blank');
 212 | }
 213 | 
 214 | loadTable();
 215 | </script>
 216 | </body>
 217 | </html>

  26 |           <h3><i class="fas fa-plus-circle"></i> <span id="form-title">Nueva Propiedad</span></h3>
  27 |           <button class="btn btn-muted btn-sm" id="btn-cancel" onclick="cancelEdit()" style="display:none;">
  28 |             <i class="fas fa-times"></i> Cancelar
  29 |           </button>
  30 |         </div>
  31 |         <div class="card-body">
  32 |           <input type="hidden" id="prop-id">
  33 | 
  34 |           <label class="field-label">Nombre</label>
  35 |           <input type="text" id="name" placeholder="Ej: Torre Alianza I">
  36 | 
  37 |           <label class="field-label">Tipo</label>
  38 |           <select id="type">
  39 |             <option value="">Seleccione tipo</option>
  40 |             <option value="PH">Penthouse (PH)</option>
  41 |             <option value="EDIFICIO">Edificio</option>
  42 |             <option value="CASA">Casa</option>
  43 |             <option value="LOCAL">Local Comercial</option>
  44 |           </select>
  45 | 
  46 |           <label class="field-label">Dirección</label>
  47 |           <input type="text" id="address" placeholder="Ej: Av. Balboa, Ciudad de Panamá">
  48 | 
  49 |           <label class="field-label">Máximo de unidades</label>
  50 |           <input type="number" id="max_units" value="50" min="1">
  51 | 
  52 |           <button onclick="saveProperty()">
  53 |             <i class="fas fa-save"></i> <span id="btn-label">Guardar Propiedad</span>
  54 |           </button>
  55 |         </div>
  56 |       </div>

  90 | renderHeader('properties');

  92 | let editingId = null;
  93 | let allUnitsCache = [];
  94 | 
  95 | async function loadTable() {
  96 |   const [props, units] = await Promise.all([
  97 |     apiRequest('/properties'),
  98 |     apiRequest('/units'),
  99 |   ]);
 100 | 
 101 |   allUnitsCache = units || [];
 102 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('props-table');
 103 |   document.getElementById('prop-count').textContent = props?.length ?? 0;
 104 | 
 105 |   if (!props?.length) {
 106 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 107 |       <i class="fas fa-building" style="font-size:1.5rem;opacity:.3;display:block;margin-bottom:.5rem;"></i>
 108 |       Sin propiedades registradas</td></tr>`;
 109 |     return;
 110 |   }
 111 | 
 112 |   tbody.innerHTML = props.map(p => {
 113 |     const unitCount = allUnitsCache.filter(u => u.property_id === p.id).length;
 114 |     return `<tr>
 115 |       <td class="td-mono">${p.id}</td>
 116 |       <td><strong>${p.name}</strong></td>
 117 |       <td><span class="badge badge-primary">${p.type}</span></td>
 118 |       <td style="color:var(--text-secondary);font-size:.83rem;">${p.address}</td>
 119 |       <td>${unitCount} / ${p.max_units}</td>
 120 |       <td>
 121 |         <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="editProperty(${p.id})">
 122 |           <i class="fas fa-pencil-alt"></i>
 123 |         </button>
 124 |       </td>
 125 |     </tr>`;
 126 |   }).join('');
 127 | }
 128 | 
 129 | async function saveProperty() {
 130 |   const name     = document.getElementById('name').value.trim();
 131 |   const type     = document.getElementById('type').value;
 132 |   const address  = document.getElementById('address').value.trim();
 133 |   const maxUnits = parseInt(document.getElementById('max_units').value);
 134 | 
 135 |   if (!name || !type || !address) {
 136 |     showToast('Completa todos los campos obligatorios', 'error'); return;
 137 |   }
 138 | 
 139 |   const data = { name, type, address, max_units: maxUnits };
 140 | 
 141 |   let result;
 142 |   if (editingId) {
 143 |     result = await apiRequest(`/properties/${editingId}`, 'PUT', data);
 144 |     if (result) showToast('Propiedad actualizada correctamente');
 145 |   } else {
 146 |     result = await apiRequest('/properties/', 'POST', data);
 147 |     if (result) showToast('Propiedad creada correctamente');
 148 |   }
 149 | 
 150 |   if (result) { cancelEdit(); loadTable(); }
 151 | }
 152 | 
 153 | async function editProperty(id) {
 154 |   const props = await apiRequest('/properties') || [];
 155 |   const p = props.find(x => x.id === id);
 156 |   if (!p) return;
 157 | 
 158 |   editingId = id;
 159 |   document.getElementById('prop-id').value    = id;
 160 |   document.getElementById('name').value        = p.name;
 161 |   document.getElementById('type').value        = p.type;
 162 |   document.getElementById('address').value     = p.address;
 163 |   document.getElementById('max_units').value   = p.max_units;
 164 |   document.getElementById('form-title').textContent = 'Editar Propiedad';
 165 |   document.getElementById('btn-label').textContent  = 'Actualizar';
 166 |   document.getElementById('btn-cancel').style.display = '';
 167 |   window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
 168 | }
 169 | 
 170 | function cancelEdit() {
 171 |   editingId = null;
 172 |   document.getElementById('prop-id').value       = '';
 173 |   document.getElementById('name').value           = '';
 174 |   document.getElementById('type').value           = '';
 175 |   document.getElementById('address').value        = '';
 176 |   document.getElementById('max_units').value      = 50;
 177 |   document.getElementById('form-title').textContent = 'Nueva Propiedad';
 178 |   document.getElementById('btn-label').textContent  = 'Guardar Propiedad';
 179 |   document.getElementById('btn-cancel').style.display = 'none';
 180 | }
 181 | 
 182 | loadTable();
 183 | </script>
 184 | </body>
 185 | </html>

 229 | function switchTab(tab) {
 230 |   document.querySelectorAll('.rep-tab').forEach((b,i) => {
 231 |     b.classList.toggle('active', ['cargos','pagos','propietarios','proveedores'][i] === tab);
 232 |   });
 233 |   document.querySelectorAll('.rep-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
 234 |   document.getElementById('panel-' + tab).classList.add('active');
 235 | }
 236 | 
 237 | async function init() {
 238 |   // Cargar props para filtro
 239 |   const props = await apiRequest('/properties') || [];
 240 |   const repProp = document.getElementById('rep-prop');
 241 |   props.forEach(p => repProp.innerHTML += `<option value="${p.id}">${p.name}</option>`);
 242 | 
 243 |   // Cargar owners para filtro
 244 |   const owners = await apiRequest('/owners') || [];
 245 |   const repOwner = document.getElementById('rep-owner');
 246 |   owners.forEach(o => repOwner.innerHTML += `<option value="${o.id}">${o.full_name}</option>`);
 247 | 
 248 |   // Cargar categorías proveedores
 249 |   const cats = await apiRequest('/suppliers/categories') || [];
 250 |   const repCat = document.getElementById('rep-cat');
 251 |   cats.forEach(c => repCat.innerHTML += `<option value="${c}">${c}</option>`);
 252 | 
 253 |   // Mes actual
 254 |   const now = new Date();
 255 |   document.getElementById('rep-month').value = `${now.getFullYear()}-${String(now.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')}`;
 256 | 
 257 |   await loadReportCargos();
 258 |   await loadReportProveedores();
 259 | }
 260 | 
 261 | // ── Reporte de cargos ──────────────────────────
 262 | async function loadReportCargos() {
 263 |   const charges = await apiRequest('/finance/charges') || [];
 264 |   const propId  = document.getElementById('rep-prop').value;
 265 |   const status  = document.getElementById('rep-status').value;
 266 |   const from    = document.getElementById('rep-from').value;
 267 |   const to      = document.getElementById('rep-to').value;
 268 | 
 269 |   let filtered = charges;
 270 |   if (status)  filtered = filtered.filter(c => c.status === status);
 271 |   if (from)    filtered = filtered.filter(c => c.due_date >= from);
 272 |   if (to)      filtered = filtered.filter(c => c.due_date <= to);
 273 | 
 274 |   // Resumen
 275 |   const total    = filtered.reduce((s,c) => s + parseFloat(c.amount||0), 0);
 276 |   const pagado   = filtered.reduce((s,c) => s + (parseFloat(c.amount||0) - parseFloat(c.balance||0)), 0);
 277 |   const pendiente= filtered.reduce((s,c) => s + parseFloat(c.balance||0), 0);
 278 |   const pendCount= filtered.filter(c => c.status !== 'PAGADO').length;
 279 | 
 280 |   document.getElementById('cargos-summary').innerHTML = `
 281 |     <div class="sum-card"><div class="sum-val">${filtered.length}</div><div class="sum-lbl">Cargos totales</div></div>
 282 |     <div class="sum-card"><div class="sum-val">$${formatMoney(total)}</div><div class="sum-lbl">Facturado</div></div>
 283 |     <div class="sum-card"><div class="sum-val" style="color:var(--success)">$${formatMoney(pagado)}</div><div class="sum-lbl">Cobrado</div></div>
 284 |     <div class="sum-card"><div class="sum-val" style="color:var(--danger)">$${formatMoney(pendiente)}</div><div class="sum-lbl">Por cobrar</div></div>
 285 |     <div class="sum-card"><div class="sum-val" style="color:var(--warning)">${pendCount}</div><div class="sum-lbl">Cargos pendientes</div></div>`;
 286 | 
 287 |   document.getElementById('cargos-count').textContent = filtered.length;
 288 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('cargos-tbody');
 289 | 
 290 |   if (!filtered.length) {
 291 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin resultados</td></tr>`;
 292 |     return;
 293 |   }
 294 | 
 295 |   tbody.innerHTML = filtered.map(c => `
 296 |     <tr>
 297 |       <td><strong>${c.owner_name || '—'}</strong></td>
 298 |       <td>${c.unit_number || '—'}</td>
 299 |       <td>${c.description}</td>
 300 |       <td>${formatDate(c.due_date)}</td>
 301 |       <td class="td-right">$${formatMoney(c.amount)}</td>
 302 |       <td class="td-right" style="color:var(--success);">$${formatMoney(parseFloat(c.amount||0)-parseFloat(c.balance||0))}</td>
 303 |       <td class="td-right" style="color:var(--danger);font-weight:700;">$${formatMoney(c.balance)}</td>
 304 |       <td><span class="badge badge-${c.status}">${c.status}</span></td>
 305 |     </tr>`).join('');
 306 | }
 307 | 
 308 | // ── Reporte de pagos ───────────────────────────
 309 | async function loadReportPagos() {
 310 |   // Usamos charges para obtener pagos aplicados
 311 |   const charges = await apiRequest('/finance/charges') || [];
 312 |   const month = document.getElementById('rep-month').value;
 313 | 
 314 |   // Filtrar por mes si se especificó
 315 |   // Como no hay endpoint de pagos por mes, mostramos todos los cargos pagados en ese periodo
 316 |   const filtered = month
 317 |     ? charges.filter(c => c.status === 'PAGADO' || c.status === 'PARCIAL')
 318 |     : charges.filter(c => c.status !== 'PENDIENTE');
 319 | 
 320 |   const totalCobrado = filtered.reduce((s,c) => s + (parseFloat(c.amount||0) - parseFloat(c.balance||0)), 0);
 321 | 
 322 |   document.getElementById('pagos-summary').innerHTML = `
 323 |     <div class="sum-card"><div class="sum-val">${filtered.length}</div><div class="sum-lbl">Cargos con pago</div></div>
 324 |     <div class="sum-card"><div class="sum-val" style="color:var(--success)">$${formatMoney(totalCobrado)}</div><div class="sum-lbl">Total cobrado</div></div>`;
 325 | 
 326 |   document.getElementById('pagos-count').textContent = filtered.length;
 327 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('pagos-tbody');
 328 | 
 329 |   if (!filtered.length) {
 330 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin pagos en este período</td></tr>`;
 331 |     return;
 332 |   }
 333 | 
 334 |   tbody.innerHTML = filtered.map((c,i) => `
 335 |     <tr>
 336 |       <td class="td-mono">${i+1}</td>
 337 |       <td><strong>${c.owner_name || '—'}</strong><br><small style="color:var(--text-muted);">Apt. ${c.unit_number||'?'}</small></td>
 338 |       <td>${formatDate(c.due_date)}</td>
 339 |       <td style="color:var(--text-muted);font-size:.8rem;">—</td>
 340 |       <td class="td-right"><strong>$${formatMoney(parseFloat(c.amount||0)-parseFloat(c.balance||0))}</strong></td>
 341 |       <td><span class="badge badge-${c.status}">${c.status}</span> — ${c.description}</td>
 342 |     </tr>`).join('');
 343 | }
 344 | 
 345 | // ── Reporte por propietario ────────────────────
 346 | async function loadReportOwner() {
 347 |   const ownerId = document.getElementById('rep-owner').value;
 348 |   if (!ownerId) return;
 349 | 
 350 |   const charges = await apiRequest(`/finance/owner-statement/${ownerId}`) || [];
 351 |   const owners  = await apiRequest('/owners') || [];
 352 |   const owner   = owners.find(o => o.id === parseInt(ownerId));
 353 | 
 354 |   const total     = charges.reduce((s,c) => s + c.total, 0);
 355 |   const pagado    = charges.reduce((s,c) => s + c.paid, 0);
 356 |   const pendiente = charges.reduce((s,c) => s + c.balance, 0);
 357 | 
 358 |   const content = document.getElementById('owner-report-content');
 359 |   content.innerHTML = `
 360 |     <div class="summary-row">
 361 |       <div class="sum-card"><div class="sum-val">${charges.length}</div><div class="sum-lbl">Cargos totales</div></div>
 362 |       <div class="sum-card"><div class="sum-val">$${formatMoney(total)}</div><div class="sum-lbl">Facturado</div></div>
 363 |       <div class="sum-card"><div class="sum-val" style="color:var(--success)">$${formatMoney(pagado)}</div><div class="sum-lbl">Pagado</div></div>
 364 |       <div class="sum-card"><div class="sum-val" style="color:var(--danger)">$${formatMoney(pendiente)}</div><div class="sum-lbl">Pendiente</div></div>
 365 |     </div>
 366 |     <div class="card">
 367 |       <div class="card-header">
 368 |         <h3><i class="fas fa-user"></i> ${owner?.full_name || 'Propietario'} — Estado de cuenta completo</h3>
 369 |         <button class="btn print-btn" onclick="window.open('/static/estado_cuenta.html?owner_id=${ownerId}','_blank')">
 370 |           <i class="fas fa-external-link-alt"></i> Ver Estado de Cuenta
 371 |         </button>
 372 |       </div>
 373 |       <div class="table-wrapper">
 374 |         <table>
 375 |           <thead>
 376 |             <tr><th>Descripción</th><th>Unidad</th><th>Vence</th>
 377 |             <th class="td-right">Total</th><th class="td-right">Pagado</th>
 378 |             <th class="td-right">Saldo</th><th>Estado</th></tr>
 379 |           </thead>
 380 |           <tbody>
 381 |             ${charges.map(c => `
 382 |               <tr>
 383 |                 <td>${c.description}</td>
 384 |                 <td>Apt. ${c.unit_number}</td>
 385 |                 <td>${formatDate(c.due_date)}</td>
 386 |                 <td class="td-right">$${formatMoney(c.total)}</td>
 387 |                 <td class="td-right" style="color:var(--success);">$${formatMoney(c.paid)}</td>
 388 |                 <td class="td-right" style="color:${c.balance>0?'var(--danger)':'var(--success)'};font-weight:700;">$${formatMoney(c.balance)}</td>
 389 |                 <td><span class="badge badge-${c.status}">${c.status}</span></td>
 390 |               </tr>`).join('')}
 391 |           </tbody>
 392 |         </table>
 393 |       </div>
 394 |     </div>`;
 395 | }
 396 | 
 397 | // ── Reporte de proveedores ─────────────────────
 398 | async function loadReportProveedores() {
 399 |   const cat = document.getElementById('rep-cat').value;
 400 |   const suppliers = await apiRequest('/suppliers') || [];
 401 |   const filtered = cat ? suppliers.filter(s => s.category === cat) : suppliers;
 402 | 
 403 |   const totalPagado   = filtered.reduce((s,p) => s + p.total_paid, 0);
 404 |   const totalPendiente= filtered.reduce((s,p) => s + p.total_pending, 0);
 405 | 
 406 |   document.getElementById('prov-summary').innerHTML = `
 407 |     <div class="sum-card"><div class="sum-val">${filtered.length}</div><div class="sum-lbl">Proveedores</div></div>
 408 |     <div class="sum-card"><div class="sum-val" style="color:var(--success)">$${formatMoney(totalPagado)}</div><div class="sum-lbl">Total pagado</div></div>
 409 |     <div class="sum-card"><div class="sum-val" style="color:var(--danger)">$${formatMoney(totalPendiente)}</div><div class="sum-lbl">Pendiente</div></div>`;
 410 | 
 411 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('prov-tbody');
 412 |   if (!filtered.length) {
 413 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin proveedores</td></tr>`;
 414 |     return;
 415 |   }
 416 |   tbody.innerHTML = filtered.map(s => `
 417 |     <tr>
 418 |       <td><strong>${s.name}</strong></td>
 419 |       <td><span class="badge badge-primary">${s.category}</span></td>
 420 |       <td style="color:var(--text-muted);font-size:.8rem;">${s.ruc || '—'}</td>
 421 |       <td class="td-right" style="color:var(--success);font-weight:700;">$${formatMoney(s.total_paid)}</td>
 422 |       <td class="td-right" style="color:${s.total_pending>0?'var(--danger)':'var(--text-muted)'};font-weight:700;">$${formatMoney(s.total_pending)}</td>
 423 |       <td style="color:var(--text-muted);">—</td>
 424 |     </tr>`).join('');
 425 | }
 426 | 
 427 | init();
 428 | </script>
 429 | </body>
 430 | </html>

 305 |           <i class="fas fa-file-invoice"></i> Cotizaciones
 306 |         </button>
 307 |       </div>
 308 | 
 309 |       <!-- Panel pagos -->
 310 |       <div class="detail-panel active" id="dp-pagos">
 311 |         <div class="table-wrapper">
 312 |           <table>
 313 |             <thead><tr><th>Descripción</th><th>Fecha</th><th>Monto</th><th>Estado</th><th>Ref.</th></tr></thead>
 314 |             <tbody id="modal-pay-tbody"></tbody>
 315 |           </table>
 316 |         </div>
 317 |       </div>
 318 | 
 319 |       <!-- Panel cotizaciones -->
 320 |       <div class="detail-panel" id="dp-cotizaciones">
 321 |         <div class="table-wrapper">
 322 |           <table>
 323 |             <thead><tr><th>Descripción</th><th>Fecha</th><th>Monto</th><th>Válida hasta</th><th>Estado</th><th>PDF</th></tr></thead>
 324 |             <tbody id="modal-quote-tbody"></tbody>
 325 |           </table>
 326 |         </div>
 327 |         <!-- Input oculto para upload PDF -->
 328 |         <input type="file" id="pdf-upload-input" accept=".pdf" style="display:none"
 329 |           onchange="uploadPdf(this)">
 330 |       </div>
 331 |     </div>
 332 |   </div>
 333 | </div>
