 335 | <div id="notification"></div>
 336 | <script src="js/main.js"></script>
 337 | <script>
 338 | renderSidebar('suppliers');
 339 | 
 340 | let allSuppliers   = [];
 341 | let editingId      = null;
 342 | let currentSupId   = null;  // para modal
 343 | let pendingPdfQuoteId = null;
 344 | 
 345 | // ── Init ──────────────────────────────────────
 346 | async function init() {
 347 |   const cats = await apiRequest('/suppliers/categories') || [];
 348 |   const sel  = document.getElementById('sup-category');
 349 |   cats.forEach(c => sel.innerHTML += `<option value="${c}">${c}</option>`);
 350 | 
 351 |   document.getElementById('pay-date').value   = todayISO();
 352 |   document.getElementById('quote-date').value = todayISO();
 353 |   await loadSuppliers();
 354 | }
 355 | 
 356 | // ── Tabs ──────────────────────────────────────
 357 | function switchTab(tab) {
 358 |   document.querySelectorAll('.sup-tab').forEach((b,i) => {
 359 |     b.classList.toggle('active', ['lista','pagos','cotizaciones'][i] === tab);
 360 |   });
 361 |   document.querySelectorAll('.sup-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
 362 |   document.getElementById('panel-' + tab).classList.add('active');
 363 | }
 364 | 
 365 | // ── Proveedores ───────────────────────────────
 366 | async function loadSuppliers() {
 367 |   allSuppliers = await apiRequest('/suppliers') || [];
 368 |   renderSupplierList(allSuppliers);
 369 |   fillSupplierSelects();
 370 | }
 371 | 
 372 | function renderSupplierList(list) {
 373 |   document.getElementById('sup-count').textContent = list.length;
 374 |   const container = document.getElementById('sup-list');
 375 |   if (!list.length) {
 376 |     container.innerHTML = `<div style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">
 377 |       <i class="fas fa-truck" style="font-size:1.8rem;opacity:.3;display:block;margin-bottom:.5rem;"></i>
 378 |       Sin proveedores registrados</div>`;
 379 |     return;
 380 |   }
 381 |   container.innerHTML = list.map(s => `
 382 |     <div class="supplier-card" onclick="openDetail(${s.id})">
 383 |       <div class="sup-avatar">${s.name.charAt(0).toUpperCase()}</div>
 384 |       <div class="sup-info">
 385 |         <strong>${s.name}</strong>
 386 |         <span><span class="cat-badge">${s.category}</span>
 387 |           ${s.contact_name ? ` · ${s.contact_name}` : ''}
 388 |           ${s.phone ? ` · ${s.phone}` : ''}
 389 |         </span>
 390 |       </div>
 391 |       <div class="sup-totals">
 392 |         <div class="paid">$${formatMoney(s.total_paid)}</div>
 393 |         ${s.total_pending > 0 ? `<div class="pending">$${formatMoney(s.total_pending)} pendiente</div>` : ''}
 394 |       </div>
 395 |       <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="event.stopPropagation();editSupplier(${s.id})" title="Editar">
 396 |         <i class="fas fa-pencil-alt"></i>
 397 |       </button>
 398 |     </div>`).join('');
 399 | }
 400 | 
 401 | function filterSuppliers() {
 402 |   const q = document.getElementById('sup-search').value.toLowerCase();
 403 |   renderSupplierList(allSuppliers.filter(s =>
 404 |     s.name.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
 405 |     s.category.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
 406 |     (s.contact_name||'').toLowerCase().includes(q)
 407 |   ));
 408 | }
 409 | 
 410 | function fillSupplierSelects() {
 411 |   ['pay-supplier-select','quote-supplier-select'].forEach(id => {
 412 |     const sel = document.getElementById(id);
 413 |     const val = sel.value;
 414 |     sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Seleccione proveedor</option>';
 415 |     allSuppliers.forEach(s => sel.innerHTML += `<option value="${s.id}">${s.name}</option>`);
 416 |     sel.value = val;
 417 |   });
 418 | }
 419 | 
 420 | async function saveSupplier() {
 421 |   const name     = document.getElementById('sup-name').value.trim();
 422 |   const category = document.getElementById('sup-category').value;
 423 |   if (!name || !category) { showToast('Nombre y categoría son obligatorios', 'error'); return; }
 424 |   const data = {
 425 |     name, category,
 426 |     ruc:          document.getElementById('sup-ruc').value.trim()     || null,
 427 |     contact_name: document.getElementById('sup-contact').value.trim() || null,
 428 |     phone:        document.getElementById('sup-phone').value.trim()   || null,
 429 |     email:        document.getElementById('sup-email').value.trim()   || null,
 430 |     address:      document.getElementById('sup-address').value.trim() || null,
 431 |     notes:        document.getElementById('sup-notes').value.trim()   || null,
 432 |   };
 433 |   let r;
 434 |   if (editingId) {
 435 |     r = await apiRequest(`/suppliers/${editingId}`, 'PUT', data);
 436 |     if (r) showToast('Proveedor actualizado');
 437 |   } else {
 438 |     r = await apiRequest('/suppliers/', 'POST', data);
 439 |     if (r) showToast('Proveedor creado');
 440 |   }
 441 |   if (r) { cancelEdit(); loadSuppliers(); }
 442 | }
 443 | 
 444 | function editSupplier(id) {
 445 |   const s = allSuppliers.find(x => x.id === id);
 446 |   if (!s) return;
 447 |   editingId = id;
 448 |   document.getElementById('sup-id').value          = id;
 449 |   document.getElementById('sup-name').value         = s.name;
 450 |   document.getElementById('sup-category').value     = s.category;
 451 |   document.getElementById('sup-ruc').value          = s.ruc || '';
 452 |   document.getElementById('sup-contact').value      = s.contact_name || '';
 453 |   document.getElementById('sup-phone').value        = s.phone || '';
 454 |   document.getElementById('sup-email').value        = s.email || '';
 455 |   document.getElementById('sup-address').value      = s.address || '';
 456 |   document.getElementById('sup-notes').value        = s.notes || '';
 457 |   document.getElementById('form-title').textContent = 'Editar Proveedor';
 458 |   document.getElementById('btn-label').textContent  = 'Actualizar';
 459 |   document.getElementById('btn-cancel').style.display = '';
 460 |   switchTab('lista');
 461 |   window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
 462 | }
 463 | 
 464 | function cancelEdit() {
 465 |   editingId = null;
 466 |   ['sup-id','sup-name','sup-ruc','sup-contact','sup-phone','sup-email','sup-address','sup-notes']
 467 |     .forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value = '');
 468 |   document.getElementById('sup-category').value     = '';
 469 |   document.getElementById('form-title').textContent = 'Nuevo Proveedor';
 470 |   document.getElementById('btn-label').textContent  = 'Guardar Proveedor';
 471 |   document.getElementById('btn-cancel').style.display = 'none';
 472 | }
 473 | 
 474 | // ── Modal detalle ─────────────────────────────
 475 | async function openDetail(supplierId) {
 476 |   currentSupId = supplierId;
 477 |   const data = await apiRequest(`/suppliers/${supplierId}/detail`);
 478 |   if (!data) return;
 479 | 
 480 |   document.getElementById('modal-sup-name').textContent = data.name;
 481 | 
 482 |   // Info básica
 483 |   const fields = [
 484 |     ['Categoría', data.category],
 485 |     ['RUC',       data.ruc || '—'],
 486 |     ['Contacto',  data.contact_name || '—'],
 487 |     ['Teléfono',  data.phone || '—'],
 488 |     ['Email',     data.email || '—'],
 489 |     ['Dirección', data.address || '—'],
 490 |   ];
 491 |   document.getElementById('modal-detail-grid').innerHTML = fields.map(([l,v]) => `
 492 |     <div class="detail-item">
 493 |       <div class="dl">${l}</div>
 494 |       <div class="dv">${v}</div>
 495 |     </div>`).join('');
 496 | 
 497 |   // Resumen financiero
 498 |   document.getElementById('modal-sum-row').innerHTML = `
 499 |     <div class="sum-chip paid">
 500 |       Total pagado<span class="sc-val">$${formatMoney(data.total_paid)}</span>
 501 |     </div>
 502 |     <div class="sum-chip pending">
 503 |       Pendiente<span class="sc-val">$${formatMoney(data.total_pending)}</span>
 504 |     </div>
 505 |     <div class="sum-chip neutral">
 506 |       Pagos<span class="sc-val">${data.payments.length}</span>
 507 |     </div>
 508 |     <div class="sum-chip neutral">
 509 |       Cotizaciones<span class="sc-val">${data.quotes.length}</span>
 510 |     </div>`;
 511 | 
 512 |   // Tabla pagos
 513 |   const payTbody = document.getElementById('modal-pay-tbody');
 514 |   if (!data.payments.length) {
 515 |     payTbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="5" style="text-align:center;padding:1.5rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin pagos registrados</td></tr>`;
 516 |   } else {
 517 |     payTbody.innerHTML = data.payments.map(p => `
 518 |       <tr>
 519 |         <td>${p.description}</td>
 520 |         <td>${formatDate(p.payment_date)}</td>
 521 |         <td><strong>$${formatMoney(p.amount)}</strong></td>
 522 |         <td><span class="status-badge status-${p.status}">${p.status}</span></td>
 523 |         <td style="color:var(--text-muted);font-size:.8rem;">${p.reference || '—'}</td>
 524 |       </tr>`).join('');
 525 |   }
 526 | 
 527 |   // Tabla cotizaciones
 528 |   const quoteTbody = document.getElementById('modal-quote-tbody');
 529 |   if (!data.quotes.length) {
 530 |     quoteTbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:1.5rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin cotizaciones registradas</td></tr>`;
 531 |   } else {
 532 |     quoteTbody.innerHTML = data.quotes.map(q => `
 533 |       <tr>
 534 |         <td>${q.description}</td>
 535 |         <td>${formatDate(q.quote_date)}</td>
 536 |         <td><strong>$${formatMoney(q.amount)}</strong></td>
 537 |         <td style="color:var(--text-muted);font-size:.8rem;">${q.valid_until ? formatDate(q.valid_until) : '—'}</td>
 538 |         <td><span class="status-badge status-${q.status}">${q.status}</span></td>
 539 |         <td>
 540 |           ${q.pdf_path
 541 |             ? `<a href="/api/suppliers/quotes/${q.id}/pdf" target="_blank" class="pdf-badge has-pdf">
 542 |                 <i class="fas fa-file-pdf"></i> Ver PDF
 543 |                </a>`
 544 |             : `<button class="pdf-badge" onclick="triggerPdfUpload(${q.id})" title="Subir PDF">
 545 |                 <i class="fas fa-upload"></i> Subir PDF
 546 |                </button>`}
 547 |         </td>
 548 |       </tr>`).join('');
 549 |   }
 550 | 
 551 |   // Resetear tabs internos
 552 |   switchDetailTab('pagos', document.querySelector('.detail-tab'));
 553 | 
 554 |   document.getElementById('detail-modal').classList.add('open');
 555 | }
 556 | 
 557 | function closeDetail() {
 558 |   document.getElementById('detail-modal').classList.remove('open');
 559 |   currentSupId = null;
 560 | }
 561 | 
 562 | function switchDetailTab(tab, el) {
 563 |   document.querySelectorAll('.detail-tab').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
 564 |   document.querySelectorAll('.detail-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
 565 |   if (el) el.classList.add('active');
 566 |   document.getElementById('dp-' + tab).classList.add('active');
 567 | }
 568 | 
 569 | // Cerrar modal al hacer clic fuera
 570 | document.getElementById('detail-modal').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
 571 |   if (e.target === this) closeDetail();
 572 | });
 573 | 
 574 | // ── Upload PDF ────────────────────────────────
 575 | function triggerPdfUpload(quoteId) {
 576 |   pendingPdfQuoteId = quoteId;
 577 |   document.getElementById('pdf-upload-input').click();
 578 | }
 579 | 
 580 | async function uploadPdf(input) {
 581 |   if (!input.files[0] || !pendingPdfQuoteId) return;
 582 |   const file     = input.files[0];
 583 |   const formData = new FormData();
 584 |   formData.append('file', file);
 585 | 
 586 |   try {
 587 |     const token    = Auth.token();
 588 |     const headers  = token ? { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } : {};
 589 |     const response = await fetch(`/api/suppliers/quotes/${pendingPdfQuoteId}/upload-pdf`, {
 590 |       method: 'POST', headers, body: formData
 591 |     });
 592 |     if (!response.ok) {
 593 |       const err = await response.json();
 594 |       showToast(err.detail || 'Error al subir el PDF', 'error');
 595 |     } else {
 596 |       showToast('PDF adjuntado correctamente', 'success');
 597 |       // Reabrir modal con datos actualizados
 598 |       await openDetail(currentSupId);
 599 |     }
 600 |   } catch(e) {
 601 |     showToast('Error al subir el PDF', 'error');
 602 |   }
 603 |   input.value = '';
 604 |   pendingPdfQuoteId = null;
 605 | }
 606 | 
 607 | // ── Pagos tab ─────────────────────────────────
 608 | async function loadSupplierPayments() {
 609 |   const id = document.getElementById('pay-supplier-select').value;
 610 |   if (!id) return;
 611 |   const payments = await apiRequest(`/suppliers/${id}/payments`) || [];
 612 |   document.getElementById('pay-count').textContent = payments.length;
 613 |   const sup   = allSuppliers.find(s => s.id === parseInt(id));
 614 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('pay-table');
 615 |   if (!payments.length) {
 616 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;padding:1.5rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin pagos</td></tr>`;
 617 |     return;
 618 |   }
 619 |   tbody.innerHTML = payments.map(p => `
 620 |     <tr>
 621 |       <td><strong>${sup?.name || '—'}</strong></td>
 622 |       <td>${p.description}</td>
 623 |       <td>${formatDate(p.payment_date)}</td>
 624 |       <td><strong>$${formatMoney(p.amount)}</strong></td>
 625 |       <td><span class="status-badge status-${p.status}">${p.status}</span></td>
 626 |       <td>
 627 |         <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="deletePayment(${p.id})" title="Eliminar">
 628 |           <i class="fas fa-trash" style="color:var(--danger);"></i>
 629 |         </button>
 630 |       </td>
 631 |     </tr>`).join('');
 632 | }
 633 | 
 634 | async function savePayment() {
 635 |   const supId = document.getElementById('pay-supplier-select').value;
 636 |   const desc  = document.getElementById('pay-desc').value.trim();
 637 |   const amt   = parseFloat(document.getElementById('pay-amount').value);
 638 |   const dt    = document.getElementById('pay-date').value;
 639 |   if (!supId || !desc || !amt || !dt) { showToast('Completa todos los campos', 'error'); return; }
 640 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/suppliers/${supId}/payments`, 'POST', {
 641 |     description: desc, amount: amt, payment_date: dt,
 642 |     status: document.getElementById('pay-status').value,
 643 |     reference: document.getElementById('pay-ref').value.trim() || null,
 644 |   });
 645 |   if (r) {
 646 |     showToast('Pago registrado');
 647 |     ['pay-desc','pay-amount','pay-ref'].forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value = '');
 648 |     document.getElementById('pay-date').value = todayISO();
 649 |     loadSupplierPayments(); loadSuppliers();
 650 |   }
 651 | }
 652 | 
 653 | async function deletePayment(id) {
 654 |   if (!confirm('¿Eliminar este pago?')) return;
 655 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/suppliers/payments/${id}`, 'DELETE');
 656 |   if (r) { showToast('Pago eliminado'); loadSupplierPayments(); loadSuppliers(); }
 657 | }
 658 | 
 659 | // ── Cotizaciones tab ──────────────────────────
 660 | async function loadSupplierQuotes() {
 661 |   const id = document.getElementById('quote-supplier-select').value;
 662 |   if (!id) return;
 663 |   const quotes = await apiRequest(`/suppliers/${id}/quotes`) || [];
 664 |   document.getElementById('quote-count').textContent = quotes.length;
 665 |   const sup   = allSuppliers.find(s => s.id === parseInt(id));
 666 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('quote-table');
 667 |   if (!quotes.length) {
 668 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="7" style="text-align:center;padding:1.5rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin cotizaciones</td></tr>`;
 669 |     return;
 670 |   }
 671 |   tbody.innerHTML = quotes.map(q => `
 672 |     <tr>
 673 |       <td><strong>${sup?.name || '—'}</strong></td>
 674 |       <td>${q.description}</td>
 675 |       <td>${formatDate(q.quote_date)}</td>
 676 |       <td><strong>$${formatMoney(q.amount)}</strong></td>
 677 |       <td>
 678 |         <select class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm"
 679 |           style="border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:6px;padding:3px 8px;font-size:.78rem;"
 680 |           onchange="updateQuoteStatus(${q.id}, this.value, ${id})">
 681 |           <option value="PENDIENTE"  ${q.status==='PENDIENTE' ?'selected':''}>Pendiente</option>
 682 |           <option value="APROBADA"   ${q.status==='APROBADA'  ?'selected':''}>Aprobada</option>
 683 |           <option value="RECHAZADA"  ${q.status==='RECHAZADA' ?'selected':''}>Rechazada</option>
 684 |         </select>
 685 |       </td>
 686 |       <td>
 687 |         ${q.pdf_path
 688 |           ? `<a href="/api/suppliers/quotes/${q.id}/pdf" target="_blank" class="pdf-badge has-pdf">
 689 |               <i class="fas fa-file-pdf"></i> Ver</a>`
 690 |           : `<label class="pdf-badge" style="cursor:pointer;">
 691 |               <i class="fas fa-upload"></i> Subir
 692 |               <input type="file" accept=".pdf" style="display:none"
 693 |                 onchange="uploadPdfInline(this, ${q.id}, ${id})">
 694 |             </label>`}
 695 |       </td>
 696 |       <td>
 697 |         <button class="btn btn-ghost btn-sm" onclick="deleteQuote(${q.id}, ${id})" title="Eliminar">
 698 |           <i class="fas fa-trash" style="color:var(--danger);"></i>
 699 |         </button>
 700 |       </td>
 701 |     </tr>`).join('');
 702 | }
 703 | 
 704 | async function saveQuote() {
 705 |   const supId = document.getElementById('quote-supplier-select').value;
 706 |   const desc  = document.getElementById('quote-desc').value.trim();
 707 |   const amt   = parseFloat(document.getElementById('quote-amount').value);
 708 |   const dt    = document.getElementById('quote-date').value;
 709 |   if (!supId || !desc || !amt || !dt) { showToast('Completa todos los campos', 'error'); return; }
 710 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/suppliers/${supId}/quotes`, 'POST', {
 711 |     description: desc, amount: amt, quote_date: dt,
 712 |     valid_until: document.getElementById('quote-valid').value  || null,
 713 |     status:      document.getElementById('quote-status').value,
 714 |     notes:       document.getElementById('quote-notes').value.trim() || null,
 715 |   });
 716 |   if (r) {
 717 |     showToast('Cotización guardada');
 718 |     ['quote-desc','quote-amount','quote-valid','quote-notes'].forEach(id => document.getElementById(id).value='');
 719 |     document.getElementById('quote-date').value   = todayISO();
 720 |     document.getElementById('quote-status').value = 'PENDIENTE';
 721 |     loadSupplierQuotes();
 722 |   }
 723 | }
 724 | 
 725 | async function updateQuoteStatus(id, status, supId) {
 726 |   const quotes = await apiRequest(`/suppliers/${supId}/quotes`) || [];
 727 |   const q = quotes.find(x => x.id === id);
 728 |   if (!q) return;
 729 |   await apiRequest(`/suppliers/quotes/${id}`, 'PUT', {
 730 |     description: q.description, amount: q.amount,
 731 |     quote_date: q.quote_date, status,
 732 |     valid_until: q.valid_until || null, notes: q.notes || null,
 733 |   });
 734 |   showToast('Estado actualizado');
 735 | }
 736 | 
 737 | async function deleteQuote(id, supId) {
 738 |   if (!confirm('¿Eliminar esta cotización?')) return;
 739 |   const r = await apiRequest(`/suppliers/quotes/${id}`, 'DELETE');
 740 |   if (r) { showToast('Cotización eliminada'); loadSupplierQuotes(); }
 741 | }
 742 | 
 743 | // Upload PDF inline (desde tab cotizaciones)
 744 | async function uploadPdfInline(input, quoteId, supId) {
 745 |   if (!input.files[0]) return;
 746 |   const formData = new FormData();
 747 |   formData.append('file', input.files[0]);
 748 |   const token    = Auth.token();
 749 |   const headers  = token ? { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` } : {};
 750 |   const response = await fetch(`/api/suppliers/quotes/${quoteId}/upload-pdf`, {
 751 |     method: 'POST', headers, body: formData
 752 |   });
 753 |   if (!response.ok) {
 754 |     showToast('Error al subir el PDF', 'error');
 755 |   } else {
 756 |     showToast('PDF adjuntado', 'success');
 757 |     loadSupplierQuotes();
 758 |   }
 759 |   input.value = '';
 760 | }
 761 | 
 762 | init();
 763 | </script>
 764 | </body>
 765 | </html>
 766 |

 101 | <script>
 102 | renderHeader('units');
 103 | 
 104 | let allUnits = [];
 105 | let allProps = [];
 106 | let allOwners = [];
 107 | 
 108 | async function loadAll() {
 109 |   const [units, props, owners] = await Promise.all([
 110 |     apiRequest('/units'),
 111 |     apiRequest('/properties'),
 112 |     apiRequest('/owners'),
 113 |   ]);
 114 | 
 115 |   allUnits  = units  || [];
 116 |   allProps  = props  || [];
 117 |   allOwners = owners || [];
 118 | 
 119 |   // Fill property select (form + filter)
 120 |   const sel = document.getElementById('property-select');
 121 |   sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Todas las propiedades</option>';
 122 |   allProps.forEach(p => sel.innerHTML += `<option value="${p.id}">${p.name}</option>`);
 123 | 
 124 |   // Fill assign selects
 125 |   const selU = document.getElementById('assign-unit-select');
 126 |   selU.innerHTML = '<option value="">Seleccione unidad</option>';
 127 |   allUnits.forEach(u => {
 128 |     const p = allProps.find(x => x.id === u.property_id);
 129 |     selU.innerHTML += `<option value="${u.id}">Apt. ${u.unit_number}${p ? ` — ${p.name}` : ''}</option>`;
 130 |   });
 131 | 
 132 |   const selO = document.getElementById('assign-owner-select');
 133 |   selO.innerHTML = '<option value="">Seleccione propietario</option>';
 134 |   allOwners.forEach(o => selO.innerHTML += `<option value="${o.id}">${o.full_name}</option>`);
 135 | 
 136 |   // Default start date
 137 |   document.getElementById('start_date').value = todayISO();
 138 | 
 139 |   await renderTable(allUnits);
 140 | }
 141 | 
 142 | async function renderTable(units) {
 143 |   document.getElementById('unit-count').textContent = units.length;
 144 |   const tbody = document.getElementById('units-table');
 145 | 
 146 |   if (!units.length) {
 147 |     tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="5" style="text-align:center;padding:2rem;color:var(--text-muted);">Sin unidades registradas</td></tr>`;
 148 |     return;
 149 |   }
 150 | 
 151 |   // Load ownerships in parallel
 152 |   const ownerships = await Promise.all(
 153 |     units.map(u => apiRequest(`/unit-owners/by-unit/${u.id}`).then(r => ({ uid: u.id, data: r || [] })))
 154 |   );
 155 |   const ownerMap = {};
 156 |   ownerships.forEach(o => ownerMap[o.uid] = o.data);
 157 | 
 158 |   tbody.innerHTML = units.map(u => {
 159 |     const prop    = allProps.find(p => p.id === u.property_id);
 160 |     const active  = (ownerMap[u.id] || []).find(o => o.role === 'Propietario Actual');
 161 |     return `<tr>
 162 |       <td><strong>Apt. ${u.unit_number}</strong></td>
 163 |       <td>${u.floor || '—'}</td>
 164 |       <td style="color:var(--text-secondary);font-size:.83rem;">${prop?.name || '—'}</td>
 165 |       <td>${active
 166 |         ? `<span style="font-weight:600;">${active.owner_name}</span>`
 167 |         : `<em style="color:var(--text-muted);">Sin asignar</em>`}</td>
 168 |       <td style="font-size:.82rem;color:var(--text-secondary);">${active ? formatDate(active.start_date) : '—'}</td>
 169 |     </tr>`;
 170 |   }).join('');
 171 | }
 172 | 
 173 | function filterUnits() {
 174 |   const propId = parseInt(document.getElementById('property-select').value) || null;
 175 |   const filtered = propId ? allUnits.filter(u => u.property_id === propId) : allUnits;
 176 |   renderTable(filtered);
 177 | }
 178 | 
 179 | async function createUnit() {
 180 |   const propId = parseInt(document.getElementById('property-select').value);
 181 |   const number = document.getElementById('unit_number').value.trim();
 182 |   const floor  = document.getElementById('floor').value.trim();
 183 | 
 184 |   if (!propId) { showToast('Selecciona una propiedad', 'error'); return; }
 185 |   if (!number) { showToast('Ingresa el número de unidad', 'error'); return; }
 186 | 
 187 |   const result = await apiRequest('/units/', 'POST', {
 188 |     property_id: propId,
 189 |     unit_number: number,
 190 |     floor: floor || null,
 191 |   });
 192 | 
 193 |   if (result) {
 194 |     showToast('Unidad creada correctamente');
 195 |     document.getElementById('unit_number').value = '';
 196 |     document.getElementById('floor').value = '';
 197 |     await loadAll();
 198 |   }
 199 | }
 200 | 
 201 | async function assignOwner() {
 202 |   const unitId  = parseInt(document.getElementById('assign-unit-select').value);
 203 |   const ownerId = parseInt(document.getElementById('assign-owner-select').value);
 204 |   const date    = document.getElementById('start_date').value;
 205 | 
 206 |   if (!unitId || !ownerId || !date) {
 207 |     showToast('Completa todos los campos', 'error'); return;
 208 |   }
 209 | 
 210 |   const result = await apiRequest('/unit-owners/', 'POST', {
 211 |     unit_id: unitId, owner_id: ownerId, start_date: date,
 212 |   });
 213 | 
 214 |   if (result) {
 215 |     showToast('Propietario asignado correctamente');
 216 |     await loadAll();
 217 |   }
 218 | }
 219 | 
 220 | loadAll();
 221 | </script>
 222 | </body>
 223 | </html>
 224 |

TIPO: JS
RUTA COMPLETA: C:\alianza_backend\app\static\js\main.js
================================================================================

   1 | /* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   2 |    main.js  — Alianza Residencial
   3 |    CAMBIOS:
   4 |    · Auth.role() ahora expone el rol del token JWT
   5 |    · Auth.isGarita() para detectar rol GARITA
   6 |    · renderSidebar() filtra menú según rol:
   7 |        ADMIN  → todo el menú
   8 |        USER   → todo excepto Administración
   9 |        GARITA → solo Garita (sin acceso a nada más)
  10 |    · Protección de páginas: si el rol no tiene acceso, redirige a garita.html
  11 |    · rolLabel muestra "Seguridad Garita" para el rol GARITA
  12 |    · Protección de rutas en cada página sensible
  13 |    · FIX: conflicto de git resuelto en NAV_PAGES (Agenda)
  14 |    · FIX: GARITA ahora solo ve el ítem "Garita / Visitas" en el sidebar
  15 | ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
  16 | 
  17 | /* ─── Auth ────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
  18 | const Auth = {
  19 |   _key: 'alianza_token',
  20 |   _user: 'alianza_user',
  21 |   _role: 'alianza_role',
  22 | 
  23 |   save(token, username, role) {
  24 |     localStorage.setItem(this._key,  token);
  25 |     localStorage.setItem(this._user, username);
  26 |     localStorage.setItem(this._role, role || 'USER');
  27 |   },
  28 | 
  29 |   token()   { return localStorage.getItem(this._key);  },
  30 |   user()    { return localStorage.getItem(this._user) || ''; },
  31 |   role()    { return localStorage.getItem(this._role) || 'USER'; },
  32 | 
  33 |   isAdmin()  { return this.role() === 'ADMIN';  },
  34 |   isGarita() { return this.role() === 'GARITA'; },
  35 | 
  36 |   clear() {
  37 |     localStorage.removeItem(this._key);
  38 |     localStorage.removeItem(this._user);
  39 |     localStorage.removeItem(this._role);
  40 |   },
  41 | 
  42 |   // Requiere sesión activa — redirige a login si no hay token
  43 |   require() {
  44 |     if (!this.token()) {
  45 |       window.location.href = '/login';
  46 |       return false;
  47 |     }
  48 |     return true;
  49 |   },
  50 | 
  51 |   // Requiere que el rol tenga acceso a esta área
  52 |   // Si es GARITA y está en una página que no es garita.html → redirige
  53 |   requireNotGarita() {
  54 |     if (this.isGarita()) {
  55 |       window.location.href = '/static/garita.html';
  56 |       return false;
  57 |     }
  58 |     return true;
  59 |   },
  60 | };
  61 | 
  62 | /* ─── API ─────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
  63 | async function apiRequest(endpoint, method = 'GET', body = null) {
  64 |   const token = Auth.token();
  65 |   const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
  66 |   if (token) headers['Authorization'] = `Bearer ${token}`;
  67 | 
  68 |   const opts = { method, headers };
  69 |   if (body) opts.body = JSON.stringify(body);
  70 | 
  71 |   try {
  72 |     const res = await fetch(`/api${endpoint}`, opts);
  73 | 
  74 |     if (res.status === 401) {
  75 |       Auth.clear();
  76 |       window.location.href = '/login';
  77 |       return null;
  78 |     }
  79 | 
  80 |     if (res.status === 403) {
  81 |       showToast('No tienes permiso para realizar esta acción', 'error');
  82 |       return null;
  83 |     }
  84 | 
  85 |     if (!res.ok) {
  86 |       let detail = `Error ${res.status}`;
  87 |       try { detail = (await res.json()).detail || detail; } catch (_) {}
  88 |       showToast(detail, 'error');
  89 |       return null;
  90 |     }
  91 | 
  92 |     if (res.status === 204) return {};
  93 |     return await res.json();
  94 |   } catch (e) {
  95 |     showToast('Error de conexión con el servidor', 'error');
  96 |     return null;
  97 |   }
  98 | }
  99 | 
 100 | /* ─── Toasts ─────────────────────────────────────────────── */
 101 | function showToast(msg, type = 'success') {
 102 |   const icons = { success: '✓', error: '✕', warning: '⚠' };
 103 |   const el = document.createElement('div');
 104 |   el.className = `toast toast-${type}`;
 105 |   el.innerHTML = `<span>${icons[type] || '·'}</span> ${msg}`;
 106 |   let box = document.getElementById('notification');
 107 |   if (!box) { box = document.createElement('div'); box.id = 'notification'; document.body.appendChild(box); }
 108 |   box.appendChild(el);
 109 |   setTimeout(() => { el.style.opacity = '0'; el.style.transition = 'opacity .4s'; setTimeout(() => el.remove(), 400); }, 3500);
 110 | }
 111 | 
 112 | /* ─── Formato ────────────────────────────────────────────── */
 113 | function formatMoney(v) {
 114 |   return parseFloat(v || 0).toLocaleString('es-PA', { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
 115 | }
 116 | function formatDate(str) {
 117 |   if (!str) return '—';
 118 |   try { const [y, m, d] = str.split('T')[0].split('-'); return `${d}/${m}/${y}`; }
 119 |   catch (_) { return str; }
 120 | }
 121 | function todayISO() { return new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]; }
 122 | function todayLong() {
 123 |   return new Date().toLocaleDateString('es-PA', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
 124 | }

 144 |   { href: '/static/reports.html',    label: 'Reportes',         icon: 'fa-chart-bar',    id: 'reports',    roles: ['ADMIN', 'USER'] },
 145 |   { href: '/static/imports.html',    label: 'Importar/Exp.',    icon: 'fa-file-import',  id: 'imports',    roles: ['ADMIN', 'USER'] },
 146 |   { href: '/static/historial.html',  label: 'Historial',        icon: 'fa-history',      id: 'historial',  roles: ['ADMIN', 'USER'] },
 147 |   // Administración: solo ADMIN
 148 |   { href: '/static/admin.html',      label: 'Administración',   icon: 'fa-shield-alt',   id: 'admin',      roles: ['ADMIN'] },
 149 |   // Garita: visible para ADMIN, USER y GARITA
 150 |   // GARITA solo verá este ítem en su menú
 151 |   { href: '/static/garita.html',     label: 'Garita / Visitas', icon: 'fa-car',          id: 'garita',     roles: ['ADMIN', 'USER', 'GARITA'] },
 152 | ];
 153 | 
 154 | // Etiquetas de rol para mostrar al usuario
 155 | const ROLE_LABELS = {
 156 |   'ADMIN':  'Administrador',
 157 |   'USER':   'Usuario',
 158 |   'GARITA': 'Seguridad Garita',
 159 | };
 160 | 
 161 | function renderSidebar(activePage) {
 162 |   if (!Auth.require()) return;
 163 | 
 164 |   const role    = Auth.role();
 165 |   const isAdmin = Auth.isAdmin();
 166 | 
 167 |   // ── Protección de ruta ────────────────────────────────────────
 168 |   // Si la página actual no está permitida para este rol → redirigir
 169 |   const currentPage = NAV_PAGES.find(p => p.id === activePage);
 170 |   if (currentPage && !currentPage.roles.includes(role)) {
 171 |     // GARITA intentando acceder a cualquier página que no sea garita → redirigir
 172 |     if (Auth.isGarita()) {
 173 |       window.location.href = '/static/garita.html';
 174 |       return;
 175 |     }
 176 |     // USER intentando llegar a página de admin → redirigir a inicio
 177 |     window.location.href = '/static/index.html';
 178 |     return;
 179 |   }
 180 | 
 181 |   // Si no hay página definida en NAV_PAGES y es GARITA → redirigir
 182 |   // (protege rutas no listadas, ej: index.html no está en roles de GARITA)
 183 |   if (!currentPage && Auth.isGarita()) {
 184 |     window.location.href = '/static/garita.html';
 185 |     return;
 186 |   }
 187 | 
 188 |   if (!document.getElementById('_sidebar')) {
 189 |     const oldHeader = document.querySelector('header.main-header');
 190 |     if (oldHeader) oldHeader.remove();
 191 | 
 192 |     const existingContent = document.body.innerHTML;
 193 | 
 194 |     document.body.innerHTML = `
 195 |       <aside class="sidebar" id="_sidebar">
 196 |         <div class="sidebar-brand">
 197 |           <div class="sidebar-logo" id="_sidebar_logo">AR</div>
 198 |           <div class="sidebar-brand-text">
 199 |             <h1>ALIANZA RESIDENCIAL</h1>
 200 |             <p>Administración de Propiedades</p>
 201 |           </div>
 202 |         </div>
 203 |         <nav class="sidebar-nav" id="_sidebar_nav"></nav>
 204 |         <div class="sidebar-footer">
 205 |           <div class="sidebar-user">
 206 |             <div class="sidebar-user-avatar" id="_sb_avatar">A</div>
 207 |             <div class="sidebar-user-info">
 208 |               <strong id="_sb_username"></strong>
 209 |               <span id="_sb_role_label">Usuario</span>
 210 |             </div>
 211 |             <div class="sidebar-user-actions">
 212 |               <button class="sidebar-icon-btn" onclick="logout()" title="Cerrar sesión">
 213 |                 <i class="fas fa-sign-out-alt"></i>
 214 |               </button>
 215 |             </div>
 216 |           </div>
 217 |         </div>
 218 |       </aside>
 219 |       <button class="sidebar-toggle" id="_sb_toggle" onclick="toggleSidebar()" title="Colapsar menú">
 220 |         <i class="fas fa-chevron-left" id="_sb_toggle_icon"></i>
 221 |       </button>
 222 |       <div class="main-wrapper">
 223 |         <div class="topbar">
 224 |           <div class="topbar-left">
 225 |             <span class="topbar-title" id="_topbar_title"></span>
 226 |           </div>
 227 |           <div class="topbar-right">
 228 |             <span class="topbar-date" id="_topbar_date"></span>
 229 |           </div>
 230 |         </div>
 231 |         ${existingContent}
 232 |       </div>
 233 |       <div id="notification"></div>`;
 234 |   }
 235 | 
 236 |   // Llenar nav — filtrar según el rol del usuario
 237 |   // GARITA solo verá los ítems donde su rol está incluido → únicamente "Garita / Visitas"
 238 |   const nav = document.getElementById('_sidebar_nav');
 239 |   nav.innerHTML = NAV_PAGES
 240 |     .filter(p => p.roles.includes(role))
 241 |     .map(p => `
 242 |       <a href="${p.href}" class="${activePage === p.id ? 'active' : ''}">
 243 |         <i class="fas ${p.icon}"></i>
 244 |         <span>${p.label}</span>
 245 |       </a>`).join('');
 246 | 
 247 |   // Usuario, rol y avatar
 248 |   const u        = Auth.user();
 249 |   const rolLabel = ROLE_LABELS[role] || role;
 250 |   const elU = document.getElementById('_sb_username');
 251 |   const elR = document.getElementById('_sb_role_label');
 252 |   const av  = document.getElementById('_sb_avatar');
 253 |   if (elU) elU.textContent = u;
 254 |   if (elR) elR.textContent = rolLabel;
 255 |   if (av)  av.textContent  = u.charAt(0).toUpperCase();
 256 | 
 257 |   // Color del avatar según rol
 258 |   if (av) {
 259 |     if (role === 'ADMIN')  av.style.background = '#fbbf24'; // amarillo admin
 260 |     if (role === 'GARITA') av.style.background = '#34d399'; // verde garita
 261 |   }
 262 | 
 263 |   // Título y fecha en topbar
 264 |   const page = NAV_PAGES.find(p => p.id === activePage);
 265 |   const tt   = document.getElementById('_topbar_title');
 266 |   const td   = document.getElementById('_topbar_date');
 267 |   if (tt && page) tt.textContent = page.label;
 268 |   if (td) td.textContent = todayLong();
 269 | 
 270 |   // Logo
 271 |   const logo = document.getElementById('_sidebar_logo');
 272 |   if (logo) {
 273 |     const img = new Image();
 274 |     img.onload  = () => { logo.innerHTML = `<img src="/static/logo.png" alt="Logo">`; };
 275 |     img.onerror = () => {};
 276 |     img.src = '/static/logo.png';
 277 |   }
 278 | 
 279 |   const collapsed = localStorage.getItem('sidebar_collapsed') === '1';
 280 |   if (collapsed) _applySidebarCollapse(true, false);
 281 | }
 282 | 
 283 | /* Alias para páginas que usan renderHeader */
 284 | function renderHeader(activePage) { renderSidebar(activePage); }
 285 | 
 286 | function toggleSidebar() {
 287 |   const collapsed = document.getElementById('_sidebar').classList.contains('collapsed');
 288 |   _applySidebarCollapse(!collapsed, true);
 289 | }
 290 | 
 291 | function _applySidebarCollapse(collapse, save) {
 292 |   const sb   = document.getElementById('_sidebar');
 293 |   const icon = document.getElementById('_sb_toggle_icon');
 294 |   if (!sb) return;
 295 |   if (collapse) {
 296 |     sb.classList.add('collapsed');
 297 |     document.body.classList.add('sidebar-collapsed');
 298 |     if (icon) { icon.classList.remove('fa-chevron-left'); icon.classList.add('fa-chevron-right'); }
 299 |   } else {
 300 |     sb.classList.remove('collapsed');
 301 |     document.body.classList.remove('sidebar-collapsed');
 302 |     if (icon) { icon.classList.remove('fa-chevron-right'); icon.classList.add('fa-chevron-left'); }
 303 |   }
 304 |   if (save) localStorage.setItem('sidebar_collapsed', collapse ? '1' : '0');
 305 | }
 306 | 
 307 | function logout() { Auth.clear(); window.location.href = '/login'; }
 308 | 
 309 | /* ─── Loaders de selects ─────────────────────────────────── */
 310 | async function loadSelectOptions(selectId, endpoint, valFn, labelFn, ph = 'Seleccione...') {
 311 |   const sel = document.getElementById(selectId);
 312 |   if (!sel) return [];
 313 |   const items = await apiRequest(endpoint) || [];
 314 |   sel.innerHTML = `<option value="">${ph}</option>`;
 315 |   items.forEach(i => sel.innerHTML += `<option value="${valFn(i)}">${labelFn(i)}</option>`);
 316 |   return items;
 317 | }
 318 | async function loadPropertiesSelect(id = 'property-select') {
 319 |   return loadSelectOptions(id, '/properties', p => p.id, p => p.name, 'Seleccione propiedad');
 320 | }
 321 | async function loadOwnersSelect(id = 'owner-select') {
 322 |   return loadSelectOptions(id, '/owners', o => o.id, o => o.full_name, 'Seleccione propietario');
 323 | }
 324 | async function loadUnitsSelect(id = 'unit-select', propId = null) {
 325 |   const all = await apiRequest('/units') || [];
 326 |   const filtered = propId ? all.filter(u => u.property_id === parseInt(propId)) : all;
 327 |   const sel = document.getElementById(id);
 328 |   if (!sel) return filtered;
 329 |   sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Seleccione unidad</option>';
 330 |   filtered.forEach(u => sel.innerHTML += `<option value="${u.id}">Apt. ${u.unit_number}</option>`);
 331 |   return filtered;
 332 | }
 333 |

   1 | ﻿import os
   2 | from datetime import datetime
   3 | 
   4 | 
   5 | def extraer_py_html_a_txt(ruta_principal, nombre_txt=None):
   6 |     """
   7 |     Extrae todos los archivos .py, .html, .css y .js y los consolida en un solo TXT.
   8 | 
   9 |     Args:
  10 |         ruta_principal (str): Ruta de la carpeta principal a escanear.
  11 |         nombre_txt (str): Nombre del archivo TXT de salida (opcional).
  12 |     """
  13 | 
  14 |     if not os.path.exists(ruta_principal):
  15 |         print(f"Error: La ruta {ruta_principal} no existe")
  16 |         return False
  17 | 
  18 |     # Si no se proporciona nombre, se genera con fecha y hora.
  19 |     if nombre_txt is None:
  20 |         fecha_actual = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
  21 |         nombre_txt = f"analisis_codigo_{fecha_actual}.txt"
  22 | 
  23 |     carpetas_excluidas = {"venv", "__pycache__", ".git", ".idea", "env"}
  24 | 
  25 |     archivos_procesados = 0
  26 |     lineas_totales = 0
  27 | 
  28 |     try:
  29 |         with open(nombre_txt, "w", encoding="utf-8") as txt_file:
  30 |             txt_file.write("=" * 80 + "\n")
  31 |             txt_file.write("ANALISIS DE CODIGO - PROYECTO ALIANZA BACKEND\n")
  32 |             txt_file.write(f"Fecha de generacion: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\n")
  33 |             txt_file.write(f"Ruta principal: {ruta_principal}\n")
  34 |             txt_file.write("=" * 80 + "\n\n")
  35 | 
  36 |             for root, dirs, files in os.walk(ruta_principal):
  37 |                 dirs[:] = [d for d in dirs if d not in carpetas_excluidas]
  38 | 
  39 |                 for file in sorted(files):
  40 |                     if file.endswith((".py", ".html", ".css", ".js", ".env", ".unit", ".md", ".bat")):
  41 |                         ruta_completa = os.path.join(root, file)
  42 | 
  43 |                         if "venv" in root.split(os.sep):
  44 |                             continue
  45 | 
  46 |                         ruta_relativa = os.path.relpath(ruta_completa, ruta_principal)
  47 | 
  48 |                         txt_file.write("\n" + "=" * 80 + "\n")
  49 |                         txt_file.write(f"ARCHIVO: {ruta_relativa}\n")
  50 |                         txt_file.write(f"TIPO: {file.split('.')[-1].upper()}\n")
  51 |                         txt_file.write(f"RUTA COMPLETA: {ruta_completa}\n")
  52 |                         txt_file.write("=" * 80 + "\n\n")
  53 | 
  54 |                         try:
  55 |                             with open(ruta_completa, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
  56 |                                 contenido = f.read()
  57 |                             lineas = contenido.split("\n")
  58 |                             lineas_totales += len(lineas)
  59 | 
  60 |                             for i, linea in enumerate(lineas, 1):
  61 |                                 txt_file.write(f"{i:4d} | {linea}\n")
  62 | 
  63 |                             archivos_procesados += 1
  64 |                             print(f"Procesado: {ruta_relativa} ({len(lineas)} lineas)")
  65 | 
  66 |                         except UnicodeDecodeError:
  67 |                             try:
  68 |                                 with open(ruta_completa, "r", encoding="latin-1") as f:
  69 |                                     contenido = f.read()
  70 |                                 txt_file.write("[ARCHIVO LEIDO CON CODIFICACION LATIN-1]\n\n")
  71 |                                 txt_file.write(contenido)
  72 |                                 archivos_procesados += 1
  73 |                                 print(f"Procesado (latin-1): {ruta_relativa}")
  74 |                             except Exception as e:
  75 |                                 error_msg = f"Error al leer archivo: {str(e)}"
  76 |                                 txt_file.write(f"\n[ERROR: {error_msg}]\n")
  77 |                                 print(f"Error al procesar {ruta_relativa}: {error_msg}")
  78 | 
  79 |                         except Exception as e:
  80 |                             error_msg = f"Error al leer archivo: {str(e)}"
  81 |                             txt_file.write(f"\n[ERROR: {error_msg}]\n")
  82 |                             print(f"Error al procesar {ruta_relativa}: {error_msg}")
  83 | 
  84 |                         txt_file.write("\n" + "-" * 80 + "\n")
  85 | 
  86 |         print("\n" + "=" * 80)
  87 |         print("RESUMEN DE PROCESAMIENTO")
  88 |         print("=" * 80)
  89 |         print(f"Ruta principal: {ruta_principal}")
  90 |         print(f"Archivo TXT creado: {nombre_txt}")
  91 |         print(f"Archivos procesados: {archivos_procesados}")
  92 |         print(f"Lineas totales: {lineas_totales}")
  93 | 
  94 |         tamano_txt = os.path.getsize(nombre_txt)
  95 |         print(f"Tamano del TXT: {tamano_txt/1024:.2f} KB ({tamano_txt/1024/1024:.2f} MB)")
  96 | 
  97 |         print("\nArchivo generado exitosamente")
  98 |         print(f"Puedes encontrar el archivo en: {os.path.abspath(nombre_txt)}")
  99 |         print("=" * 80)
 100 | 
 101 |         return True
 102 | 
 103 |     except Exception as e:
 104 |         print(f"Error al crear el archivo: {e}")
 105 |         return False
 106 | 
 107 | 
 108 | def main():
 109 |     ruta_principal = r"C:\alianza_backend"
 110 | 
 111 |     print("INICIANDO ANALISIS DE CODIGO")
 112 |     print("=" * 80)
 113 |     print(f"Escaneando: {ruta_principal}")
 114 |     print("Excluyendo: venv, __pycache__, .git, .idea")
 115 |     print("=" * 80 + "\n")
 116 | 
 117 |     # Solo crear TXT con fecha y hora en el nombre.
 118 |     extraer_py_html_a_txt(ruta_principal)

 121 | if __name__ == "__main__":
 122 |     main()

   1 | """
   2 | importar_historial.py
   3 | ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   4 | Importa pagos históricos desde Excel al sistema Alianza.
   5 | Los pagos se guardan vinculados al propietario del apartamento
   6 | como historial — sin crear ni vincular cargos.
   7 | 
   8 | Compatible con la plantilla: plantilla_historial_pagos.xlsx
   9 | 
  10 | Uso:
  11 |   cd C:\alianza_backend
  12 |   python importar_historial.py
  13 | 
  14 | O especificando el archivo:
  15 |   python importar_historial.py mi_archivo.xlsx
  16 | ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  17 | """
  18 | 
  19 | import sys, os, time, json
  20 | from collections import defaultdict
  21 | 
  22 | try:
  23 |     import openpyxl
  24 | except ImportError:
  25 |     print("Falta openpyxl.  Ejecuta: pip install openpyxl"); sys.exit(1)
  26 | try:
  27 |     import requests
  28 | except ImportError:
  29 |     print("Falta requests.  Ejecuta: pip install requests"); sys.exit(1)
  30 | 
  31 | # ── Configuración ──────────────────────────────────────────
  32 | BASE_URL = "https://alianzaresidencial-production.up.railway.app/api"
  33 | USERNAME  = "Kadin02"
  34 | PASSWORD  = "Panama123*"
  35 | 
  36 | DEFAULT_FILE = "plantilla_historial_pagos.xlsx"
  37 | 
  38 | # Columnas aceptadas en el Excel (nombres alternativos por si el usuario renombra)
  39 | COL_FACTURA    = ["# Factura", "Factura", "N Factura", "factura", "num_factura"]
  40 | COL_FECHA      = ["Fecha", "fecha", "Fecha Pago", "fecha_pago"]
  41 | COL_APTO       = ["Apartamento", "Apto", "apto", "apartamento", "Unidad"]
  42 | COL_RAZON      = ["Razon", "Razón", "razon", "Concepto", "Descripcion"]
  43 | COL_MONTO      = ["Cantidad", "Monto", "monto", "cantidad", "Total", "Importe"]
  44 | COL_COMENTARIO = ["Comentario", "comentario", "Notas", "Nota", "Observacion"]
  45 | COL_PROPIETARIO= ["Propietario", "propietario", "Nombre", "Cliente"]  # opcional
  46 | 
  47 | 
  48 | def find_col(headers, candidates):
  49 |     """Devuelve el índice de la primera columna que coincida, o None."""
  50 |     for i, h in enumerate(headers):
  51 |         if str(h or "").strip() in candidates:
  52 |             return i
  53 |     return None
  54 | 
  55 | 
  56 | def safe_float(val):
  57 |     if val is None: return None
  58 |     try: return round(float(str(val).replace(",", ".")), 2)
  59 |     except: return None
  60 | 
  61 | 
  62 | def safe_str(val):
  63 |     s = str(val or "").strip()
  64 |     return s if s not in ("None", "nan", "") else None
  65 | 
  66 | 
  67 | def safe_date(val):
  68 |     if val is None: return None
  69 |     if hasattr(val, "strftime"): return val.strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
  70 |     s = str(val).strip()
  71 |     # Formatos comunes
  72 |     for fmt in ("%Y-%m-%d", "%d/%m/%Y", "%m/%d/%Y", "%d-%m-%Y"):
  73 |         try:
  74 |             from datetime import datetime
  75 |             return datetime.strptime(s[:10], fmt).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
  76 |         except: pass
  77 |     return s[:10] if len(s) >= 10 else None
  78 | 
  79 | 
  80 | # ── Cliente API ────────────────────────────────────────────
  81 | class API:
  82 |     def __init__(self):
  83 |         self.s = requests.Session()
  84 | 
  85 |     def login(self):
  86 |         try:
  87 |             r = self.s.post(f"{BASE_URL}/auth/login",
  88 |                             json={"username": USERNAME, "password": PASSWORD},
  89 |                             timeout=10)
  90 |             if r.status_code == 200:
  91 |                 self.s.headers.update({"Authorization": f"Bearer {r.json()['access_token']}"})
  92 |                 return True
  93 |             print(f"  ✕ Error de autenticación: {r.status_code}")
  94 |             return False
  95 |         except requests.ConnectionError:
  96 |             print("  ✕ No se puede conectar. ¿Está el servidor corriendo?")
  97 |             return False
  98 | 
  99 |     def get(self, ep):
 100 |         r = self.s.get(f"{BASE_URL}{ep}", timeout=15)
 101 |         return r.json() if r.status_code == 200 else []
 102 | 
 103 |     def post(self, ep, data):
 104 |         r = self.s.post(f"{BASE_URL}{ep}", json=data, timeout=15)
 105 |         if r.status_code in (200, 201): return r.json(), None
 106 |         try:    return None, r.json().get("detail", r.text)
 107 |         except: return None, r.text
 108 | 
 109 | 
 110 | # ── Leer Excel ─────────────────────────────────────────────
 111 | def leer_excel(filepath):
 112 |     wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(filepath)
 113 |     ws = wb.active
 114 |     headers = [cell.value for cell in ws[1]]
 115 | 
 116 |     # Mapear columnas
 117 |     cols = {
 118 |         "factura":     find_col(headers, COL_FACTURA),
 119 |         "fecha":       find_col(headers, COL_FECHA),
 120 |         "apto":        find_col(headers, COL_APTO),
 121 |         "razon":       find_col(headers, COL_RAZON),
 122 |         "monto":       find_col(headers, COL_MONTO),
 123 |         "comentario":  find_col(headers, COL_COMENTARIO),
 124 |         "propietario": find_col(headers, COL_PROPIETARIO),
 125 |     }
 126 | 
 127 |     faltantes = [k for k in ["fecha", "apto", "monto"] if cols[k] is None]
 128 |     if faltantes:
 129 |         print(f"\n  ✕ Columnas obligatorias no encontradas: {faltantes}")
 130 |         print(f"  Columnas del archivo: {headers}")
 131 |         sys.exit(1)
 132 | 
 133 |     print(f"  Columnas detectadas:")
 134 |     for k, v in cols.items():
 135 |         if v is not None:
 136 |             print(f"    {k:15} → columna {v+1} ({headers[v]})")
 137 | 
 138 |     registros = []
 139 |     for row in ws.iter_rows(min_row=2, values_only=True):
 140 |         def get(key):
 141 |             i = cols.get(key)
 142 |             return row[i] if i is not None and i < len(row) else None
 143 | 
 144 |         fecha = safe_date(get("fecha"))
 145 |         apto  = safe_str(get("apto"))
 146 |         monto = safe_float(get("monto"))
 147 | 
 148 |         if not fecha or not apto or not monto or monto <= 0:
 149 |             continue
 150 | 
 151 |         registros.append({
 152 |             "factura":     safe_str(get("factura")),
 153 |             "fecha":       fecha,
 154 |             "apto":        apto,
 155 |             "razon":       safe_str(get("razon")) or "Historial",
 156 |             "monto":       monto,
 157 |             "comentario":  safe_str(get("comentario")),
 158 |             "propietario": safe_str(get("propietario")),
 159 |         })
 160 | 
 161 |     return registros
 162 | 
 163 | 
 164 | # ── Validar y mostrar plan ─────────────────────────────────
 165 | def analizar(registros, unit_by_num, owner_by_unit):
 166 |     stats = {"ok": 0, "sin_unit": 0, "sin_owner": 0}
 167 |     aptos_faltantes = set()
 168 |     aptos_sin_owner = set()
 169 | 
 170 |     for r in registros:
 171 |         unit = unit_by_num.get(r["apto"])
 172 |         if not unit:
 173 |             stats["sin_unit"] += 1
 174 |             aptos_faltantes.add(r["apto"])
 175 |         elif not owner_by_unit.get(r["apto"]):
 176 |             stats["sin_owner"] += 1
 177 |             aptos_sin_owner.add(r["apto"])
 178 |         else:
 179 |             stats["ok"] += 1
 180 | 
 181 |     return stats, sorted(aptos_faltantes), sorted(aptos_sin_owner)
 182 |

 184 | # ── Main ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
 185 | def main():
 186 |     print()
 187 |     print("═" * 62)
 188 |     print("  Importador de Historial de Pagos — Alianza Residencial")
 189 |     print("═" * 62)
 190 | 
 191 |     # Archivo a importar
 192 |     filepath = sys.argv[1] if len(sys.argv) > 1 else DEFAULT_FILE
 193 |     if not os.path.exists(filepath):
 194 |         print(f"\n  ✕ Archivo no encontrado: {filepath}")
 195 |         print(f"  Uso: python importar_historial.py [archivo.xlsx]")
 196 |         sys.exit(1)
 197 | 
 198 |     print(f"\n  Archivo: {filepath}")
 199 |     print()
 200 | 
 201 |     # Leer Excel
 202 |     print("  Leyendo registros...")
 203 |     registros = leer_excel(filepath)
 204 |     print(f"  Registros válidos: {len(registros)}")
 205 | 
 206 |     if not registros:
 207 |         print("  No hay registros para importar.")
 208 |         sys.exit(0)
 209 | 
 210 |     # Estadísticas del archivo
 211 |     from collections import Counter
 212 |     años    = Counter(r["fecha"][:4] for r in registros)
 213 |     razones = Counter(r["razon"] for r in registros)
 214 |     aptos   = set(r["apto"] for r in registros)
 215 | 
 216 |     print(f"\n  Distribución por año:  {dict(sorted(años.items()))}")
 217 |     print(f"  Apartamentos únicos:   {len(aptos)}")
 218 |     print(f"  Razones/Conceptos:")
 219 |     for razon, cnt in razones.most_common():
 220 |         print(f"    {cnt:4d}x  {razon}")
 221 | 
 222 |     # Conectar
 223 |     print("\n  Conectando al servidor...")
 224 |     api = API()
 225 |     if not api.login():
 226 |         sys.exit(1)
 227 |     print("  ✓ Conectado")
 228 | 
 229 |     # Cargar catálogos
 230 |     units       = api.get("/units")
 231 |     unit_owners = api.get("/unit-owners/all")
 232 | 
 233 |     unit_by_num  = {u["unit_number"].strip(): u for u in units}
 234 |     owner_by_unit= {}
 235 |     for uo in unit_owners:
 236 |         if not uo.get("is_active"): continue
 237 |         for num, u in unit_by_num.items():
 238 |             if u["id"] == uo["unit_id"]:
 239 |                 owner_by_unit[num] = uo["owner_id"]
 240 |                 break
 241 | 
 242 |     print(f"  Unidades en sistema:   {len(units)}")
 243 | 
 244 |     # Analizar
 245 |     stats, faltantes, sin_owner = analizar(registros, unit_by_num, owner_by_unit)
 246 | 
 247 |     print()
 248 |     print("  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐")
 249 |     print("  │  PLAN DE IMPORTACIÓN                        │")
 250 |     print("  ├─────────────────────────────────────────────┤")
 251 |     print(f"  │  Registros que se importarán:  {stats['ok']:>6}       │")
 252 |     print(f"  │  Apto no existe en sistema:    {stats['sin_unit']:>6}       │")
 253 |     print(f"  │  Apto sin propietario activo:  {stats['sin_owner']:>6}       │")
 254 |     print("  └─────────────────────────────────────────────┘")
 255 | 
 256 |     if faltantes:
 257 |         print(f"\n  ⚠  Aptos no registrados (se omitirán):")
 258 |         for a in faltantes[:15]:
 259 |             print(f"     · {a}")
 260 |         if len(faltantes) > 15:
 261 |             print(f"     ... y {len(faltantes)-15} más")
 262 | 
 263 |     if sin_owner:
 264 |         print(f"\n  ⚠  Aptos sin propietario activo (se omitirán):")
 265 |         for a in sin_owner[:10]:
 266 |             print(f"     · {a}")
 267 | 
 268 |     if stats["ok"] == 0:
 269 |         print("\n  No hay registros que se puedan importar.")
 270 |         sys.exit(0)
 271 | 
 272 |     print()
 273 |     resp = input(f"  ¿Importar {stats['ok']} registros? (s/n): ").strip().lower()
 274 |     if resp != "s":
 275 |         print("  Cancelado.")
 276 |         sys.exit(0)
 277 | 
 278 |     # ── Importar ───────────────────────────────────────────
 279 |     ok = 0; err = 0; omitidos = 0
 280 |     errores = []
 281 |     total = len(registros)
 282 |     t0 = time.time()
 283 | 
 284 |     print()
 285 |     for i, r in enumerate(registros, 1):
 286 |         if i % 50 == 0:
 287 |             print(f"  Progreso: {i}/{total} ({i*100//total}%)", end="\r")
 288 | 
 289 |         unit     = unit_by_num.get(r["apto"])
 290 |         owner_id = owner_by_unit.get(r["apto"])
 291 | 
 292 |         if not unit or not owner_id:
 293 |             omitidos += 1
 294 |             continue
 295 | 
 296 |         # Construir referencia combinando razón + comentario
 297 |         referencia = r["razon"]
 298 |         if r["comentario"]:
 299 |             referencia = f"{r['razon']} — {r['comentario']}"
 300 | 
 301 |         resultado, error = api.post("/finance/payment-complete", {
 302 |             "owner_id":       owner_id,
 303 |             "payment_date":   r["fecha"],
 304 |             "amount":         r["monto"],
 305 |             "invoice_number": r["factura"],
 306 |             "reference":      referencia,
 307 |             "applications":   [],   # historial puro — sin vincular a cargo
 308 |         })
 309 | 
 310 |         if resultado:
 311 |             ok += 1
 312 |         else:
 313 |             errores.append(f"Fac {r['factura']} | {r['apto']} | {r['fecha']} | ${r['monto']}: {error}")
 314 |             err += 1
 315 | 
 316 |     elapsed = time.time() - t0
 317 |     print()
 318 |     print()
 319 |     print("═" * 62)
 320 |     print("  RESULTADO")
 321 |     print("─" * 62)
 322 |     print(f"  ✓ Importados correctamente: {ok}")
 323 |     print(f"  ─ Omitidos (sin unidad):    {omitidos}")
 324 |     print(f"  ✕ Errores:                  {err}")
 325 |     print(f"  Tiempo: {elapsed:.1f}s")
 326 |     print("═" * 62)
 327 | 
 328 |     if errores:
 329 |         log_file = "historial_errores.txt"
 330 |         with open(log_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
 331 |             from datetime import datetime
 332 |             f.write(f"Errores de importación — {datetime.now()}\n\n")
 333 |             for e in errores: f.write(f"· {e}\n")
 334 |         print(f"\n  Log guardado en: {log_file}")
 335 |         print("  Primeros errores:")
 336 |         for e in errores[:8]: print(f"    · {e}")
 337 | 
 338 |     print()
 339 |     print("  Los pagos ya están disponibles en:")
 340 |     print("  · Finanzas → Historial de Cargos (por propietario)")
 341 |     print("  · Reportes → Por Propietario")
 342 |     print("  · Estado de Cuenta de cada propietario")
 343 | 
 344 | 
 345 | if __name__ == "__main__":
 346 |     main()
